RV agnimīḷe purohitaṃ yajñasya devam ṛtvijam
RV hotāraṃ ratnadhātamam
RV agniḥ pūrvebhirṛṣibhirīḍyo nūtanairuta
RV sa devāneha vakṣati
RV agninā rayimaśnavat poṣameva divedive
RV yaśasaṃ vīravattamam
RV agne yaṃ yajñamadhvaraṃ viśvataḥ paribhūrasi
RV sa iddeveṣu gachati
RV agnirhotā kavikratuḥ satyaścitraśravastamaḥ
RV devo devebhirā gamat
RV yadaṅga dāśuṣe tvamagne bhadraṃ kariṣyasi
RV tavet tat satyamaṅgiraḥ
RV upa tvāgne divedive doṣāvastardhiyā vayam
RV namo bharanta emasi
RV rājantamadhvarāṇāṃ gopām ṛtasya dīdivim
RV vardhamānaṃ sve dame
RV sa naḥ piteva sūnave 'gne sūpāyano bhava
RV sacasvā naḥ svastaye
RV vāyavā yāhi darśateme somā araṃkṛtāḥ
RV teṣāṃ pāhi śrudhī havam
RV vāya ukthebhirjarante tvāmachā jaritāraḥ
RV sutasomā aharvidaḥ
RV vāyo tava prapṛñcatī dhenā jigāti dāśuṣe
RV urūcī somapītaye
RV indravāyū ime sutā upa prayobhirā gatam
RV indavo vāmuśanti hi
RV vāyavindraśca cetathaḥ sutānāṃ vājinīvasū
RV tāvā yātamupa dravat
RV vāyavindraśca sunvata ā yātamupa niṣkṛtam
RV makṣvitthā dhiyā narā
RV mitraṃ huve pūtadakṣaṃ varuṇaṃ ca riśādasam
RV dhiyaṃ ghṛtācīṃ sādhantā
RV ṛtena mitrāvaruṇāv ṛtāvṛdhāv ṛtaspṛśā
RV kratuṃ bṛhantamāśāthe
RV kavī no mitrāvaruṇā tuvijātā urukṣayā
RV dakṣaṃ dadhāte apasam
RV aśvinā yajvarīriṣo dravatpāṇī śubhas patī
RV purubhujācanasyatam
RV aśvinā purudaṃsasā narā śavīrayā dhiyā
RV dhiṣṇyā vanataṃ giraḥ
RV dasrā yuvākavaḥ sutā nāsatyā vṛktabarhiṣaḥ
RV ā yātaṃrudravartanī
RV indrā yāhi citrabhāno sutā ime tvāyavaḥ
RV aṇvībhistanā pūtāsaḥ
RV indrā yāhi dhiyeṣito viprajūtaḥ sutāvataḥ
RV upa brahmāṇi vāghataḥ
RV indrā yāhi tūtujāna upa brahmāṇi harivaḥ
RV sute dadhiṣvanaścanaḥ
RV omāsaścarṣaṇīdhṛto viśve devāsa ā gata
RV dāśvāṃso dāśuṣaḥ sutam
RV viśve devāso apturaḥ sutamā ganta tūrṇayaḥ
RV usrā ivasvasarāṇi
RV viśve devāso asridha ehimāyāso adruhaḥ
RV medhaṃ juṣanta vahnayaḥ
RV pāvakā naḥ sarasvatī vājebhirvājinīvatī
RV yajñaṃ vaṣṭu dhiyāvasuḥ
RV codayitrī sūnṛtānāṃ cetantī sumatīnām
RV yajñaṃ dadhe sarasvatī
RV maho arṇaḥ sarasvatī pra cetayati ketunā
RV dhiyo viśvā vi rājati
RV surūpakṛtnumūtaye sudughāmiva goduhe
RV juhūmasi dyavidyavi
RV upa naḥ savanā gahi somasya somapāḥ piba
RV godā id revatomadaḥ
RV athā te antamānāṃ vidyāma sumatīnām
RV mā no ati khya āgahi
RV parehi vigramastṛtamindraṃ pṛchā vipaścitam
RV yaste sakhibhya ā varam
RV uta bruvantu no nido niranyataścidārata
RV dadhānā indra id duvaḥ
RV uta naḥ subhagānarirvoceyurdasma kṛṣṭayaḥ
RV syāmedindrasya śarmaṇi
RV emāśumāśave bhara yajñaśriyaṃ nṛmādanam
RV patayan mandayatsakham
RV asya pītvā śatakrato ghano vṛtrāṇāmabhavaḥ
RV prāvo vājeṣu vājinam
RV taṃ tvā vājeṣu vājinaṃ vājayāmaḥ śatakrato
RV dhanānāmindra sātaye
RV yo rāyo 'vanirmahān supāraḥ sunvataḥ sakhā
RV tasmā indrāya gāyata
RV ā tvetā ni ṣīdatendramabhi pra gāyata
RV sakhāya stomavāhasaḥ
RV purūtamaṃ purūṇāmīśānaṃ vāryāṇām
RV indraṃ some sacā sute
RV sa ghā no yoga ā bhuvat sa rāye sa purandhyām
RV gamad vājebhirā sa naḥ
RV yasya saṃsthe na vṛṇvate harī samatsu śatravaḥ
RV tasmā indrāya gāyata
RV sutapāvne sutā ime śucayo yanti vītaye
RV somāso dadhyāśiraḥ
RV tvaṃ sutasya pītaye sadyo vṛddho ajāyathāḥ
RV indra jyaiṣṭhyāya sukrato
RV ā tvā viśantvāśavaḥ somāsa indra girvaṇaḥ
RV śaṃ te santu pracetase
RV tvāṃ stomā avīvṛdhan tvāmukthā śatakrato
RV tvāṃ vardhantu no giraḥ
RV akṣitotiḥ sanedimaṃ vājamindraḥ sahasriṇam
RV yasmin viśvāni pauṃsyā
RV mā no martā abhi druhan tanūnāmindra girvaṇaḥ
RV īśāno yavayā vadham
RV yuñjanti bradhnamaruṣaṃ carantaṃ pari tasthuṣaḥ
RV rocanterocanā divi
RV yuñjantyasya kāmyā harī vipakṣasā rathe
RV śoṇā dhṛṣṇū nṛvāhasā
RV ketuṃ kṛṇvannaketave peśo maryā apeśase
RV samuṣadbhirajāyathāḥ
RV ādaha svadhāmanu punargarbhatvamerire
RV dadhānā nāmayajñiyam
RV vīḷu cidārujatnubhirguhā cidindra vahnibhiḥ
RV avinda usriyā anu
RV devayanto yathā matimachā vidadvasuṃ giraḥ
RV mahāmanūṣata śrutam
RV indreṇa saṃ hi dṛkṣase saṃjagmāno abibhyuṣā
RV mandū samānavarcasā
RV anavadyairabhidyubhirmakhaḥ sahasvadarcati
RV gaṇairindrasya kāmyaiḥ
RV ataḥ parijmannā gahi divo vā rocanādadhi
RV samasminnṛñjate giraḥ
RV ito vā sātimīmahe divo vā pārthivādadhi
RV indraṃ mahovā rajasaḥ
RV indramid gāthino bṛhadindramarkebhirarkiṇaḥ
RV indraṃ vāṇīranūṣata
RV indra id dharyoḥ sacā sammiśla ā vacoyujā
RV indro vajrīhiraṇyayaḥ
RV indro dīrghāya cakṣasa ā sūryaṃ rohayad divi
RV vi gobhiradrimairayat
RV indra vājeṣu no 'va sahasrapradhaneṣu ca
RV ugra ugrābhirūtibhiḥ
RV indraṃ vayaṃ mahādhana indramarbhe havāmahe
RV yujaṃ vṛtreṣu vajriṇam
RV sa no vṛṣannamuṃ caruṃ satrādāvannapā vṛdhi
RV asmabhyamapratiṣkutaḥ
RV tuñjetuñje ya uttare stomā indrasya vajriṇaḥ
RV na vindheasya suṣṭutim
RV vṛṣā yūtheva vaṃsagaḥ kṛṣṭīriyartyojasā
RV īśāno apratiṣkutaḥ
RV ya ekaścarṣaṇīnāṃ vasūnāmirajyati
RV indraḥ pañca ksitīnām
RV indraṃ vo viśvatas pari havāmahe janebhyaḥ
RV asmākamastu kevalaḥ
RV endra sānasiṃ rayiṃ sajitvānaṃ sadāsaham
RV varṣiṣṭhamūtaye bhara
RV ni yena muṣṭihatyayā ni vṛtrā ruṇadhāmahai
RV tvotāso nyarvatā
RV indra tvotāsa ā vayaṃ vajraṃ ghanā dadīmahi
RV jayema saṃ yudhi spṛdhaḥ
RV vayaṃ śūrebhirastṛbhirindra tvayā yujā vayam
RV sāsahyāma pṛtanyataḥ
RV mahānindraḥ paraśca nu mahitvamastu vajriṇe
RV dyaurnaprathinā śavaḥ
RV samohe vā ya āśata narastokasya sanitau
RV viprāso vā dhiyāyavaḥ
RV yaḥ kukṣiḥ somapātamaḥ samudra iva pinvate
RV urvīrāpo na kākudaḥ
RV evā hyasya sūnṛtā virapśī gomatī mahī
RV pakvā śākhā na dāśuṣe
RV evā hi te vibhūtaya ūtaya indra māvate
RV sadyaścit santidāśuṣe
RV evā hyasya kāmyā stoma ukthaṃ ca śaṃsyā
RV indrāya somapītaye
RV indrehi matsyandhaso viśvebhiḥ somaparvabhiḥ
RV mahānabhiṣṭirojasā
RV emenaṃ sṛjatā sute mandimindrāya mandine
RV cakriṃ viśvāni cakraye
RV matsvā suśipra mandibhiḥ stomebhirviśvacarṣaṇe
RV sacaiṣusavaneṣvā
RV asṛgramindra te giraḥ prati tvāmudahāsata
RV ajoṣā vṛṣabhaṃ patim
RV saṃ codaya citramarvāg rādha indra vareṇyam
RV asadit te vibhu prabhu
RV asmān su tatra codayendra rāye rabhasvataḥ
RV tuvidyumna yaśasvataḥ
RV saṃ gomadindra vājavadasme pṛthu śravo bṛhat
RV viśvāyurdhehyakṣitam
RV asme dhehi śravo bṛhad dyumnaṃ sahasrasātamam
RV indra tā rathinīriṣaḥ
RV vasorindraṃ vasupatiṃ gīrbhirgṛṇanta ṛgmiyam
RV homa gantāramūtaye
RV sutesute nyokase bṛhad bṛhata edariḥ
RV indrāya śūṣamarcati
RV gāyanti tvā gāyatriṇo 'rcantyarkamarkiṇaḥ
RV brahmāṇastvā śatakrata ud vaṃśamiva yemire
RV yat sānoḥ sānumāruhad bhūryaspaṣṭa kartvam
RV tadindro arthaṃ cetati yūthena vṛṣṇirejati
RV yukṣvā hi keśinā harī vṛṣaṇā kakṣyaprā
RV athā na indra somapā girāmupaśrutiṃ cara
RV ehi stomānabhi svarābhi gṛṇīhyā ruva
RV brahma ca no vasosacendra yajñaṃ ca vardhaya
RV ukthamindrāya śaṃsyaṃ vardhanaṃ puruniṣṣidhe
RV śakro yathā suteṣu ṇo rāraṇat sakhyeṣu ca
RV tamit sakhitva īmahe taṃ rāye taṃ suvīrye
RV sa śakra uta naḥ śakadindro vasu dayamānaḥ
RV suvivṛtaṃ sunirajamindra tvādātamid yaśaḥ
RV gavāmapavrajaṃ vṛdhi kṛṇuṣva rādho adrivaḥ
RV nahi tvā rodasī ubhe ṛghāyamāṇaminvataḥ
RV jeṣaḥ svarvatīrapaḥ saṃ gā asmabhyaṃ dhūnuhi
RV āśrutkarṇa śrudhī havaṃ nū cid dadhiṣva me giraḥ
RV indra stomamimaṃ mama kṛṣvā yujaścidantaram
RV vidmā hi tvā vṛṣantamaṃ vājeṣu havanaśrutam
RV vṛṣantamasya hūmaha ūtiṃ sahasrasātamām
RV ā tū na indra kauśika mandasānaḥ sutaṃ piba
RV navyamāyuḥpra sū tira kṛdhī sahasrasām ṛṣim
RV pari tvā girvaṇo gira imā bhavantu viśvataḥ
RV vṛddhāyumanu vṛddhayo juṣṭā bhavantu juṣṭayaḥ
RV indraṃ viśvā avīvṛdhan samudravyacasaṃ giraḥ
RV rathītamaṃrathīnāṃ vājānāṃ satpatiṃ patim

RV pūrvīrindrasya rātayo na vi dasyantyūtayaḥ
RV yadī vājasya gomata stotṛbhyo maṃhate magham

RV indro viśvasyakarmaṇo dhartā vajrī puruṣṭutaḥ
RV tvaṃ valasya gomato 'pāvaradrivo bilam

RV tavāhaṃ śūra rātibhiḥ pratyāyaṃ sindhumāvadan
RV upātiṣṭhanta girvaṇo viduṣ ṭe tasya kāravaḥ
RV māyābhirindra māyinaṃ tvaṃ śuṣṇamavātiraḥ
RV viduṣ ṭe tasya medhirāsteṣāṃ śravāṃsyut tira
RV indramīśānamojasābhi stomā anūṣata
RV sahasraṃ yasya rātaya uta vā santi bhūyasīḥ
RV agniṃ dūtaṃ vṛṇīmahe hotāraṃ viśvavedasam
RV asya yajñasya sukratum
RV agnimagniṃ havīmabhiḥ sadā havanta viśpatim
RV havyavāhaṃ purupriyam
RV agne devānihā vaha jajñāno vṛktabarhiṣe
RV asi hotā na īḍyaḥ
RV tānuśato vi bodhaya yadagne yāsi dūtyam
RV devairā satsi barhiṣi
RV ghṛtāhavana dīdivaḥ prati ṣma riṣato daha
RV agne tvaṃ rakṣasvinaḥ
RV agnināgniḥ samidhyate kavirgṛhapatiryuvā
RV havyavāḍ juhvāsyaḥ
RV kavimagnimupa stuhi satyadharmāṇamadhvare
RV devamamīvacātanam
RV yastvāmagne haviṣpatirdūtaṃ deva saparyati
RV tasya sma prāvitā bhava
RV yo agniṃ devavītaye haviṣmānāvivāsati
RV tasmai pāvaka mṛḷaya
RV sa naḥ pāvaka dīdivo 'gne devānihā vaha

RV sa na stavāna ā bhara gāyatreṇa navīyasā
RV rayiṃ vīravatīmiṣam
RV agne śukreṇa śociṣā viśvābhirdevahūtibhiḥ
RV imaṃ stomaṃ juṣasva naḥ
RV susamiddho na ā vaha devānagne haviṣmate
RV hotaḥ pāvaka yakṣi ca
RV madhumantaṃ tanūnapād yajñaṃ deveṣu naḥ kave
RV adyā kṛṇuhi vītaye
RV narāśaṃsamiha priyamasmin yajña upa hvaye
RV madhujihvaṃhaviṣkṛtam
RV agne sukhatame rathe devānīḷita ā vaha
RV asi hotā manurhitaḥ
RV stṛṇīta barhirānuṣag ghṛtapṛṣṭhaṃ manīṣiṇaḥ
RV yatrāmṛtasya cakṣaṇam
RV vi śrayantām ṛtāvṛdho dvāro devīrasaścataḥ
RV adyā nūnaṃ ca yaṣṭave
RV naktoṣāsā supeśasāsmin yajña upa hvaye
RV idaṃ no barhirāsade
RV tā sujihvā upa hvaye hotārā daivyā kavī
RV yajñaṃ no yakṣatāmimam
RV iḷā sarasvatī mahī tisro devīrmayobhuvaḥ
RV barhiḥ sīdantvasridhaḥ
RV iha tvaṣṭāramagriyaṃ viśvarūpamupa hvaye

RV ava sṛjā vanaspate deva devebhyo haviḥ
RV pra dāturastu cetanam

RV tatra devānupa hvaye
RV aibhiragne duvo giro viśvebhiḥ somapītaye

RV matsarāsastadokasaḥ

RV yūyaṃ hi ṣṭhā sudānavaḥ

RV tvaṃhi ratnadhā asi

RV brāhmaṇādindra rādhasaḥ pibā somam ṛtūnranu
RV taved dhi sakhyamastṛtam

RV draviṇodā draviṇaso grāvahastāso adhvare

RV deveṣu tā vanāmahe
RV draviṇodāḥ pipīṣati juhota pra ca tiṣṭhata

RV aśvinā pibataṃ madhu dīdyagnī śucivrata

RV pra vāmaśnotu suṣṭutirindrāvaruṇa yāṃ huve

RV yo revān yo amīvahā vasuvit puṣṭivardhanaḥ

RV dakṣiṇā pātvaṃhasaḥ
RV sadasas patimadbhutaṃ priyamindrasya kāmyam

RV tvamagna uruśaṃsāya vāghate spārhaṃ yad rekṇaḥ paramaṃ vanoṣi tat
RV ādhrasya cit pramatirucyase pitā pra pākaṃśāssi pra diśo viduṣṭaraḥ
RV tvamagne prayatadakṣiṇaṃ naraṃ varmeva syūtaṃ pari pāsi viśvataḥ
RV svādukṣadmā yo vasatau syonakṛjjīvayājaṃ yajate sopamā divaḥ
RV imāmagne śaraṇiṃ mīmṛṣo na imamadhvānaṃ yamagāma dūrāt
RV āpiḥ pitā pramatiḥ somyānāṃ bhṛmirasy ṛṣikṛn martyānām
RV manuṣvadagne aṅgirasvadaṅgiro yayātivat sadane pūrvavacchuce
RV acha yāhyā vahā daivyaṃ janamā sādaya barhiṣi yakṣi ca priyam
RV etenāgne brahmaṇā vāvṛdhasva śaktī vā yat te cakṛmā vidā vā
RV uta pra ṇeṣyabhi vasyo asmān saṃ naḥ sṛja sumatyā vājavatyā
RV indrasya nu vīryāṇi pra vocaṃ yāni cakāra prathamāni vajrī
RV ahannahimanvapastatarda pra vakṣaṇā abhinat parvatānām
RV ahannahiṃ parvate śiśriyāṇaṃ tvaṣṭāsmai vajraṃ svaryaṃ tatakṣa
RV vāśrā iva dhenavaḥ syandamānā añjaḥ samudramava jagmurāpaḥ
RV vṛṣāyamāṇo 'vṛṇīta somaṃ trikadrukeṣvapibat sutasya
RV āsāyakaṃ maghavādatta vajramahannenaṃ prathamajāmahīnām
RV yadindrāhan prathamajāmahīnāmān māyināmamināḥ prota māyāḥ
RV āt sūryaṃ janayan dyāmuṣāsaṃ tādītnāśatruṃ na kilā vivitse
RV ahan vṛtraṃ vṛtrataraṃ vyaṃsamindro vajreṇa mahatā vadhena
RV skandhāṃsīva kuliśenā vivṛkṇāhiḥ śayata upapṛk pṛthivyāḥ
RV ayoddheva durmada ā hi juhve mahāvīraṃ tuvibādham ṛjīṣam
RV nātārīdasya samṛtiṃ vadhānāṃ saṃ rujānāḥ pipiṣaindraśatruḥ
RV apādahasto apṛtanyadindramāsya vajramadhi sānau jaghāna
RV vṛṣṇo vadhriḥ pratimānaṃ bubhūṣan purutrā vṛtro aśayad vyastaḥ
RV nadaṃ na bhinnamamuyā śayānaṃ mano ruhāṇā ati yantyāpaḥ
RV yāścid vṛtro mahinā paryatiṣṭhat tāsāmahiḥ patsutaḥśīrbabhūva
RV nīcāvayā abhavad vṛtraputrendro asyā ava vadharjabhāra
RV uttarā sūradharaḥ putra āsīd dānuḥ śaye sahavatsā na dhenuḥ
RV atiṣṭhantīnāmaniveśanānāṃ kāṣṭhānāṃ madhye nihitaṃśarīram
RV vṛtrasya niṇyaṃ vi carantyāpo dīrghaṃ tama āśayadindraśatruḥ
RV dāsapatnīrahigopā atiṣṭhan niruddhā āpaḥ paṇineva gāvaḥ
RV apāṃ bilamapihitaṃ yadāsīd vṛtraṃ jaghanvānapatad vavāra
RV aśvyo vāro abhavastadindra sṛke yat tvā pratyahan deva ekaḥ
RV ajayo gā ajayaḥ śūra somamavāsṛjaḥ sartave sapta sindhūn
RV nāsmai vidyun na tanyatuḥ siṣedha na yāṃ mihamakirad dhrāduniṃ ca
RV indraśca yad yuyudhāte ahiścotāparībhyo maghavā vi jigye
RV aheryātāraṃ kamapaśya indra hṛdi yat te jaghnuṣo bhīragachat
RV nava ca yan navatiṃ ca sravantīḥ śyeno na bhītoataro rajāṃsi
RV indro yāto 'vasitasya rājā śamasya ca śṛṅgiṇo vajrabāhuḥ
RV sedu rājā kṣayati carṣaṇīnāmarān na nemiḥ pari tā babhūva
RV etāyāmopa gavyanta indramasmākaṃ su pramatiṃ vāvṛdhāti
RV anāmṛṇaḥ kuvidādasya rāyo gavāṃ ketaṃ paramāvarjate naḥ
RV upedahaṃ dhanadāmapratītaṃ juṣṭaṃ na śyeno vasatimpatāmi
RV indraṃ namasyannupamebhirarkairyaḥ stotṛbhyo havyo asti yāman
RV ni sarvasena iṣudhīnrasakta samaryo gā ajati yasya vaṣṭi
RV coṣkūyamāṇa indra bhūri vāmaṃ mā paṇirbhūrasmadadhi pravṛddha
RV vadhīrhi dasyuṃ dhaninaṃ ghanenanekaścarannupaśākebhirindra
RV dhanoradhi viṣuṇak te vyāyannayajvanaḥ sanakāḥ pretimīyuḥ
RV parā cicchīrṣā vavṛjusta indrāyajvāno yajvabhiḥ spardhamānāḥ
RV pra yad divo hariva sthātarugra niravratānadhamorodasyoḥ
RV ayuyutsannanavadyasya senāmayātayanta kṣitayo navagvāḥ
RV vṛṣāyudho na vadhrayo niraṣṭāḥ pravadbhirindrāccitayanta āyan
RV tvametān rudato jakṣataścāyodhayo rajasa indra pāre
RV avādaho diva ā dasyumuccā pra sunvataḥ stuvataḥ śaṃsamāvaḥ
RV cakrāṇāsaḥ parīṇahaṃ pṛthivyā hiraṇyena maṇinā śumbhamānāḥ
RV na hinvānāsastitirusta indraṃ pari spaśo adadhāt sūryeṇa
RV pari yadindra rodasī ubhe abubhojīrmahinā viśvataḥ sīm
RV amanyamānānabhi manyamānairnirbrahmabhiradhamo dasyumindra
RV na ye divaḥ pṛthivyā antamāpurna māyābhirdhanadāṃ paryabhūvan
RV yujaṃ vajraṃ vṛṣabhaścakra indro nirjyotiṣā tamaso gā adukṣat
RV anu svadhāmakṣarannāpo asyāvardhata madhya ā nāvyānām
RV sadhrīcīnena manasā tamindra ojiṣṭhena hanmanāhannabhi dyūn
RV nyāvidhyadilībiśasya dṛlhā vi śṛṅgiṇamabhinacchuṣṇamindraḥ
RV yāvat taro maghavan yāvadojo vajreṇa śatrumavadhīḥ pṛtanyum
RV abhi sidhmo ajigādasya śatrūn vi tigmena vṛṣabheṇa puro 'bhet
RV saṃ vajreṇāsṛjad vṛtramindraḥ pra svāṃ matimatiracchāśadānaḥ
RVxx āvaḥ kutsam indra yasmi cākan prāvo yudhyantaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ daśadyum 
RVxx śaphacyuto reṇur nakṣata dyām uc chvaitreyo nṛṣāhyāya tasthau 
RVxx āvaḥ śamaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ tugryāsu kṣetrajeṣe maghavañchvitryaṃ gām 
RVxx jyok cid atra tasthivāṃso akrañchatrūyatām adharā vedanākaḥ 
RVxx triś cin no adyā bhavataṃ navedasā vibhur vāṃ yāma uta rātir aśvinā 
RVxx yuvor hi yantraṃ himyeva vāsaso 'bhyāyaṃsenyā bhavatam manīṣibhiḥ 
RVxx trayaḥ pavayo madhuvāhane rathe somasya venām anu viśva id viduḥ 
RVxx traya skambhāsa skabhitāsa ārabhe trir naktaṃ yāthas trir v aśvinā divā 
RVxx samāne ahan trir avadyagohanā trir adya yajñam madhunā mimikṣatam 
RVxx trir vājavatīr iṣo aśvinā yuvaṃ doṣā asmabhyam uṣasaś ca pinvatam 
RVxx trir vartir yātaṃ trir anuvrate jane triḥ suprāvyetredheva śikṣatam 
RVxx trir nāndyaṃ vahatam aśvinā yuvaṃ triḥ pṛkṣo asme akṣareva pinvatam 
RVxx trir no rayiṃ vahatam aśvinā yuvaṃ trir devatātā trir utāvataṃ dhiyaḥ 
RVxx triḥ saubhagatvaṃ trir uta śravāṃsi nas triṣṭhaṃ vāṃ sūre duhitā ruhad ratham 
RVxx trir no aśvinā divyāni bheṣajā triḥ pārthivāni trir u dattam adbhyaḥ 
RVxx omānaṃ śaṃyor mamakāya sūnave tridhātu śarma vahataṃ śubhas patī 
RVxx trir no aśvinā yajatā divedive pari tridhātu pṛthivīm aśāyatam 
RVxx tisro nāsatyā rathyā parāvata ātmeva vātaḥ svasarāṇi gachatam 
RVxx trir aśvinā sindhubhiḥ saptamātṛbhis traya āhāvās tredhā haviṣ kṛtam 
RVxx tisraḥ pṛthivīr upari pravā divo nākaṃ rakṣethe dyubhir aktubhir hitam 
RVxx kva trī cakrā trivṛto rathasya kva trayo vandhuro ye sanīḷāḥ 
RVxx kadā yogo vājino rāsabhasya yena yajñaṃ nāsatyopayāthaḥ 
RVxx ā nāsatyā gachataṃ hūyate havir madhvaḥ pibatam madhupebhir āsabhiḥ 
RVxx yuvor hi pūrvaṃ savitoṣaso ratham ṛtāya citraṃ ghṛtavantam iṣyati 
RVxx ā nāsatyā tribhir ekādaśair iha devebhir yātam madhupeyam aśvinā 
RVxx prāyus tāriṣṭaṃ nī rapāṃsi mṛkṣataṃ sedhataṃ dveṣo bhavataṃ sacābhuvā 
RVxx ā no aśvinā trivṛtā rathenārvāñcaṃ rayiṃ vahataṃ suvīram 
RVxx śṛṇvantā vām avase johavīmi vṛdhe ca no bhavataṃ vājasātau 
RVxx hvayāmy agnim prathamaṃ svastaye hvayāmi mitrāvaruṇāv ihāvase 
RVxx hvayāmi rātrīṃ jagato niveśanīṃ hvayāmi devaṃ savitāram ūtaye 
RVxx ā kṛṣṇena rajasā vartamāno niveśayann amṛtam martyaṃ ca 
RVxx hiraṇyayena savitā rathenā devo yāti bhuvanāni paśyan 
RVxx yāti devaḥ pravatā yāty udvatā yāti śubhrābhyāṃ yajato haribhyām 
RVxx ā devo yāti savitā parāvato 'pa viśvā duritā bādhamānaḥ 
RVxx abhīvṛtaṃ kṛśanair viśvarūpaṃ hiraṇyaśamyaṃ yajato bṛhantam 
RVxx āsthād rathaṃ savitā citrabhānuḥ kṛṣṇā rajāṃsi taviṣīṃ dadhānaḥ 
RVxx vi janāñchyāvāḥ śitipādo akhyan rathaṃ hiraṇyapraraugaṃ vahantaḥ 
RVxx śaśvad viśaḥ savitur daivyasyopasthe viśvā bhuvanāni tasthuḥ 
RVxx tisro dyāvaḥ savitur dvā upasthāṃ ekā yamasya bhuvane virāṣāṭ 
RVxx āṇiṃ na rathyam amṛtādhi tasthur iha bravītu ya u tac ciketat 
RVxx vi suparṇo antarikṣāṇy akhyad gabhīravepā asuraḥ sunīthaḥ 
RVxx kvedānīṃ sūryaḥ kaś ciketa katamāṃ dyāṃ raśmir asyā tatāna 
RVxx aṣṭau vy akhyat kakubhaḥ pṛthivyās trī dhanva yojanā sapta sindhūn 
RVxx hiraṇyākṣaḥ savitā deva āgād dadhad ratnā dāśuṣe vāryāṇi 
RVxx hiraṇyapāṇiḥ savitā vicarṣaṇir ubhe dyāvāpṛthivī antar īyate 
RVxx apāmīvām bādhate veti sūryam abhi kṛṣṇena rajasā dyām ṛṇoti 
RV hiraṇyahasto asuraḥ sunīthaḥ sumṛḷīkaḥ svavān yātvarvāṃ
RV apasedhan rakṣaso yātudhānānasthād devaḥ pratidoṣaṃ gṛṇānaḥ
RV ye te panthāḥ savitaḥ pūrvyāso 'reṇavaḥ sukṛtā antarikṣe
RV tebhirno adya pathibhiḥ sugebhī rakṣā ca no adhi ca brūhi deva
RV pra vo yahvaṃ purūṇāṃ viśāṃ devayatīnām
RV agniṃ sūktebhirvacobhirīmahe yaṃ sīmidanya īḷate
RV janāso agniṃ dadhire sahovṛdhaṃ haviṣmanto vidhema te
RV sa tvaṃ no adya sumanā ihāvitā bhavā vājeṣu santya
RV pra tvā dūtaṃ vṛṇīmahe hotāraṃ viśvavedasam
RV mahaste sato vi carantyarcayo divi spṛśanti bhānavaḥ
RV devāsastvā varuṇo mitro aryamā saṃ dūtaṃ pratnamindhate
RV viśvaṃ so agne jayati tvayā dhanaṃ yaste dadāśa martyaḥ
RV mandro hotā gṛhapatiragne dūto viśāmasi
RV tve viśvā saṃgatāni vratā dhruvā yāni devā akṛṇvata
RV tve idagne subhage yaviṣṭhya viśvamā hūyate haviḥ
RV satvaṃ no adya sumanā utāparaṃ yakṣi devān suvīryā
RV taṃ ghemitthā namasvina upa svarājamāsate
RV hotrābhiragniṃ manuṣaḥ samindhate titirvāṃso ati sridhaḥ
RV ghnanto vṛtramataran rodasī apa uru kṣayāya cakrire
RV bhuvat kaṇve vṛṣā dyumnyāhutaḥ krandadaśvo gaviṣṭiṣu
RV saṃ sīdasva mahānasi śocasva devavītamaḥ
RV vi dhūmamagne aruṣaṃ miyedhya sṛja praśasta darśatam
RV yaṃ tvā devāso manave dadhuriha yajiṣṭhaṃ havyavāhana
RV yaṃ kaṇvo medhyātithirdhanaspṛtaṃ yaṃ vṛṣā yamupastutaḥ
RV yamagniṃ medhyātithiḥ kaṇva īdha ṛtādadhi
RV tasya preṣo dīdiyustamimā ṛcastamagniṃ vardhayāmasi
RV rāyas pūrdhi svadhāvo 'sti hi te 'gne deveṣvāpyam
RV tvaṃvājasya śrutyasya rājasi sa no mṛḷa mahānasi

RV ūrdhvovājasya sanitā yadañjibhirvāghadbhirvihvayāmahe
RV ūrdhvo naḥ pāhyaṃhaso ni ketunā viśvaṃ samatriṇaṃ daha
RV kṛdhī na ūrdhvāñcarathāya jīvase vidā deveṣu no duvaḥ
RV pāhi no agne rakṣasaḥ pāhi dhūrterarāvṇaḥ
RV pāhi rīṣata uta vā jighāṃsato bṛhadbhāno yaviṣṭhya

RV agnirvavne suvīryamagniḥ kaṇvāya saubhagam
RV agniḥ prāvan mitrota medhyātithimagniḥ sātā upastutam
RV agninā turvaśaṃ yaduṃ parāvata ugrādevaṃ havāmahe
RV agnirnayan navavāstvaṃ bṛhadrathaṃ turvītiṃ dasyave sahaḥ
RV ni tvāmagne manurdadhe jyotirjanāya śaśvate

RV tveṣāso agneramavanto arcayo bhīmāso na pratītaye
RV rakṣasvinaḥ sadamid yātumāvato viśvaṃ samatriṇaṃ daha
RV krīḷaṃ vaḥ śardho mārutamanarvāṇaṃ ratheśubham
RV kaṇvā abhi pra gāyata
RV ye pṛṣatībhirṛṣṭibhiḥ sākaṃ vāśībhirañjibhiḥ

RV iheva śṛṇva eṣāṃ kaśā hasteṣu yad vadān

RV jambhe rasasya vāvṛdhe

RVxx yat sīm antaṃ na dhūnutha

RV imāṃ ca vācaṃ pratiharyathā naro viśved vāmā vo aśnavat
RV ko devayantamaśnavajjanaṃ ko vṛktabarhiṣam
RV prapra dāśvān pastyābhirasthitāntarvāvat kṣayaṃ dadhe
RV upa kṣstraṃ pṛñcīta hanti rājabhirbhaye cit sukṣitiṃ dadhe
RV nāsya vartā na tarutā mahādhane nārbhe asti vajriṇaḥ
RV yaṃ rakṣanti pracetaso varuṇo mitro aryamā
RV nū cit sa dabhyate janaḥ
RV yaṃ bāhuteva piprati pānti martyaṃ riṣaḥ
RV ariṣṭaḥ sarva edhate
RV vi durgā vi dviṣaḥ puro ghnanti rājāna eṣām
RV nayanti duritā tiraḥ
RV sugaḥ panthā anṛkṣara ādityāsa ṛtaṃ yate
RV nātrāvakhādo asti vaḥ
RV yaṃ yajñaṃ nayathā nara ādityā ṛjunā pathā
RV pra vaḥ sa dhītaye naśat
RV sa ratnaṃ martyo vasu viśvaṃ tokamuta tmanā
RV achā gachatyastṛtaḥ
RV kathā rādhāma sakhāyaḥ stomaṃ mitrasyāryamṇaḥ
RV mahi psaro varuṇasya
RV mā vo ghnantaṃ mā śapantaṃ prati voce devayantam
RV sumnairid va ā vivāse
RV caturaścid dadamānād bibhīyādā nidhātoḥ
RV na duruktāya spṛhayet
RV saṃ pūṣannadhvanastira vyaṃho vimuco napāt
RV sakṣvā devapra ṇas puraḥ
RV yo naḥ pūṣannagho vṛko duḥśeva ādideśati
RV apa sma tampatho jahi
RV apa tyaṃ paripanthinaṃ muṣīvāṇaṃ huraścitam
RV dūramadhisruteraja
RV tvaṃ tasya dvayāvino 'ghaśaṃsasya kasya cit
RV padābhi tiṣṭha tapuṣim
RV ā tat te dasra mantumaḥ pūṣannavo vṛṇīmahe
RV yena pitṝnacodayaḥ
RV adhā no viśvasaubhaga hiraṇyavāśīmattama
RV dhanāni suṣaṇā kṛdhi
RV ati naḥ saścato naya sugā naḥ supathā kṛṇu
RV pūṣannihakratuṃ vidaḥ
RV abhi sūyavasaṃ naya na navajvāro adhvane
RV pū
RV śagdhi pūrdhi pra yaṃsi ca śiśīhi prāsyudaram
RV pū
RV na pūṣaṇaṃ methāmasi sūktairabhi gṛṇīmasi
RV vasūni dasmamīmahe
RV kad rudrāya pracetase mīḷhuṣṭamāya tavyase
RV vocema śantamaṃ hṛde
RV yathā no aditiḥ karat paśve nṛbhyo yathā gave
RV yathā tokāya rudriyam
RV yathā no mitro varuṇo yathā rudraściketati
RV yathā viśve sajoṣasaḥ
RV gāthapatiṃ medhapatiṃ rudraṃ jalāṣabheṣajam
RV tacchaṃyoḥ sumnamīmahe
RV yaḥ śukra iva sūryo hiraṇyamiva rocate
RV śreṣṭho devānāṃ vasuḥ
RV śaṃ naḥ karatyarvate sugaṃ meṣāya meṣye
RV nṛbhyo nāribhyo gave
RV asme soma śriyamadhi ni dhehi śatasya nṛṇām
RV mahi śravastuvinṛmṇam
RV mā naḥ somaparibādho mārātayo juhuranta
RV ā na indo vāje bhaja
RV yāste prajā amṛtasya parasmin dhāmannṛtasya
RV mūrdhā nābhā soma vena ābhūṣantīḥ soma vedaḥ
RV agne vivasvaduṣasaścitraṃ rādho amartya
RV ā dāśuṣe jātavedo vahā tvamadyā devānuṣarbudhaḥ
RV juṣṭo hi dūto asi havyavāhano 'gne rathīradhvarāṇām
RV sajūraśvibhyāmuṣasā suvīryamasme dhehi śravo bṛhat
RV adyā dūtaṃ vṛṇīmahe vasumagniṃ purupriyam
RV dhūmaketuṃ bhāṛjīkaṃ vyuṣṭiṣu yajñānāmadhvaraśriyam
RV śreṣṭhaṃ yaviṣṭhamatithiṃ svāhutaṃ juṣṭaṃ janāya dāśuṣe
RV devānachā yātave jātavedasamagnimīḷe vyuṣṭiṣu
RV staviṣyāmi tvāmahaṃ viśvasyāmṛta bhojana
RV agne trātāramamṛtaṃ miyedhya yajiṣṭhaṃ havyavāhana
RV suśaṃso bodhi gṛṇate yaviṣṭhya madhujihvaḥ svāhutaḥ
RV praskaṇvasya pratirannāyurjīvase namasyā daivyaṃ janam
RV hotāraṃ viśvavedasaṃ saṃ hi tvā viśa indhate
RV sa ā vaha puruhūta pracetaso 'gne devāniha dravat
RV savitāramuṣasamaśvinā bhagamagniṃ vyuṣṭiṣu kṣapaḥ
RV kaṇvāsastvā sutasomāsa indhate havyavāhaṃ svadhvara
RV patir hi adhvarāṇām agne dūto viśām asi
RV uṣarbudha āvaha somapītaye devānadya svardṛśaḥ
RV agne pūrvā anūṣaso vibhāvaso dīdetha viśvadarṣataḥ
RV asi grāmeṣvavitā purohito 'si yajñeṣu mānuṣaḥ
RV ni tvā yajñasya sādhanamagne hotāram ṛtvijam
RV manuṣvad deva dhīmahi pracetasaṃ jīraṃ dūtamamartyam
RV yad devānāṃ mitramahaḥ purohito 'ntaro yāsi dūtyam
RV sindhoriva prasvanitāsa ūrmayo 'gnerbhrājante arcayaḥ
RV śrudhi śrutkarṇa vahnibhirdevairagne sayāvabhiḥ
RV ā sīdantu barhiṣi mitro aryamā prātaryāvāṇo adhvaram
RV śṛṇvantu stomaṃ marutaḥ sudānavo 'gnijihvā ṛtāvṛdhaḥ
RV pibatu somaṃ varuṇo dhṛtavrato 'śvibhyāmuṣasā sajūḥ
RV tvamagne vasūnriha rudrānādityānuta
RV yajā svadhvaraṃ janaṃ manujātaṃ ghṛtapruṣam
RV śruṣṭīvāno hi dāśuṣe devā agne vicetasaḥ
RV tān rohidaśva girvaṇastrayastriṃśatamā vaha
RV priyamedhavadatrivajjātavedo virūpavat
RV aṅgirasvan mahivrata praskaṇvasya śrudhī havam
RV mahikerava ūtaye priyamedhā ahūṣata
RV rājantamadhvarāṇāmagniṃ śukreṇa śociṣā
RV ghṛtāhavana santyemā u ṣu śrudhī giraḥ
RV yābhiḥ kaṇvasya sūnavo havante 'vase tvā
RV tvāṃ citraśravastama havante vikṣu jantavaḥ
RV śociṣkeśampurupriyāgne havyāya voḷhave
RV ni tvā hotāram ṛtvijaṃ dadhire vasuvittamam
RV śrutkarṇaṃ saprathastamaṃ viprā agne diviṣṭiṣu
RV ā tvā viprā acucyavuḥ sutasomā abhi prayaḥ
RV bṛhad bhā bibhrato haviragne martāya dāśuṣe
RV prātaryāvṇaḥ sahaskṛta somapeyāya santya
RV ihādya daivyaṃjanaṃ barhirā sādayā vaso
RV arvāñcaṃ daivyaṃ janamagne yakṣva sahūtibhiḥ
RV ayaṃ somaḥ sudānavastaṃ pāta tiroahnyam
RV eṣo uṣā apūrvya vyuchati priyā divaḥ
RV stuṣe vāmaśvinā bṛhat
RV yā dasrā sindhumātarā manotarā rayīṇām
RV dhiyā devā vasuvidā
RV vacyante vāṃ kakuhāso jūrṇāyāmadhi viṣṭapi
RV yad vāṃratho vibhiṣ patāt
RV haviṣā jāro apāṃ piparti papurirnarā
RV pitā kuṭasya carṣaṇiḥ
RV ādāro vāṃ matīnāṃ nāsatyā matavacasā
RV pātaṃ somasya dhṛṣṇuyā
RV yā naḥ pīparadaśvinā jyotiṣmatī tamastiraḥ
RV tāmasme rāsāthāmiṣam
RV ā no nāvā matīnāṃ yātaṃ pārāya gantave
RV yuñjāthāmaśvinā ratham
RV aritraṃ vāṃ divas pṛthu tīrthe sindhūnāṃ rathaḥ
RV dhiyā yuyujra indavaḥ
RV divas kaṇvāsa indavo vasu sindhūnāṃ pade
RV svaṃ vavriṃ kuha dhitsathaḥ
RV abhūdu bhā u aṃśave hiraṇyaṃ prati sūryaḥ
RV vyakhyajjihvayāsitaḥ
RV abhūdu pārametave panthā ṛtaysa sādhuyā
RV adarśi vi srutirdivaḥ
RV tattadidaśvinoravo jaritā prati bhūṣati
RV made somasyapipratoḥ
RV vāvasānā vivasvati somasya pītyā girā
RV manuṣvacchambhūā gatam
RV yuvoruṣā anu śriyaṃ parijmanorupācarat
RV ṛtā vanatho aktubhiḥ
RV ubhā pibatamaśvinobhā naḥ śarma yachatam
RV avidriyābhirūtibhiḥ
RV ayaṃ vāṃ madhumattamaḥ sutaḥ soma ṛtāvṛdhā
RV tamaśvinā pibataṃ tiroahnyaṃ dhattaṃ ratnāni dāśuśe
RV trivandhureṇa trivṛtā supeśasā rathenā yātamaśvinā
RV kaṇvāso vāṃ brahma kṛṇvantyadhvare teṣāṃ su śṛṇutaṃ havam
RV aśvinā madhumattamaṃ pātaṃ somam ṛtāvṛdhā
RV athādya dasrā vasu bibhratā rathe dāśvāṃsamupa gachatam
RV triṣadhasthe barhiṣi viśvavedasā madhvā yajñaṃ mimikṣatam
RV kaṇvāso vāṃ sutasomā abhidyavo yuvāṃ havante aśvinā
RV yābhiḥ kaṇvamabhiṣṭibhiḥ prāvataṃ yuvamaśvinā
RV tābhiḥ ṣvasmānavataṃ śubhas patī pātaṃ somam ṛtāvṛdhā
RV sudāse dasrā vasu bibhratā rathe pṛkṣo vahatamaśvinā
RV rayiṃ samudrāduta vā divas paryasme dhattaṃ puruspṛham
RV yan nāsatyā parāvati yad vā stho adhi turvaśe
RV ato rathena suvṛtā na ā gataṃ sākaṃ sūryasya raśmibhiḥ
RV arvāñcā vāṃ saptayo 'dhvaraśriyo vahantu savanedupa
RV iṣaṃ pṛñcantā sukṛte sudānava ā barhiḥ sīdataṃ narā
RV tena nāsatyā gataṃ rathena sūryatvacā
RV yena śaśvadūhathurdāśuṣe vasu madhvaḥ somasya pītaye
RV ukthebhirarvāgavase purūvasū arkaiśca ni hvayāmahe
RV śaśvat kaṇvānāṃ sadasi priye hi kaṃ somaṃ papathuraśvinā
RV saha vāmena na uṣo vyuchā duhitardivaḥ
RV saha dyumnena bṛhatā vibhāvari rāyā devi dāsvatī
RV aśvāvatīrgomatīrviśvasuvido bhūri cyavanta vastave
RV udīraya prati mā sūnṛtā uṣaścoda rādho maghonām
RV uvāsoṣā uchācca nu devī jīrā rathānām
RV ye asyā ācaraṇeṣu dadhrire samudre na śravasyavaḥ
RV uṣo ye te pra yāmeṣu yuñjate mano dānāya sūrayaḥ
RV atrāha tat kaṇva eṣāṃ kaṇvatamo nāma gṛṇāti nṛṇām
RV ā ghā yoṣeva sūnaryuṣā yāti prabhuñjatī
RV jarayantī vṛjanaṃ padvadīyata ut pātayati pakṣiṇaḥ
RV vi yā sṛjati samanaṃ vyarthinaḥ padāṃ na vetyodatī
RV vayo nakiṣ ṭe paptivāṃsa āsate vyuṣṭau vājinīvati
RV eṣāyukta parāvataḥ sūryasyodayanādadhi
RV śataṃ rathebhiḥ subhagoṣā iyaṃ vi yātyabhi mānuṣān
RV viśvamasyā nānāma cakṣase jagajjyotiṣ kṛṇoti sūnarī
RV apa dveṣo maghonī duhitā diva uṣā uchadapa sridhaḥ
RV uṣa ā bhāhi bhānunā candreṇa duhitardivaḥ
RV āvahantī bhūryasmabhyaṃ saubhagaṃ vyuchantī diviṣṭiṣu
RV viśvasya hi prāṇanaṃ jīvanaṃ tve vi yaduchasi sūnari
RV sā no rathena bṛhatā vibhāvari śrudhi citrāmaghe havam
RV uṣo vājaṃ hi vaṃsva yaścitro mānuṣe jane
RV tenā vaha sukṛto adhvarānupa ye tvā gṛṇanti vahnayaḥ
RV viśvān devānā vaha somapītaye 'ntarikṣāduṣastvam
RV sāsmāsu dhā gomadaśvāvadukthyamuṣo vājaṃ suvīryam
RV yasyā ruśanto arcayaḥ prati bhadrā adṛkṣata
RV sā no rayiṃ viśvavāraṃ supeśasamuṣā dadātu sugmyam
RV ye cid dhi tvām ṛṣayaḥ pūrva ūtaye juhūre 'vase mahi
RV sā na stomānabhi gṛṇīhi rādhasoṣaḥ śukreṇa śociṣā
RV uṣo yadadya bhānunā vi dvārāv ṛṇavo divaḥ
RV pra no yachatādavṛkaṃ pṛthu chardiḥ pra devi gomatīriṣaḥ
RV saṃ no rāyā bṛhatā viśvapeśasā mimikṣvā samiḷābhirā
RV saṃ dyumnena viśvaturoṣo mahi saṃ vājairvājinīvati
RV uṣo bhadrebhirā gahi divaścid rocanādadhi
RV vahantvaruṇapsava upa tvā somino gṛham
RV supeśasaṃ sukhaṃ rathaṃ yamadhyasthā uṣastvam
RV tenā suśravasaṃ janaṃ prāvādya duhitardivaḥ
RV vayaścit te patatriṇo dvipaccatuṣpadarjuni
RV uṣaḥ prārannṛtūnranu divo antebhyas pari
RV vyuchantī hi raśmibhirviśvamābhāsi rocanam
RV tāṃ tvāmuṣarvasūyavo gīrbhiḥ kaṇvā ahūṣata
RV udu tyaṃ jātavedasaṃ devaṃ vahanti ketavaḥ
RV dṛśe viśvāya sūryam
RV apa tye tāyavo yathā nakṣatrā yantyaktubhiḥ
RV sūrāya viśvacakṣase
RV adṛśramasya ketavo vi raśmayo janānanu
RV bhrājanto agnayo yathā
RV taraṇirviśvadarśato jyotiṣkṛdasi sūrya
RV viśvamā bhāsirocanam
RV pratyaṃ devānāṃ viśaḥ pratyaṅṅ udeṣi mānuṣān
RV pratyaṃ viśvaṃ svardṛśe
RV yenā pāvaka cakṣasā bhuraṇyantaṃ janānanu
RV tvaṃ varuṇa paśyasi
RV vi dyāmeṣi rajas pṛthvahā mimāno aktubhiḥ
RV paśyañ janmāni sūrya
RV sapta tvā harito rathe vahanti deva sūrya
RV śociṣkeśaṃ vicakṣaṇa
RV ayukta sapta śundhyuvaḥ sūro rathasya naptyaḥ
RV tābhiryāti svayuktibhiḥ
RV ud vayaṃ tamasas pari jyotiṣ paśyanta uttaram
RV devaṃ devatrā sūryamaganma jyotiruttamam
RV udyannadya mitramaha ārohannuttarāṃ divam
RV hṛdrogaṃ mamasūrya harimāṇaṃ ca nāśaya
RV śukeṣu me harimāṇaṃ ropaṇākāsu dadhmasi
RV atho hāridraveṣu me harimāṇaṃ ni dadhmasi
RV udagādayamādityo viśvena sahasā saha
RV dviṣantaṃ mahyaṃ randhayan mo aham dviṣate radham
RV abhi tyaṃ meṣaṃ puruhūtam ṛgmiyamindraṃ gīrbhirmadatā vasvo arṇavam
RV yasya dyāvo na vicaranti mānuṣā bhuje maṃhiṣṭhamabhi vipramarcata
RV abhīmavanvan svabhiṣṭimūtayo 'ntarikṣaprāṃ taviṣībhirāvṛtam
RV indraṃ dakṣāsa ṛbhavo madacyutaṃ śatakratuṃ javanī sūnṛtāruhat
RV tvaṃ gotramaṅgirobhyo 'vṛṇorapotātraye śatadureṣu gātuvit
RV sasena cid vimadāyāvaho vasvājāvadriṃ vāvasānasyanartayan
RV tvamapāmapidhānāvṛṇor apādhārayaḥ parvate dānumad vasu
RV vṛtraṃ yadindra śavasāvadhīrahimādit sūryaṃ divyārohayo dṛśe
RV tvaṃ māyābhirapa māyino 'dhamaḥ svadhābhirye adhi śuptāvajuhvata
RV tvaṃ piprornṛmaṇaḥ prārujaḥ puraḥ pra ṛjiśvānaṃ dasyuhatyeṣvāvitha
RV tvaṃ kutsaṃ śuṣṇahatyeṣvāvithārandhayo 'tithigvāya śambaram
RV mahāntaṃ cidarbudaṃ ni kramīḥ padā sanādeva dasyuhatyāya jajñiṣe
RV tve viśvā taviṣī sadhryag ghitā tava rādhaḥ somapīthāya harṣate
RV tava vajraścikite bāhvorhito vṛścā śatrorava viśvāni vṛṣṇyā
RV vi jānīhyāryān ye ca dasyavo barhiṣmate randhayā śāsadavratān
RV śākī bhava yajamānasya coditā viśvet tā te sadhamādeṣu cākana
RV anuvratāya randhayannapavratānābhūbhirindraḥ śnathayannanābhuvaḥ
RV vṛddhasya cid vardhato dyāminakṣata stavāno vamro vi jaghāna sandihaḥ
RV takṣad yat ta uśanā sahasā saho vi rodasī majmanā bādhate śavaḥ
RV ā tvā vātasya nṛmaṇo manoyuja ā pūryamāṇamavahannabhi śravaḥ
RV mandiṣṭa yaduśane kāvye sacānindro vaṅkū vaṅkutarādhi tiṣṭhati
RV ugro yayiṃ nirapaḥ srotasāsṛjad vi śuṣṇasya dṛṃhitā airayat puraḥ
RV ā smā rathaṃ vṛṣapāṇeṣu tiṣṭhasi śāryātasya prabhṛtāyeṣu mandase
RV indra yathā sutasomeṣu cākano 'narvāṇaṃślokamā rohase divi
RV adadā arbhāṃ mahate vacasyave kakṣīvate vṛcayāmindra sunvate
RV menābhavo vṛṣaṇaśvasya sukrato viśvet tā te savaneṣu pravācyā
RV indro aśrāyi sudhyo nireke pajreṣu stomo duryo na yūpaḥ
RV aśvayurgavyū rathayurvasūyurindra id rāyaḥ kṣayati prayantā
RV idaṃ namo vṛṣabhāya svarāje satyaśuṣmāya tavase 'vāci
RV asminnindra vṛjane sarvavīrāḥ smat sūribhistava śarman syāma
RV tyaṃ su meṣaṃ mahayā svarvidaṃ śataṃ yasya subhvaḥ sākamīrate
RV atyaṃ na vājaṃ havanasyadaṃ rathamendraṃ vavṛtyāmavase suvṛktibhiḥ
RV sa parvato na dharuṇeṣvacyutaḥ sahasramūtistaviṣīṣu vāvṛdhe
RV indro yad vṛtramavadhīn nadīvṛtamubjannarṇāṃsijarhṛṣāṇo andhasā
RV sa hi dvaro dvariṣu vavra ūdhani candrabudhno madavṛddho manīṣibhiḥ
RV indraṃ tamahve svapasyayā dhiyā maṃhiṣṭharātiṃ sa hi paprirandhasaḥ
RV ā yaṃ pṛṇanti divi sadmabarhiṣaḥ samudraṃ na subhvaḥ svā abhiṣṭayaḥ
RV taṃ vṛtrahatye anu tasthurūtayaḥ śuṣmāindramavātā ahrutapsavaḥ
RV abhi svavṛṣṭiṃ made asya yudhyato raghvīriva pravaṇe sasrurūtayaḥ
RV indro yad vajrī dhṛṣamāṇo andhasā bhinad valasya paridhīnriva tritaḥ
RV parīṃ ghṛṇā carati titviṣe śavo 'po vṛtvī rajaso budhnamāśayat
RV vṛtrasya yat pravaṇe durgṛbhiśvano nijaghantha hanvorindra tanyatum
RV hradaṃ na hi tvā nyṛṣantyūrmayo brahmāṇīndra tava yāni vardhanā
RV tvaṣṭā cit te yujyaṃ vāvṛdhe śavastatakṣa vajramabhibhūtyojasam
RV jaghanvānu haribhiḥ sambhṛtakratavindra vṛtraṃ manuṣe gātuyannapaḥ
RV ayachathā bāhvorvajramāyasamadhārayo divyā sūryaṃ dṛśe
RV bṛhat svaścandramamavad yadukthyamakṛṇvata bhiyasā rohaṇaṃ divaḥ
RV yan mānuṣapradhanā indramūtayaḥ svarnṛṣāco maruto 'madannanu
RV dyauścidasyāmavānaheḥ svanādayoyavīd bhiyasā vajra indra te
RV vṛtrasya yad badbadhānasya rodasī made sutasya śavasābhinacchiraḥ
RV yadin nvindra pṛthivī daśabhujirahāni viśvā tatanantakṛṣṭayaḥ
RV atrāha te maghavan viśrutaṃ saho dyāmanu śavasā barhaṇā bhuvat
RV tvamasya pāre rajaso vyomanaḥ svabhūtyojā avase dhṛṣanmanaḥ
RV cakṛṣe bhūmiṃ pratimānamojaso 'paḥ svaḥ paribhūreṣyā divam
RV tvaṃ bhuvaḥ pratimānaṃ pṛthivyā ṛṣvavīrasya bṛhataḥ patirbhūḥ
RV viśvamāprā antarikṣaṃ mahitvā satyamaddhā nakiranyastvāvān
RV na yasya dyāvāpṛthivī anu vyaco na sindhavo rajaso antamānaśuḥ
RV nota svavṛṣṭiṃ made asya yudhyata eko anyaccakṛṣe viśvamānuṣak
RV ārcannatra marutaḥ sasminnājau viśve devāso amadannanutvā
RV vṛtrasya yad bhṛṣṭimatā vadhena ni tvamindra pratyānaṃ jaghantha
RV nyū ṣu vācaṃ pra mahe bharāmahe gira indrāya sadane vivasvataḥ
RV nū cid dhi ratnaṃ sasatāmivāvidan na duṣṭutirdraviṇodeṣu śasyate
RV duro aśvasya dura indra gorasi duro yavasya vasuna inas patiḥ
RV śikṣānaraḥ pradivo akāmakarśanaḥ sakhā sakhibhyastamidaṃ gṛṇīmasi
RV śacīva indra purukṛd dyumattama tavedidamabhitaścekite vasu
RV ataḥ saṃgṛbhyābhibhūta ā bhara mā tvāyato jarituḥ kāmamūnayīḥ
RV ebhirdyubhiḥ sumanā ebhirindubhirnirundhāno amatiṃ gobhiraśvinā
RV indreṇa dasyuṃ darayanta indubhiryutadveṣasaḥsamiṣā rabhemahi
RV samindra rāyā samiṣā rabhemahi saṃ vājebhiḥ puruścandrairabhidyubhiḥ
RV saṃ devyā pramatyā vīraśuṣmayā goagrayāśvāvatyā rabhemahi
RV te tvā madā amadan tāni vṛṣṇyā te somāso vṛtrahatyeṣu satpate
RV yat kārave daśa vṛtrāṇyaprati barhiṣmate ni sahasrāṇi barhayaḥ
RV yudhā yudhamupa ghedeṣi dhṛṣṇuyā purā puraṃ samidaṃ haṃsyojasā
RV namyā yadindra sakhyā parāvati nibarhayo namuciṃ nāma māyinam
RV tvaṃ karañjamuta parṇayaṃ vadhīstejiṣṭhayātithigvasyavartanī
RV tvaṃ śatā vaṅgṛdasyābhinat puro 'nānudaḥ pariṣūtā ṛjiśvanā
RV tvametāñ janarājño dvirdaśābandhunā suśravasopajagmuṣaḥ
RV ṣaṣṭiṃ sahasrā navatiṃ nava śruto ni cakreṇa rathyā duṣpadāvṛṇak
RV tvamāvitha suśravasaṃ tavotibhistava trāmabhirindra tūrvayāṇam
RV tvamasmai kutsamatithigvamāyuṃ mahe rājñe yūne arandhanāyaḥ
RV ya udṛcīndra devagopāḥ sakhāyaste śivatamā asāma
RV tvāṃ stoṣāma tvayā suvīrā drāghīya āyuḥ prataraṃ dadhānāḥ
RV mā no asmin maghavan pṛtsvaṃhasi nahi te antaḥ śavasaḥ parīṇaśe
RV akrandayo nadyo roruvad vanā kathā na kṣoṇīrbhiyasā samārata
RV arcā śakrāya śākine śacīvate śṛṇvantamindraṃ mahayannabhi ṣṭuhi
RV yo dhṛṣṇunā śavasā rodasī ubhe vṛṣā vṛṣatvā vṛṣabho nyṛñjate
RV arcā dive bṛhate śūṣyaṃ vacaḥ svakṣatraṃ yasya dhṛṣato dhṛṣan manaḥ
RV bṛhacchravā asuro barhaṇā kṛtaḥ puro haribhyāṃ vṛṣabho ratho hi ṣaḥ
RV tvaṃ divo bṛhataḥ sānu kopayo 'va tmanā dhṛṣatā śambaraṃ bhinat
RV yan māyino vrandino mandinā dhṛṣacchitāṃ gabhastimaśaniṃ pṛtanyasi
RV ni yad vṛṇakṣi śvasanasya mūrdhani śuṣṇasya cid vrandinororuvad vanā
RV prācīnena manasā barhaṇāvatā yadadyā cit kṛṇavaḥ kastvā pari
RV tvamāvitha naryaṃ turvaśaṃ yaduṃ tvaṃ turvītiṃ vayyaṃśatakrato
RV tvaṃ rathametaśaṃ kṛtvye dhane tvaṃ puro navatiṃ dambhayo nava
RV sa ghā rājā satpatiḥ śūśuvajjano rātahavyaḥ prati yaḥ śāsaminvati
RV ukthā vā yo abhigṛṇāti rādhasā dānurasmā uparā pinvate divaḥ
RV asamaṃ kṣatramasamā manīṣā pra somapā apasā santu neme
RV ye ta indra daduṣo vardhayanti mahi kṣatraṃ sthaviraṃ vṛṣṇyaṃ ca
RV tubhyedete bahulā adridugdhāścamūṣadaścamasā indrapānāḥ
RV vyaśnuhi tarpayā kāmameṣāmathā mano vasudeyāya kṛṣva
RV apāmatiṣṭhad dharuṇahvaraṃ tamo 'ntarvṛtrasya jaṭhareṣuparvataḥ
RV abhīmindro nadyo vavriṇā hitā viśvā anuṣṭhāḥ pravaṇeṣu jighnate
RV sa śevṛdhamadhi dhā dyumnamasme mahi kṣatraṃ janāṣāḷindra tavyam
RV rakṣā ca no maghonaḥ pāhi sūrīn rāye ca naḥ svapatyā iṣe dhāḥ
RV divaścidasya varimā vi papratha indraṃ na mahnā pṛthivīcana prati
RV bhīmastuviṣmāñcarṣaṇibhya ātapaḥ śiśīte vajraṃ tejase na vaṃsagaḥ
RV so arṇavo na nadyaḥ samudriyaḥ prati gṛbhṇāti viśritā varīmabhiḥ
RV indraḥ somasya pītaye vṛṣāyate sanāt sa yudhma ojasā panasyate
RV tvaṃ tamindra parvataṃ na bhojase maho nṛmṇasya dharmaṇāmirajyasi
RV pra vīryeṇa devatāti cekite viśvasmā ugraḥ karmaṇe purohitaḥ
RV sa id vane namasyubhirvacasyate cāru janeṣu prabruvāṇa indriyam
RV vṛṣā chandurbhavati haryato vṛṣā kṣemeṇa dhenāmmaghavā yadinvati
RV sa in mahāni samithāni majmanā kṛṇoti yudhma ojasā janebhyaḥ
RV adhā cana śrad dadhati tviṣīmata indrāya vajraṃ nighanighnate vadham
RV sa hi śravasyuḥ sadanāni kṛtrimā kṣmayā vṛdhāna ojasāvināśayan
RV jyotīṃṣi kṛṇvannavṛkāṇi yajyave 'va sukratuḥ sartavā apaḥ sṛjat
RV dānāya manaḥ somapāvannastu te 'rvāñcā harī vandanaśrudā kṛdhi
RV yamiṣṭhāsaḥ sārathayo ya indra te na tvā ketāā dabhnuvanti bhūrṇayaḥ
RV aprakṣitaṃ vasu bibharṣi hastayoraṣāḷhaṃ sahastanvi śruto dadhe
RV āvṛtāso 'vatāso na kartṛbhistanūṣu te kratavaindra bhūrayaḥ
RV eṣa pra pūrvīrava tasya camriṣo 'tyo na yoṣāmudayaṃsta bhurvaṇiḥ
RV dakṣaṃ mahe pāyayate hiraṇyayaṃ rathamāvṛtyā hariyogam ṛbhvasam
RV taṃ gūrtayo nemanniṣaḥ parīṇasaḥ samudraṃ na saṃcaraṇe saniṣyavaḥ
RV patiṃ dakṣasya vidathasya nū saho giriṃ na venā adhi roha tejasā
RV sa turvaṇirmahānareṇu pauṃsye girerbhṛṣṭirna bhrājate tujā śavaḥ
RV yena śuṣṇaṃ māyinamāyaso made dudhraābhūṣu rāmayan ni dāmani
RV devī yadi taviṣī tvāvṛdhotaya indraṃ siṣaktyuṣasaṃ na sūryaḥ
RV yo dhṛṣṇunā śavasā bādhate tama iyarti reṇuṃ bṛhadarhariṣvaṇiḥ
RV vi yat tiro dharuṇamacyutaṃ rajo 'tiṣṭhipo diva ātāsubarhaṇā
RV svarmīḷhe yan mada indra harṣyāhan vṛtraṃ nirapāmaubjo arṇavam
RV tvaṃ divo dharuṇaṃ dhiṣa ojasā pṛthivyā indra sadaneṣu māhinaḥ
RV tvaṃ sutasya made ariṇā apo vi vṛtrasya samayā pāṣyārujaḥ
RV pra maṃhiṣṭhāya bṛhate bṛhadraye satyaśuṣmāya tavase matiṃ bhare
RV apāmiva pravaṇe yasya durdharaṃ rādho viśvāyuśavase apāvṛtam
RV adha te viśvamanu hāsadiṣṭaya āpo nimneva savanā haviṣmataḥ
RV yat parvate na samaśīta haryata indrasya vajraḥ śnathitā hiraṇyayaḥ
RV asmai bhīmāya namasā samadhvara uṣo na śubhra ā bharāpanīyase
RV yasya dhāma śravase nāmendriyaṃ jyotirakāriharito nāyase
RV ime ta indra te vayaṃ puruṣṭuta ye tvārabhya carāmasi prabhūvaso
RV nahi tvadanyo girvaṇo giraḥ saghat kṣoṇīriva prati no harya tad vacaḥ
RV bhūri ta indra vīryaṃ tava smasyasya stoturmaghavan kāmamā pṛṇa
RV anu te dyaurbṛhatī vīryaṃ mama iyaṃ ca te pṛthivī nema ojase
RV tvaṃ tamindra parvataṃ mahāmuruṃ vajreṇa vajrin parvaśaścakartitha
RV avāsṛjo nivṛtāḥ sartavā apaḥ satrā viśvaṃ dadhiṣe kevalaṃ sahaḥ
RV nū cit sahojā amṛto ni tundate hotā yad dūto abhavad vivasvataḥ
RV vi sādhiṣṭhebhiḥ pathibhī rajo mama ā devatātāhaviṣā vivāsati
RV ā svamadma yuvamāno ajarastṛṣvaviṣyannataseṣu tiṣṭhati
RV atyo na pṛṣṭhaṃ pruṣitasya rocate divo na sānu stanayannacikradat
RV krāṇā rudrebhirvasubhiḥ purohito hotā niṣatto rayiṣāḷamartyaḥ
RV ratho na vikṣv ṛñjasāna āyuṣu vyānuṣag vāryā deva ṛṇvati
RV vi vātajūto ataseṣu tiṣṭhate vṛthā juhūbhiḥ sṛṇyā tuviṣvaṇiḥ
RV tṛṣu yadagne vanino vṛṣāyase kṛṣṇaṃ ta ema ruśadūrme ajara
RV tapurjambho vana ā vātacodito yūthe na sāhvānava vāti vaṃsagaḥ
RV abhivrajannakṣitaṃ pājasā rajaḥ sthātuścarathaṃ bhayate patatriṇaḥ
RV dadhuṣ ṭvā bhṛgavo mānuṣeṣvā rayiṃ na cāruṃ suhavaṃ janebhyaḥ
RV hotāramagne atithiṃ vareṇyaṃ mitraṃ na śevaṃ divyāya janmane
RV hotāraṃ sapta juhvo yajiṣṭhaṃ yaṃ vāghato vṛṇate adhvareṣu
RV agniṃ viśveṣāmaratiṃ vasūnāṃ saparyāmi prayasā yāmi ratnam
RV achidrā sūno sahaso no adya stotṛbhyo mitramahaḥ śarma yacha
RV agne gṛṇantamaṃhasa uruṣyorjo napāt pūrbhirāyasībhiḥ
RV bhavā varūthaṃ gṛṇate vibhāvo bhavā maghavan maghavadbhyaḥśarma
RV uruṣyāgne aṃhaso gṛṇantaṃ prātarmakṣū dhiyāvasurjagamyāt
RV vayā idagne agnayaste anye tve viśve amṛtā mādayante
RV vaiśvānara nābhirasi kṣitīnāṃ sthūṇeva janānupamid yayantha
RV mūrdhā divo nābhiragniḥ pṛthivyā athābhavadaratī rodasyoḥ
RV taṃ tvā devāso 'janayanta devaṃ vaiśvānara jyotiridāryāya
RV ā sūrye na raśmayo dhruvāso vaiśvānare dadhire 'gnā vasūni
RV yā parvateṣvoṣadhīṣvapsu yā mānuṣeṣvasi tasya rājā
RV bṛhatī iva sūnave rodasī giro hotā manuṣyo na dakṣaḥ
RV svarvate satyaśuṣmāya pūrvīrvaiśvānarāya nṛtamāya yahvīḥ
RV divaścit te bṛhato jātavedo vaiśvānara pra ririce mahitvam
RV rājā kṛṣṭīnāmasi mānuṣīṇāṃ yudhā devebhyo varivaścakartha
RV pra nū mahitvaṃ vṛṣabhasya vocaṃ yaṃ pūravo vṛtrahaṇaṃ sacante
RV vaiśvānaro dasyumagnirjaghanvānadhūnot kāṣṭhā ava śambaraṃ bhet
RV vaiśvānaro mahimnā viśvakṛṣṭirbharadvājeṣu yajato vibhāvā
RV śātavaneye śatinībhiragniḥ puruṇīthe jarate sūnṛtāvān
RV vahniṃ yaśasaṃ vidathasya ketuṃ suprāvyaṃ dūtaṃ sadyoartham
RV dvijanmānaṃ rayimiva praśastaṃ rātiṃ bharad bhṛgavemātariśvā
RV asya śāsurubhayāsaḥ sacante haviṣmanta uśijo ye ca martāḥ
RV divaścit pūrvo nyasādi hotāpṛchyo viśpatirvikṣuvedhāḥ
RV taṃ navyasī hṛda ā jāyamānamasmat sukīrtirmadhujihvamaśyāḥ
RV yam ṛtvijo vṛjane mānuṣāsaḥ prayasvanta āyavo jījananta
RV uśik pāvako vasurmānuṣeṣu vareṇyo hotādhāyi vikṣu
RV damūnā gṛhapatirdama ā agnirbhuvad rayipatī rayīṇām
RV taṃ tvā vayaṃ patimagne rayīṇāṃ pra śaṃsāmo matibhirgotamāsaḥ
RV āśuṃ na vājambharaṃ marjayantaḥ prātarmakṣū dhiyāvasurjagamyāt
RV asmā idu pra tavase turāya prayo na harmi stomaṃ māhināya
RV ṛcīṣamāyādhrigava ohamindrāya brahmāṇi rātatamā
RV asmā idu praya iva pra yaṃsi bharāmyāṅgūṣaṃ bādhe suvṛkti
RV indrāya hṛdā manasā manīṣā pratnāya patye dhiyomarjayanta
RV asmā idu tyamupamaṃ svarṣāṃ bharāmyāṅgūṣamāsyena
RV maṃhiṣṭhamachoktibhirmatīnāṃ suvṛktibhiḥ sūriṃ vāvṛdhadhyai
RV asmā idu stomaṃ saṃ hinomi rathaṃ na taṣṭeva tatsināya
RV giraśca girvāhase suvṛktīndrāya viśvaminvaṃ medhirāya
RV asmā idu saptimiva śravasyendrāyārkaṃ juhvā samañje
RV vīraṃ dānaukasaṃ vandadhyai purāṃ gūrtaśravasaṃ darmāṇam
RV asmā idu tvaṣṭā takṣad vajraṃ svapastamaṃ svaryaṃ raṇāya
RV vṛtrasya cid vidad yena marma tujannīśānastujatā kiyedhāḥ
RV asyedu mātuḥ savaneṣu sadyo mahaḥ pituṃ papivāñcārvannā
RV muṣāyad viṣṇuḥ pacataṃ sahīyān vidhyad varāhantiro adrimastā
RV asmā idu gnāścid devapatnīrindrāyārkamahihatya ūvuḥ
RV pari dyāvāpṛthivī jabhra urvī nāsya te mahimānaṃ pariṣṭaḥ
RV asyedeva pra ririce mahitvaṃ divas pṛthivyāḥ paryantarikṣāt
RV svarāḷ indro dama ā viśvagūrtaḥ svariramatro vavakṣe raṇāya
RV asyedeva śavasā śuṣantaṃ vi vṛścad vajreṇa vṛtramindraḥ
RV gā na vrāṇā avanīramuñcadabhi śravo dāvane sacetāḥ
RV asyedu tveṣasā ranta sindhavaḥ pari yad vajreṇa sīmayachat
RV īśānakṛd dāśuṣe daśasyan turvītaye gādhaṃ turvaṇiḥ kaḥ
RV asmā idu pra bharā tūtujāno vṛtrāya vajramīśānaḥ kiyedhāḥ
RV gorna parva vi radā tiraśceṣyannarṇāṃsyapāṃ caradhyai
RV asyedu pra brūhi pūrvyāṇi turasya karmāṇi navya ukthaiḥ
RV yudhe yadiṣṇāna āyudhāny ṛghāyamāṇo niriṇāti śatrūn
RV asyedu bhiyā girayaśca dṛḷhā dyāvā ca bhūmā januṣastujete
RV upo venasya joguvāna oṇiṃ sadyo bhuvad vīryāya nodhāḥ
RV asmā idu tyadanu dāyyeṣāmeko yad vavne bhūrerīśānaḥ
RV praitaśaṃ sūrye paspṛdhānaṃ sauvaśvye suṣvimāvadindraḥ
RV evā te hāriyojanā suvṛktīndra brahmāṇi gotamāso akran
RV aiṣu viśvapeśasaṃ dhiyaṃ dhāḥ prātar makṣū dhiyāvasur jagamyāt
RV pra manmahe śavasānāya śūṣamāṅgūṣaṃ girvaṇase aṅgirasvat
RV suvṛktibhiḥ stuvata ṛgmiyāyārcāmārkaṃ nare viśrutāya
RV pra vo mahe mahi namo bharadhvamāṅgūṣyaṃ śavasānāya sāma
RV yenā naḥ pūrve pitaraḥ padajñā arcanto aṅgiraso gā avindan
RV indrasyāṅgirasāṃ ceṣṭau vidat saramā tanayāya dhāsim
RV bṛhaspatirbhinadadriṃ vidad gāḥ samusriyābhirvāvaśanta naraḥ
RV sa suṣṭubhā sa stubhā sapta vipraiḥ svareṇādriṃ svaryo navagvaiḥ
RV saraṇyubhiḥ phaligamindra śakra valaṃ raveṇadarayo daśagvaiḥ
RV gṛṇāno aṅgirobhirdasma vi varuṣasā sūryeṇa gobhirandhaḥ
RV vi bhūmyā aprathaya indra sānu divo raja uparamastabhāyaḥ
RV tadu prayakṣatamamasya karma dasmasya cārutamamasti daṃsaḥ
RV upahvare yaduparā apinvan madhvarṇaso nadyaścatasraḥ
RV dvitā vi vavre sanajā sanīḷe ayāsya stavamānebhirarkaiḥ
RV bhago na mene parame vyomannadhārayad rodasī sudaṃsāḥ
RV sanād divaṃ pari bhūmā virūpe punarbhuvā yuvatī svebhirevaiḥ
RV kṛṣṇebhiraktoṣā ruśadbhirvapurbhirā carato anyānyā
RV sanemi sakhyaṃ svapasyamānaḥ sūnurdādhāra śavasā sudaṃsāḥ
RV āmāsu cid dadhiṣe pakvamantaḥ payaḥ kṛṣṇāsu ruśad rohiṇīṣu
RV sanāt sanīlā avanīravātā vratā rakṣante amṛtāḥ sahobhiḥ
RV purū sahasrā janayo na patnīrduvasyanti svasāro ahrayāṇam
RV sanāyuvo namasā navyo arkairvasūyavo matayo dasma dadruḥ
RV patiṃ na patnīruśatīruśantaṃ spṛśanti tvā śavasāvanmanīṣāḥ
RV sanādeva tava rāyo gabhastau na kṣīyante nopa dasyanti dasma
RV dyumānasi kratumānindra dhīraḥ śikṣā śacīvastava naḥ śacībhiḥ
RV sanāyate gotama indra navyamatakṣad brahma hariyojanāya
RV sunīthāya naḥ śavasāna nodhāḥ prātar makṣū dhiyāvasur jagamyāt
RV tvaṃ mahānindra yo ha śuṣmairdyāvā jajñānaḥ pṛthivīame dhāḥ
RV yad dha te viśvā girayaścidabhvā bhiyā dṛḷhāsaḥ kiraṇā naijan
RV ā yad dharī indra vivratā verā te vajraṃ jaritā bāhvordhāt
RV yenāviharyatakrato amitrān pura iṣṇāsi puruhūta pūrvīḥ
RV tvaṃ satya indra dhṛṣṇuretān tvam ṛbhukṣā naryastvaṃṣāṭ
RV tvaṃ śuṣṇaṃ vṛjane pṛkṣa āṇau yūne kutsāyadyumate sacāhan
RV tvaṃ ha tyadindra codīḥ sakhā vṛtraṃ yad vajrin vṛṣakarmannubhnāḥ
RV yad dha śūra vṛṣamaṇaḥ parācairvi dasyūnryonāvakṛto vṛthāṣāṭ
RV tvaṃ ha tyadindrāriṣaṇyan dṛḷhasya cin martānāmajuṣṭau
RV vyasmadā kāṣṭhā arvate varghaneva vajriñchnathihyamitrān
RV tvāṃ ha tyadindrārṇasātau svarmīḷhe nara ājā havante
RV tava svadhāva iyamā samarya ūtirvājeṣvatasāyyā bhūt
RV tvaṃ ha tyadindra sapta yudhyan puro vajrin purukutsāya dardaḥ
RV barhirna yat sudāse vṛthā vargaṃho rājan varivaḥ pūrave kaḥ
RV tvaṃ tyāṃ na indra deva citrāmiṣamāpo na pīpayaḥ parijman
RV yayā śūra pratyasmabhyaṃ yaṃsi tmanamūrjaṃ na viśvadha kṣaradhyai
RV akāri ta indra gotamebhirbrahmāṇyoktā namasā haribhyām
RV supeśasaṃ vājamā bharā naḥ prātar makṣū dhiyāvasur jagamyāt
RV vṛṣṇe śardhāya sumakhāya vedhase nodhaḥ suvṛktiṃ pra bharā marudbhyaḥ
RV apo na dhīro manasā suhastyo giraḥ samañje vidatheṣvābhuvaḥ
RV te jajñire diva ṛṣvāsa ukṣaṇo rudrasya maryā asurā arepasaḥ
RV pāvakāsaḥ śucayaḥ sūryā iva satvāno na drapsinoghoravarpasaḥ
RV yuvāno rudrā ajarā abhogghano vavakṣuradhrigāvaḥ parvatā iva
RV dṛḷhā cid viśvā bhuvanāni pārthivā pra cyāvayantidivyāni majmanā
RV citrairañjibhirvapuṣe vyañjate vakṣassu rukmānadhi yetire śubhe
RV aṃseṣveṣāṃ ni mimṛkṣur ṛṣṭayaḥ sākaṃ jajñire svadhayā divo naraḥ
RV īśānakṛto dhunayo riśādaso vātān vidyutastaviṣībhirakrata
RV duhantyūdhardivyāni dhūtayo bhūmiṃ pinvanti payasāparijrayaḥ
RV pinvantyapo marutaḥ sudānavaḥ payo ghṛtavad vidatheṣvābhuvaḥ
RV atyaṃ na mihe vi nayanti vājinamutsaṃ duhanti stanayantamakṣitam
RV mahiṣāso māyinaścitrabhānavo girayo na svatavaso raghuṣyadaḥ
RV mṛgā iva hastinaḥ khādathā vanā yadāruṇīṣu taviṣīrayugdhvam
RV siṃhā iva nānadati pracetasaḥ piśā iva supiśo viśvavedasaḥ
RV kṣapo jinvantaḥ pṛṣatībhir ṛṣṭibhiḥ samit sabādhaḥ śavasāhimanyavaḥ
RV rodasī ā vadatā gaṇaśriyo nṛṣācaḥ śūrāḥ śavasāhimanyavaḥ
RV ā vandhureṣvamatirna darśatā vidyun na tasthau maruto ratheṣu vaḥ
RV viśvavedaso rayibhiḥ samokasaḥ sammiślāsastaviṣībhirvirapśinaḥ
RV astāra iṣuṃ dadhire gabhastyoranantaśuṣmā vṛṣakhādayo naraḥ
RV hiraṇyayebhiḥ pavibhiḥ payovṛdha ujjighnanta āpathyo na parvatān
RV makhā ayāsaḥ svasṛto dhruvacyuto dudhrakṛto maruto bhrājadṛṣṭayaḥ
RV ghṛṣuṃ pāvakaṃ vaninaṃ vicarṣaṇiṃ rudrasya sūnuṃ havasā gṛṇīmasi
RV rajasturaṃ tavasaṃ mārutaṃ gaṇam ṛjīṣiṇaṃvṛṣaṇaṃ saścata śriye
RV pra nū sa martaḥ śavasā janānati tasthau va ūtī maruto yamāvata
RV arvadbhirvajaṃ bharate dhanā nṛbhirāpṛchyaṃkratumā kṣeti puṣyati
RV carkṛtyaṃ marutaḥ pṛtsu duṣṭaraṃ dyumantaṃ śuṣmaṃ maghavatsu dhattana
RV dhanaspṛtamukthyaṃ viśvacarṣaṇiṃ tokaṃ puṣyema tanayaṃ śataṃ himaḥ
RV nū ṣṭhiraṃ maruto vīravantam ṛtīṣāhaṃ rayimasmāsu dhatta
RV sahasriṇaṃ śatinaṃ śūśuvāṃsaṃ prātar makṣū dhiyāvasur jagamyāt
RV paśvā na tāyuṃ guhā catantaṃ namo yujānaṃ namo vahantam
RV sajoṣā dhīrāḥ padairanu gmannupa tvā sīdan viśveyajatrāḥ
RV ṛtasya devā anu vratā gurbhuvat pariṣṭirdyaurna bhūma
RV vardhantīmāpaḥ panvā suśiśvim ṛtasya yonā garbhe sujātam
RV puṣṭirna raṇvā kṣitirna pṛthivī girirna bhujma kṣodo na śambhu
RV atyo nājman sargaprataktaḥ sindhurna kṣodaḥ ka īṃ varāte
RV jāmiḥ sindhūnāṃ bhrāteva svasrāmibhyān na rājā vanānyatti
RV yad vātajūto vanā vyasthādagnirha dāti romā pṛthivyāḥ
RV śvasityapsu haṃso na sīdan kratvā cetiṣṭho viśāmuṣarbhut
RV somo na vedhā ṛtaprajātaḥ paśurna śiśvā vibhurdūrebhāḥ
RV rayirna citrā sūro na sandṛgāyurna prāṇo nityo nasūnuḥ
RV takvā na bhūrṇirvanā siṣakti payo na dhenuḥ śucirvibhāvā
RV dādhāra kṣemamoko na raṇvo yavo na pakvo jetā janānām
RV ṛṣirna stubhvā vikṣu praśasto vājī na prīto vayodadhati
RV durokaśociḥ kraturna nityo jāyeva yonāvaraṃ viśvasmai
RV citro yadabhrāṭ chveto na vikṣu ratho na rukmī tveṣaḥ samatsu
RV seneva sṛṣṭāmaṃ dadhātyasturna didyut tveṣapratīkā
RV yamo ha jāto yamo janitvaṃ jāraḥ kanīnāṃ patirjanīnām
RV taṃ vaścarāthā vayaṃ vasatyāstaṃ na gāvo nakṣanta iddham
RV sindhurna kṣodaḥ pra nīcīrainon navanta gāvaḥ svardṛśīke
RV vaneṣu jāyurmarteṣu mitro vṛṇīte śruṣṭiṃ rājevājuryam
RV kṣemo na sādhuḥ kraturna bhadro bhuvat svādhirhotā havyavāṭ
RV haste dadhāno nṛmṇā viśvānyame devān dhād guhā niṣīdan
RV vidantīmatra naro dhiyandhā hṛdā yat taṣṭān mantrānaśaṃsan
RV ajo na kṣāṃ dādhāra pṛthivīṃ tastambha dyāṃ mantrebhiḥ satyaiḥ
RV priyā padāni paśvo ni pāhi viśvāyuragne guhā guhaṃ gāḥ
RV ya īṃ ciketa guhā bhavantamā yaḥ sasāda dhārām ṛtasya
RV vi ye cṛtanty ṛtā sapanta ādid vasūni pra vavācāsmai
RV vi yo vīrutsu rodhan mahitvota prajā uta prasūṣvantaḥ
RV cittirapāṃ dame viśvāyuḥ sadmeva dhīrāḥ sammāya cakruḥ
RV śrīṇannupa sthād divaṃ bhuraṇyu sthātuścarathamaktūnvyūrṇot
RV pari yadeṣāmeko viśveṣāṃ bhuvad devo devānāṃ mahitvā
RV ādit te viśve kratuṃ juṣanta śuṣkād yad deva jīvo janiṣṭhāḥ
RV bhajanta viśve devatvaṃ nāma ṛtaṃ sapanto amṛtamevaiḥ
RV ṛtasya preṣā ṛtasya dhītirviśvāyurviśve apāṃsi cakruḥ
RV yastubhyaṃ dāśād yo vā te śikṣāt tasmai cikitvānrayiṃ dayasva
RV hotā niṣatto manorapatye sa cin nvāsāṃ patī rayīṇām
RV ichanta reto mithastanūṣu saṃ jānata svairdakṣairamūrāḥ
RV piturna putrāḥ kratuṃ juṣanta śroṣan ye asya śāsaṃ turāsaḥ
RV vi rāya aurṇod duraḥ purukṣuḥ pipeśa nākaṃ stṛbhirdamūnāḥ
RV śukraḥ śuśukvānuṣo na jāraḥ paprā samīcī divo najyotiḥ
RV pari prajātaḥ kratvā babhūtha bhuvo devānāṃ pitā putraḥ san
RV vedhā adṛpto agnirvijānannūdharna gonāṃ svādmā pitūnām
RV jane na śeva āhūryaḥ san madhye niṣatto raṇvo duroṇe
RV putro na jāto raṇvo duroṇe vājī na prīto viśo vi tārīt
RV viśo yadahve nṛbhiḥ sanīḷā agnirdevatvā viśvānyaśyāḥ
RV nakiṣ ṭa etā vratā minanti nṛbhyo yadebhyaḥ śruṣṭiṃ cakartha
RV tat tu te daṃso yadahan samānairnṛbhiryad yukto vive rapāṃsi
RV uṣo na jāro vibhāvosraḥ saṃjñātarūpaściketadasmai
RV tmanā vahanto duro vy ṛṇvan navanta viśve svardṛśīke
RV vanema pūrvīraryo manīṣā agniḥ suśoko viśvānyaśyāḥ
RV ā daivyāni vratā cikitvānā mānuṣasya janasya janma
RV garbho yo apāṃ garbho vanānāṃ garbhaśca sthātāṃ garbhaścarathām
RV adrau cidasmā antarduroṇe viśāṃ na viśvo amṛtaḥ svādhīḥ
RV sa hi kṣapāvānagnī rayīṇāṃ dāśad yo asmā araṃ sūktaiḥ
RV etā cikitvo bhūmā ni pāhi devānāṃ janma martāṃśca vidvān
RV vardhān yaṃ pūrvīḥ kṣapo virūpā sthātuśca ratham ṛtapravītam
RV arādhi hotā svarniṣattaḥ kṛṇvan viśvānyapāṃsi satyā
RV goṣu praśastiṃ vaneṣu dhiṣe bharanta viśve baliṃ svarṇaḥ
RV vi tvā naraḥ purutrā saparyan piturna jivrervi vedobharanta
RV sādhurna gṛdhnurasteva śūro yāteva bhīmastveṣaḥ samatsu
RV upa pra jinvannuśatīruśantaṃ patiṃ na nityaṃ janayaḥ sanīḷāḥ
RV svasāraḥ śyāvīmaruṣīmajuṣrañcitramuchantīmuṣasaṃ na gāvaḥ
RV vīḷu cid dṛḷhā pitaro na ukthairadriṃ rujannaṅgiraso raveṇa
RV cakrurdivo bṛhato gātumasme ahaḥ svarvividuḥ ketumusrāḥ
RV dadhannṛtaṃ dhanayannasya dhītimādidaryo didhiṣvo vibhṛtrāḥ
RV atṛṣyantīrapaso yantyachā devāñ janma prayasā vardhayantīḥ
RV mathīd yadīṃ vibhṛto mātariśvā gṛhegṛhe śyeto jenyo bhūt
RV ādīṃ rājñe na sahīyase sacā sannā dūtyaṃ bhṛgavāṇo vivāya
RV mahe yat pitra īṃ rasaṃ dive karava tsarat pṛśanyaścikitvān
RV sṛjadastā dhṛṣatā didyumasmai svāyāṃ devo duhitari tviṣiṃ dhāt
RV sva ā yastubhyaṃ dama ā vibhāti namo vā dāśāduśato anu dyūn
RV vardho agne vayo asya dvibarhā yāsad rāyā sarathaṃ yaṃ junāsi
RV agniṃ viśvā abhi pṛkṣaḥ sacante samudraṃ na sravataḥ sapta yahvīḥ
RV na jāmibhirvi cikite vayo no vidā deveṣu pramatiṃ cikitvān
RV ā yadiṣe nṛpatiṃ teja ānaṭ chuci reto niṣiktaṃ dyaurabhīke
RV agniḥ śardhamanavadyaṃ yuvānaṃ svādhyaṃ janayat sūdayacca
RV mano na yo 'dhvanaḥ sadya etyekaḥ satrā sūro vasva īśe
RV rājānā mitrāvaruṇā supāṇī goṣu priyamamṛtaṃ rakṣamāṇā
RV mā no agne sakhyā pitryāṇi pra marṣiṣṭhā abhi viduṣ kaviḥ san
RV nabho na rūpaṃ jarimā mināti purā tasyā abhiśasteradhīhi
RV ni kāvyā vedhasaḥ śaśvatas karhaste dadhāno naryā purūṇi
RV agnirbhuvad rayipatī rayīṇāṃ satrā cakrāṇo amṛtāni viśvā
RV asme vatsaṃ pari ṣantaṃ na vindannichanto viśve amṛtā amūrāḥ
RV śramayuvaḥ padavyo dhiyandhāstasthuḥ pade paramecārvagneḥ
RV tisro yadagne śaradastvāmicchuciṃ ghṛtena śucayaḥ saparyān
RV nāmāni cid dadhire yajñiyānyasūdayanta tanvaḥ sujātāḥ
RV ā rodasī bṛhatī vevidānāḥ pra rudriyā jabhrire yajñiyāsaḥ
RV vidan marto nemadhitā cikitvānagniṃ pade parame tasthivāṃsam
RV saṃjānānā upa sīdannabhijñu patnīvanto namasyaṃ namasyan
RV ririkvāṃsastanvaḥ kṛṇvata svāḥ sakhā sakhyurnimiṣirakṣamāṇāḥ
RV triḥ sapta yad guhyāni tve it padāvidan nihitā yajñiyāsaḥ
RV tebhī rakṣante amṛtaṃ sajoṣāḥ paśūñca sthātṝñcarathaṃ ca pāhi
RV vidvānagne vayunāni kṣitīnāṃ vyānuṣak churudho jīvasedhāḥ
RV antarvidvānadhvano devayānānatandro dūto abhavo havirvāṭ
RV svādhyo diva ā sapta yahvī rāyo duro vy ṛtajñā ajānan
RV vidad gavyaṃ saramā dṛḷhamūrvaṃ yenā nu kaṃ mānuṣībhojate viṭ
RV ā ye viśvā svapatyāni tasthuḥ kṛṇvānāso amṛtatvāya gātum
RV mahnā mahadbhiḥ pṛthivī vi tasthe mātā putrairaditirdhāyase veḥ
RV adhi sriyaṃ ni dadhuścārumasmin divo yadakṣī amṛtā akṛṇvan
RV adha kṣaranti sindhavo na sṛṣṭāḥ pra nī cīragnearuṣīrajānan
RV rayirna yaḥ pitṛvitto vayodhāḥ supraṇītiścikituṣo naśāsuḥ
RV syonāśīratithirna prīṇāno hoteva sadma vidhato vi tārīt
RV devo na yaḥ savitā satyamanmā kratvā nipāti vṛjanāni viśvā
RV purupraśasto amatirna satya ātmeva śevo didhiṣāyyo bhūt
RV devo na yaḥ pṛthivīṃ viśvadhāyā upakṣeti hitamitro na rājā
RV puraḥsadaḥ śarmasado na vīrā anavadyā patijuṣṭeva nārī
RV taṃ tvā naro dama ā nityamiddhamagne sacanta kṣitiṣu dhruvāsu
RV adhi dyumnaṃ ni dadhurbhūryasmin bhavā viśvāyurdharuṇo rayīṇām
RV vi pṛkṣo agne maghavāno aśyurvi sūrayo dadato viśvamāyuḥ
RV sanema vājaṃ samitheṣvaryo bhāgaṃ deveṣu śravasedadhānāḥ
RV ṛtasya hi dhenavo vāvaśānāḥ smadūdhnīḥ pīpayanta dyubhaktāḥ
RV parāvataḥ sumatiṃ bhikṣamāṇā vi sindhavaḥ samayā sasruradrim
RV tve agne sumatiṃ bhikṣamāṇā divi śravo dadhire yajñiyāsaḥ
RV naktā ca cakruruṣasā virūpe kṛṣṇaṃ ca varṇamaruṇaṃ ca saṃ dhuḥ
RV yān rāye martān suṣūdo agne te syāma maghavāno vayaṃ ca
RV chāyeva viśvaṃ bhuvanaṃ sisakṣyāpaprivān rodasī antarikṣam
RV arvadbhiragne arvato nṛbhirnṝn vīrairvīrān vanuyāmā tvotāḥ
RV īśānāsaḥ pitṛvittasya rāyo vi sūrayaḥ śatahimā no aśyuḥ
RV etā te agna ucathāni vedho juṣṭāni santu manase hṛde ca
RV śakema rāyaḥ sudhuro yamaṃ te 'dhi śravo devabhaktaṃ dadhānāḥ
RV upaprayanto adhvaraṃ mantraṃ vocemāgnaye
RV āre asme ca śṛṇvate
RV yaḥ snīhitīṣu pūrvyaḥ saṃjagmānāsu kṛṣṭiṣu
RV arakṣad dāśuṣe gayam
RV uta bruvantu jantava udagnirvṛtrahājani
RV dhanaṃjayo raṇeraṇe
RV yasya dūto asi kṣaye veṣi havyāni vītaye
RV dasmat kṛṇoṣyadhvaram
RV tamit suhavyamaṅgiraḥ sudevaṃ sahaso yaho
RV janā āhuḥ subarhiṣam
RV ā ca vahāsi tāniha devānupa praśastaye
RV havyā suścandra vītaye
RV na yorupabdiraśvyaḥ śṛṇve rathasya kaccana
RV yadagneyāsi dūtyam
RV tvoto vājyahrayo 'bhi pūrvasmādaparaḥ
RV pra dāśvānagne asthāt
RV uta dyumat suvīryaṃ bṛhadagne vivāsasi
RV devebhyo deva dāśuṣe
RV juṣasva saprathastamaṃ vaco devapsarastamam
RV havyā juhvānaāsani
RV athā te aṅgirastamāgne vedhastama priyam
RV vocema brahma sānasi
RV kaste jāmirjanānāmagne ko dāśvadhvaraḥ
RV ko ha kasminnasi śritaḥ
RV tvaṃ jāmirjanānāmagne mitro asi priyaḥ
RV sakhā sakhibhya īḍyaḥ
RV yajā no mitrāvaruṇā yajā devān ṛtaṃ bṛhat
RV agne yakṣisvaṃ damam
RV kā ta upetirmanaso varāya bhuvadagne śantamā kā manīṣā
RV ko vā yajñaiḥ pari dakṣaṃ ta āpa kena vā te manasādāśema
RV ehyagna iha hotā ni ṣīdādabdhaḥ su puraetā bhavā naḥ
RV avatāṃ tvā rodasī viśvaminve yajā mahe saumanasāya devān
RV pra su viśvān rakṣaso dhakṣyagne bhavā yajñānāmabhiśastipāvā
RV athā vaha somapatiṃ haribhyāmātithyamasmai cakṛmā sudāvne
RV prajāvatā vacasā vahnirāsā ca huve ni ca satsīha devaiḥ
RV veṣi hotramuta potraṃ yajatra bodhi prayantarjanitarvasūnām
RV yathā viprasya manuṣo havirbhirdevānayajaḥ kavibhiḥ kaviḥ san
RV evā hotaḥ satyatara tvamadyāgne mandrayā juhvā yajasva
RV kathā dāśemāgnaye kāsmai devajuṣṭocyate bhāmine gīḥ
RV yo martyeṣvamṛta ṛtāvā hotā yajiṣṭha it kṛṇoti devān
RV yo adhvareṣu śantama ṛtāvā hotā tamū namobhirā kṛṇudhvam
RV agniryad vermartāya devān sa cā bodhāti manasāyajāti
RV sa hi kratuḥ sa maryaḥ sa sādhurmitro na bhūdadbhutasya rathīḥ
RV taṃ medheṣu prathamaṃ devayantīrviśa upa bruvate dasmamārīḥ
RV sa no nṛṇāṃ nṛtamo riśāda agnirgiro 'vasā vetu dhītim
RV tanā ca ye maghavānaḥ śaviṣṭha vājaprasūtā iṣayantamanma
RV evāgnirgotamebhirṛtāvā viprebhirastoṣṭa jātavedāḥ
RV sa eṣu dyumnaṃ pīpayat sa vājaṃ sa puṣṭiṃ yāti joṣamā cikitvān
RV abhi tvā gotamā girā jātavedo vicarṣaṇe
RV dyumnairabhi pra ṇonumaḥ
RV tamu tvā gotamo girā rāyaskāmo duvasyati
RV dyumnair

RV dyumnair

RV avocāma rahūgaṇā agnaye madhumad vacaḥ
RV dyumnair
RV hiraṇyakeśo rajaso visāre 'hirdhunirvāta iva dhrajīmān
RV śucibhrājā uṣaso navedā yaśasvatīrapasyuvo na satyāḥ
RV ā te suparṇā aminantamevaiḥ kṛṣṇo nonāva vṛṣabho yadīdam
RV śivābhirna smayamānābhirāgāt patanti mihaḥ stanayantyabhrā
RV yadīm ṛtasya payasā piyāno nayannṛtasya pathibhī rajiṣṭhaiḥ
RV aryamā mitro varunaḥ parijmā tvacaṃ pṛñcantyuparasya yonau
RV agne vājasya gomata īśānaḥ sahaso yaho
RV asme dhehi jātavedo mahi śravaḥ
RV sa idhano vasuṣ kaviragnirīḷenyo girā
RV revadasmabhyampurvaṇīka dīdihi
RV kṣapo rājannuta tmanāgne vastorutoṣasaḥ
RV sa tigmajambha rakṣaso daha prati
RV avā no agna ūtibhirgāyatrasya prabharmaṇi
RV viśvāsu dhīṣu vandya
RV ā no agne rayiṃ bhara satrāsāhaṃ vareṇyam
RV viśvāsu pṛtsuduṣṭaram
RV ā no agne sucetunā rayiṃ viśvāyupoṣasam
RV mārḍīkaṃ dhehi jīvase
RV pra pūtāstigmaśociṣe vāco gotamāgnaye
RV bharasva sumnayurgiraḥ
RV yo no agne 'bhidāsatyanti dūre padīṣṭa saḥ
RV asmākamid vṛdhe bhava
RV sahasrākṣo vicarṣaṇiragnī rakṣāṃsi sedhati
RV hotā gṛṇīta ukthyaḥ
RV itthā hi soma in made brahmā cakāra vardhanam
RV śaviṣṭha vajrinnojasā pṛthivyā niḥ śaśā ahimarcannanu svarājyam
RV sa tvāmadad vṛṣā madaḥ somaḥ śyenābhṛtaḥ sutaḥ
RV yenāvṛtraṃ niradbhyo jaghantha vajrinnojasārcann
RV prehyabhīhi dhṛṣṇuhi na te vajro ni yaṃsate
RV indra nṛmṇaṃ hi te śavo hano vṛtraṃ jayā apo 'rcann
RV nirindra bhūmyā adhi vṛtraṃ jaghantha nirdivaḥ
RV sṛjā marutvatīrava jīvadhanyā imā apo 'rcann
RV indro vṛtrasya dodhataḥ sānuṃ vajreṇa hīḷitaḥ
RV abhikramyāva jighnate 'paḥ sarmāya codayannarcann
RV adhi sānau ni jighnate vajreṇa śataparvaṇā
RV mandāna indro andhasaḥ sakhibhyo gātumichatyarcann
RV indra tubhyamidadrivo 'nuttaṃ vajrin vīryam
RV yad dha tyammāyinaṃ mṛgaṃ tamu tvaṃ māyayāvadhīrarcann
RV vi te vajrāso asthiran navatiṃ nāvyā anu
RV mahat ta indra vīryaṃ bāhvoste balaṃ hitamarcann
RV sahasraṃ sākamarcata pari ṣṭobhata viṃśatiḥ
RV śatainamanvanonavurindrāya brahmodyatamarcann
RV indro vṛtrasya taviṣīṃ nirahan sahasā sahaḥ
RV mahat tadasya pauṃsyaṃ vṛtraṃ jaghanvānasṛjadarcann
RV ime cit tava manyave vepete bhiyasā mahī
RV yadindra vajrinnojasā vṛtraṃ marutvānavadhīrarcann
RV na vepasā na tanyatendraṃ vṛtro vi bībhayat
RV abhyenaṃ vajra āyasaḥ sahasrabhṛṣṭirāyatārcann
RV yad vṛtraṃ tava caśaniṃ vajreṇa samayodhayaḥ
RV ahimindrajighāṃsato divi te badbadhe śavo 'rcann
RV abhiṣṭane te adrivo yat sthā jagacca rejate
RV tvaṣṭā cit tava manyava indra vevijyate bhiyārcann
RV nahi nu yādadhīmasīndraṃ ko vīryā paraḥ
RV tasmin nṛmṇamuta kratuṃ devā ojāṃsi saṃ dadhurarcann
RV yamatharva manuṣ pitā dadhyaṃ dhiyamatnata
RV tasmin brahmāṇi purvathendra ukthā samagmatārcann
RV indro madāya vāvṛdhe śavase vṛtrahā nṛbhiḥ
RV tamin mahatsvājiṣūtemarbhe havāmahe sa vājeṣu pra no 'viṣat
RV asi hi vīra senyo 'si bhūri parādadiḥ
RV asi dabhrasya cidvṛdho yajamānāya śikṣasi sunvate bhūri te vasu
RV yadudīrata ājayo dhṛṣṇave dhīyate dhanā
RV yukṣvā madacyutā harī kaṃ hanaḥ kaṃ vasau dadho 'smānindra vasau dadhaḥ
RV kratvāmahānanuṣvadhaṃ bhīma ā vāvṛdhe śavaḥ
RV śriyaṛṣva upākayorni śiprī harivān dadhe hastayorvajramāyasam
RV ā paprau pārthivaṃ rajo badbadhe rocanā divi
RV na tvāvānindra kaścana na jāto na janiṣyate 'ti viśvaṃ vavakṣitha
RV yo aryo martabhojanaṃ parādadāti dāśuṣe
RV indro asmabhyaṃśikṣatu vi bhajā bhūri te vasu bhakṣīya tava rādhasaḥ
RV mademade hi no dadiryūthā gavām ṛjukratuḥ
RV saṃ gṛbhāyapurū śatobhayāhastyā vasu śiśīhi rāya ā bhara
RV mādayasva sute sacā śavase śūra rādhase
RV vidmā hi tvāpurūvasumupa kāmān sasṛjmahe 'thā no 'vitā bhava
RV ete ta indra jantavo viśvaṃ puṣyanti vāryam
RV antarhi khyojanānāmaryo vedo adāśuṣāṃ teṣāṃ no veda ā bhara
RV upo ṣu śṛṇuhī giro maghavan mātathā iva
RV yadā naḥ sūnṛtāvataḥ kara ādarthayāsa id yojā nvindra te harī
RV akṣannamīmadanta hyava priyā adhūṣata
RV astoṣata svabhānavo viprā naviṣṭhayā matī yojā 
RV susandṛśaṃ tvā vayaṃ maghavan vandiṣīmahi
RV pra nūnaṃ pūrṇavandhura stuto yāhi vaśānanu yojā 
RV sa ghā taṃ vṛṣaṇaṃ rathamadhi tiṣṭhāti govidam
RV yaḥpātraṃ hāriyojanaṃ pūrṇamindra ciketati yojā 
RV yuktaste astu dakṣiṇa uta savyaḥ śatakrato
RV tena jāyāmupa priyāṃ mandāno yāhyandhaso yojā 
RV yunajmi te brahmaṇā keśinā harī upa pra yāhi dadhiṣe gabhastyoḥ
RV ut tvā sutāso rabhasā amandiṣuḥ pūṣaṇvān vajrin samu patnyāmadaḥ
RV aśvāvati prathamo goṣu gachati suprāvīrindra martyastavotibhiḥ
RV tamit pṛṇakṣi vasunā bhavīyasā sindhumāpo yathābhito vicetasaḥ
RV āpo na devīrupa yanti hotriyamavaḥ paśyanti vitataṃ yathā rajaḥ
RV prācairdevāsaḥ pra ṇayanti devayuṃ brahmapriyaṃ joṣayante varā iva
RV adhi dvayoradadhā ukthyaṃ vaco yatasrucā mithunā yā saparyataḥ
RV asaṃyatto vrate te kṣeti puṣyati bhadrā śaktiryajamānāya sunvate
RV ādaṅgirāḥ prathamaṃ dadhire vaya iddhāgnayaḥ śamyā yesukṛtyayā
RV sarvaṃ paṇeḥ samavindanta bhojanamaśvāvantaṃ gomantamā paśuṃ naraḥ
RV yajñairatharvā prathamaḥ pathastate tataḥ sūryo vratapāvena ājani
RV ā gā ājaduśanā kāvyaḥ sacā yamasya jātamamṛtaṃ yajāmahe
RV barhirvā yat svapatyāya vṛjyate 'rko vā ślokamāghoṣatedivi
RV grāvā yatra vadati kārurukthyastasyedindro abhipitveṣu raṇyati
RV asāvi soma indra te śaviṣṭha dhṛṣṇavā gahi
RV ā tvā pṛṇaktvindriyaṃ rajaḥ sūryo na raśmibhiḥ
RV indramid dharī vahato 'pratidhṛṣṭaśavasam
RV ṛṣīṇāṃ ca stutīrupa yajñaṃ ca mānuṣāṇām
RV ā tiṣṭha vṛtrahan rathaṃ yuktā te brahmaṇā harī
RV arvācīnaṃ su te mano grāvā kṛṇotu vagnunā
RV imamindra sutaṃ piba jyeṣṭhamamartyaṃ madam
RV śukrasya tvābhyakṣaran dhārā ṛtasya sādane
RV indrāya nūnamarcatokthāni ca bravītana
RV sutā amatsurindavo jyeṣṭhaṃ namasyatā sahaḥ
RV nakiṣ ṭvad rathītaro harī yadindra yachase
RV nakiṣ ṭvānu majmanā nakiḥ svaśva ānaśe
RV ya eka id vidayate vasu martāya dāśuṣe
RV īśāno apratiṣkuta indro aṅga
RV kadā martamarādhasaṃ padā kṣumpamiva sphurat
RV kadā naḥśuśravad gira indro aṅga
RV yaścid dhi tvā bahubhya ā sutāvānāvivāsati
RV ugraṃ tat patyate śava indro aṅga
RV svādoritthā viṣūvato madhvaḥ pibanti gauryaḥ
RV yā indreṇa sayāvarīrvṛṣṇā madanti śobhase vasvīranu svarājyam
RV tā asya pṛśanāyuvaḥ somaṃ śrīṇanti pṛśnayaḥ
RV priyā indrasya dhenavo vajraṃ hinvanti sāyakaṃ vasvīr
RV tā asya namasā sahaḥ saparyanti pracetasaḥ
RV vratānyasya saścire purūṇi pūrvacittaye vasvīr
RV indro dadhīco asthabhirvṛtrāṇyapratiṣkutaḥ
RV jaghāna navatīrnava
RV ichannaśvasya yacchiraḥ parvateṣvapaśritam
RV tad vidaccharyaṇāvati
RV atrāha goramanvata nāma tvaṣṭurapīcyam
RV itthā candramaso gṛhe
RV ko adya yuṅkte dhuri gā ṛtasya śimīvato bhāmino durhṛṇāyūn
RV asanniṣūn hṛtsvaso mayobhūn ya eṣāṃ bhṛtyām ṛṇadhat sa jīvāt
RV ka īṣate tujyate ko bibhāya ko maṃsate santamindraṃ ko anti
RV kastokāya ka ibhāyota rāye 'dhi bravat tanve ko janāya
RV ko agnimīṭṭe haviṣā ghṛtena srucā yajātā ṛtubhirdhruvebhiḥ
RV kasmai devā ā vahānāśu homa ko maṃsate vītihotraḥ sudevaḥ
RV tvamaṅga pra śaṃsiṣo devaḥ śaviṣṭha martyam
RV na tvadanyo maghavannasti marḍitendra bravīmi te vacaḥ
RV mā te rādhāṃsi mā ta ūtayo vaso 'smān kadā canā dabhan
RV viśvā ca na upamimīhi mānuṣa vasūni carṣaṇibhya ā
RV pra ye śumbhante janayo na saptayo yāman rudrasya sūnavaḥsudaṃsasaḥ
RV rodasī hi marutaścakrire vṛdhe madanti vīrā vidatheṣu ghṛṣvayaḥ
RV ta ukṣitāso mahimānamāśata divi rudrāso adhi cakrire sadaḥ
RV arcanto arkaṃ janayanta indriyamadhi śriyo dadhire pṛśnimātaraḥ
RV gomātaro yacchubhayante añjibhistanūṣu śubhrā dadhire virukmataḥ
RV bādhante viśvamabhimātinamapa vartmānyeṣāmanu rīyate ghṛtam
RV vi ye bhrājante sumakhāsa ṛṣṭibhiḥ pracyāvayanto acyutācidojasā
RV manojuvo yan maruto ratheṣvā vṛṣavrātāsaḥ pṛṣatīrayugdhvam
RV pra yad ratheṣu pṛṣatīrayugdhvaṃ vāje adriṃ maruto raṃhayantaḥ
RV utāruṣasya vi ṣyanti dhārāścarmevodabhirvyundanti bhūma
RV ā vo vahantu saptayo raghuṣyado raghupatvānaḥ pra jigāta bāhubhiḥ
RV sīdatā barhiruru vaḥ sadas kṛtaṃ mādayadhvaṃ maruto madhvo andhasaḥ
RV te 'vardhanta svatavaso mahitvanā nākaṃ tasthururu cakrire sadaḥ
RV viṣṇuryad dhāvad vṛṣaṇaṃ madacyutaṃ vayo na sīdannadhi barhiṣi priye
RV śūrā ived yuyudhayo na jagmayaḥ śravasyavo na pṛtanāsu yetire
RV bhayante viśvā bhuvanā marudbhyo rājāna iva tveṣasandṛśo naraḥ
RV tvaṣṭā yad vajraṃ sukṛtaṃ hiraṇyayaṃ sahasrabhṛṣṭiṃ svapā avartayat
RV dhatta indro naryapāṃsi kartave 'han vṛtraṃ nirapāmaubjadarṇavam
RV ūrdhvaṃ nunudre 'vataṃ ta ojasā dadṛhāṇaṃ cid bibhidurviparvatam
RV dhamanto vāṇaṃ marutaḥ sudānavo made somasya raṇyāni cakrire
RV jihmaṃ nunudre 'vataṃ tayā diśāsiñcannutsaṃ gotamāya tṛṣṇaje
RV ā gachantīmavasā citrabhānavaḥ kāmaṃ viprasyatarpayanta dhāmabhiḥ
RV yā vaḥ śarma śaśamānāya santi tridhātūni dāśuṣe yachatādhi
RV asmabhyaṃ tāni maruto vi yanta rayiṃ no dhatta vṛṣaṇaḥ suvīram
RV maruto yasya hi kṣaye pāthā divo vimahasaḥ
RV sa sugopātamo janaḥ
RV yajñairvā yajñavāhaso viprasya vā matīnām
RV marutaḥ śṛṇutā havam
RV uta vā yasya vājino 'nu vipramatakṣata
RV sa gantā gomativraje
RV asya vīrasya barhiṣi sutaḥ somo diviṣṭiṣu
RV ukthaṃ madaśca śasyate
RV asya śroṣantvā bhuvo viśvā yaścarṣaṇīrabhi
RV sūraṃ cit sasruṣīriṣaḥ
RV pūrvībhirhi dadāśima śaradbhirmaruto vayam
RV avobhiścarṣaṇīnām
RV subhagaḥ sa prayajyavo maruto astu martyaḥ
RV yasya prayāṃsiparṣatha
RV śaśamānasya vā naraḥ svedasya satyaśavasaḥ
RV vidā kāmasyavenataḥ
RV yūyaṃ tat satyaśavasa āviṣ karta mahitvanā
RV vidhyatā vidyutā rakṣaḥ
RV gūhatā guhyaṃ tamo vi yāta viśvamatriṇam
RV jyotiṣ kartā yaduśmasi
RV pratvakṣasaḥ pratavaso virapśino 'nānatā avithurā ṛjīṣiṇaḥ
RV juṣṭatamāso nṛtamāso añjibhirvyānajre ke cidusrā iva stṛbhiḥ
RV upahvareṣu yadacidhvaṃ yayiṃ vaya iva marutaḥ kena cit pathā
RV ścotanti kośā upa vo ratheṣvā ghṛtamukṣatā madhuvarṇamarcate
RV praiṣāmajmeṣu vithureva rejate bhūmiryāmeṣu yad dha yuñjate śubhe
RV te krīḷayo dhunayo bhrājadṛṣṭayaḥ svayaṃ mahitvaṃ panayanta dhūtayaḥ
RV sa hi svasṛt pṛṣadaśvo yuvā gaṇo 'yā īśānastaviṣībhirāvṛtaḥ
RV asi satya ṛṇayāvānedyo 'syā dhiyaḥ prāvitāthā vṛṣā gaṇaḥ
RV pituḥ pratnasya janmanā vadāmasi somasya jihvā pra jigāti cakṣasā
RV yadīmindraṃ śamy ṛkvāṇa āśatādin nāmāni yajñiyāni dadhire
RV śriyase kaṃ bhānubhiḥ saṃ mimikṣire te raśmibhista ṛkvabhiḥ sukhādayaḥ
RV te vāśīmanta iṣmiṇo abhīravo vidre priyasya mārutasya dhāmnaḥ
RV ā vidyunmadbhirmarutaḥ svarkai rathebhiryāta ṛṣṭimadbhiraśvaparṇaiḥ
RV ā varṣiṣṭhayā na iṣā vayo na paptatā sumāyāḥ
RV te 'ruṇebhirvaramā piśaṅgaiḥ śubhe kaṃ yānti rathatūrbhiraśvaiḥ
RV rukmo na citraḥ svadhitīvān pavyā rathasya jaṅghananta bhūma
RV śriye kaṃ vo adhi tanūṣu vāśīrmedhā vanā na kṛṇavanta ūrdhvā
RV yuṣmabhyaṃ kaṃ marutaḥ sujātāstuvidyumnāso dhanayante adrim
RV ahāni gṛdhrāḥ paryā va āgurimāṃ dhiyaṃ vārkāryāṃca devīm
RV brahma kṛṇvanto gotamāso arkairūrdhvaṃ nunudrautsadhiṃ pibadhyai
RV etat tyan na yojanamaceti sasvarha yan maruto gotamo vaḥ
RV paśyan hiraṇyacakrānayodaṃṣṭrān vidhāvato varāhūn
RV eṣā syā vo maruto 'nubhartrī prati ṣṭobhati vāghato na vāṇī
RV astobhayad vṛthāsāmanu svadhāṃ gabhastyoḥ
RV ā no bhadrāḥ kratavo xyantu viśvato 'dabdhāso aparītāsa udbhidaḥ
RV devā no yathā sadamid vṛdhe asannaprāyuvo rakṣitāro divedive
RV devānāṃ bhadrā sumatirṛjūyatāṃ devānāṃ rātirabhi noni vartatām
RV devānāṃ sakhyamupa sedimā vayaṃ devā na āyuḥ pra tirantu jīvase
RV tān pūrvayā nividā hūmahe vayaṃ bhagaṃ mitramaditiṃ dakṣamasridham
RV aryamaṇaṃ varuṇaṃ somamaśvinā sarasvatīnaḥ subhagā mayas karat
RV tan no vāto mayobhu vātu bheṣajaṃ tan mātā pṛthivī tatpitā dyauḥ
RV tad grāvāṇaḥ somasuto mayobhuvastadaśvinā śṛṇutaṃ dhiṣṇyā yuvam
RV tamīśānaṃ jagatastasthuṣas patiṃ dhiyaṃjinvamavase hūmahe vayam
RV pūṣā no yathā vedasāmasad vṛdhe rakṣitā pāyuradabdhaḥ svastaye
RV svasti na indro vṛddhaśravāḥ svasti naḥ puṣā viśvavedāḥ
RV svasti nastārkṣyo ariṣṭanemiḥ svasti no bṛhaspatirdadhātu
RV pṛṣadaśvā marutaḥ pṛśnimātaraḥ śubhaṃyāvāno vidatheṣujagmayaḥ
RV agnijihvā manavaḥ sūracakṣaso viśve no devā avasā gamanniha
RV bhadraṃ karṇebhiḥ śṛṇuyāma devā bhadraṃ paśyemākṣabhiryajatrāḥ
RV sthirairaṅgaistuṣṭuvāṃsastanūbhirvyaśemadevahitaṃ yadāyuḥ
RV śatamin nu śarado anti devā yatrā naścakrā jarasaṃ tanūnām
RV putrāso yatra pitaro bhavanti mā no madhyā rīriṣatāyurgantoḥ
RV aditirdyauraditirantarikṣamaditirmātā sa pitā sa putraḥ
RV viśve devā aditiḥ pañca janā aditirjātamaditirjanitvam
RV ṛjunītī no varuṇo mitro nayatu vidvān
RV aryamā devaiḥ sajoṣāḥ
RV te hi vasvo vasavānāste apramūrā mahobhiḥ
RV vratā rakṣante viśvāhā
RV te asmabhyaṃ śarma yaṃsannamṛtā martyebhyaḥ
RV bādhamānāapa dviṣaḥ
RV vi naḥ pathaḥ suvitāya ciyantvindro marutaḥ
RV pūṣā bhago vandyāsaḥ
RV uta no dhiyo goagrāḥ pūṣan viṣṇavevayāvaḥ
RV kartā naḥ svastimataḥ
RV madhu vātā ṛtāyate madhu kṣaranti sindhavaḥ
RV mādhvīrnaḥ santvoṣadhīḥ
RV madhu naktamutoṣaso madhumat pārthivaṃ rajaḥ
RV madhu dyaurastu naḥ pitā
RV madhumān no vanaspatirmadhumānastu sūryaḥ
RV mādhvīrgāvo bhavantu naḥ
RV śaṃ no mitraḥ śaṃ varuṇaḥ śaṃ no bhavatvaryamā
RV śaṃ na indro bṛhaspatiḥ śaṃ no viṣṇururukramaḥ
RV tvaṃ soma pra cikito manīṣā tvaṃ rajiṣṭhamanu neṣi panthām
RV tava praṇītī pitaro na indo deveṣu ratnamabhajanta dhīrāḥ
RV tvaṃ soma kratubhiḥ subhūstvaṃ dakṣaiḥ sudakṣo viśvavedāḥ
RV tvaṃ vṛṣā vṛṣatvebhirmahitvā dyumnebhirdyumnyabhavo nṛcakṣāḥ
RV rājño nu te varuṇasya vratāni bṛhad gabhīraṃ tava soma dhāma
RV śuciṣ ṭvamasi priyo na mitro dakṣāyyo aryamevāsisoma
RV yā te dhāmāni divi yā pṛthivyāṃ yā parvateṣvoṣadhīṣvapsu
RV tebhirno viśvaiḥ sumanā aheḷan rājan soma pratihavyā gṛbhāya
RV tvaṃ somāsi satpatistvaṃ rājota vṛtrahā
RV tvaṃ bhadro asi kratuḥ
RV tvaṃ ca soma no vaśo jīvātuṃ na marāmahe
RV priyastotro vanaspatiḥ
RV tvaṃ soma mahe bhagaṃ tvaṃ yūna ṛtāyate
RV dakṣaṃ dadhāsi jīvase
RV tvaṃ naḥ soma viśvato rakṣā rājannaghāyataḥ
RV na riṣyettvāvataḥ sakhā
RV soma yāste mayobhuva ūtayaḥ santi dāśuṣe
RV tābhirno 'vitā bhava
RV imaṃ yajñamidaṃ vaco jujuṣāṇa upāgahi
RV soma tvaṃ novṛdhe bhava
RV soma gīrbhiṣ ṭvā vayaṃ vardhayāmo vacovidaḥ
RV sumṛḷīkona ā viśa
RV gayasphāno amīvahā vasuvit puṣṭivardhanaḥ
RV sumitraḥ somano bhava
RV soma rārandhi no hṛdi gāvo na yavaseṣvā
RV marya iva svaokye
RV yaḥ soma sakhye tava rāraṇad deva martyaḥ
RV taṃ dakṣaḥ sacate kaviḥ
RV uruṣyā ṇo abhiśasteḥ soma ni pāhyaṃhasaḥ
RV sakhā suśeva edhi naḥ
RV ā pyāyasva sametu te viśvataḥ soma vṛṣṇyam
RV bhavā vājasya saṃgathe
RV ā pyāyasva madintama soma viśvebhiraṃśubhiḥ
RV bhavā naḥsuśravastamaḥ sakhā vṛdhe
RV saṃ te payāṃsi samu yantu vājāḥ saṃ vṛṣṇyānyabhimātiṣāhaḥ
RV āpyāyamāno amṛtāya soma divi śravāṃsyuttamāni dhiṣva
RV yā te dhāmāni haviṣā yajanti tā te viśvā paribhūrastuyajñam
RV gayasphānaḥ prataraṇaḥ suvīro 'vīrahā pra carā soma duryān
RV somo dhenuṃ somo arvantamāśuṃ somo vīraṃ karmaṇyaṃ dadāti
RV sādanyaṃ vidathyaṃ sabheyaṃ pitṛśravaṇaṃ yo dadāśadasmai
RV aṣāḷhaṃ yutsu pṛtanāsu papriṃ svarṣāmapsāṃ vṛjanasyagopām
RV bhareṣujāṃ sukṣitiṃ suśravasaṃ jayantaṃ tvāmanu madema soma
RV tvamimā oṣadhīḥ soma viśvāstvamapo ajanayastvaṃ gāḥ
RV tvamā tatanthorvantarikṣaṃ tvaṃ jyotiṣā vi tamo vavartha
RV devena no manasā deva soma rāyo bhāgaṃ sahasāvannabhi yudhya
RV mā tvā tanadīśiṣe vīryasyobhayebhyaḥ pra cikitsā gaviṣṭau
RV etā u tyā uṣasaḥ ketumakrata pūrve ardhe rajaso bhānumañjate
RV niṣkṛṇvānā āyudhānīva dhṛṣṇavaḥ prati gāvo'ruṣīryanti mātaraḥ
RV udapaptannaruṇā bhānavo vṛthā svāyujo aruṣīrgā ayuksata
RV akrannuṣāso vayunāni pūrvathā ruśantaṃ bhānumaruṣīraśiśrayuḥ
RV arcanti nārīrapaso na viṣṭibhiḥ samānena yojanenā parāvataḥ
RV iṣaṃ vahantīḥ sukṛte sudānave viśvedaha yajamānāya sunvate
RV adhi peśāṃsi vapate nṛtūrivāporṇute vakṣa usreva barjaham
RV jyotirviśvasmai bhuvanāya kṛṇvatī gāvo na vrajaṃ vyuṣā āvartamaḥ
RV pratyarcī ruśadasyā adarśi vi tiṣṭhate bādhate kṛṣṇamabhvam
RV svaruṃ na peśo vidatheṣvañjañcitraṃ divo duhitā bhānumaśret
RV atāriṣma tamasas pāramasyoṣā uchantī vayunā kṛṇoti
RV śriye chando na smayate vibhātī supratīkā saumanasāyājīgaḥ
RV bhāsvatī netrī sūnṛtānāṃ diva stave duhitā gotamebhiḥ
RV prajāvato nṛvato aśvabudhyānuṣo goagrānupa māsi vājān
RV uṣastamaśyāṃ yaśasaṃ suvīraṃ dāsapravargaṃ rayimaśvabudhyam
RV sudaṃsasā śravasā yā vibhāsi vājaprasūtā subhage bṛhantam
RV viśvāni devī bhuvanābhicakṣyā pratīcī cakṣururviyā vi bhāti
RV viśvaṃ jīvaṃ carase bodhayantī viśvasya vācamavidan manāyoḥ

RV uruvyacā jathara ā vṛṣasva piteva naḥ śṛṇuhi hūyamānaḥ
RV candramā apsvantarā suparṇo dhāvate divi
RV na vo hiraṇyanemayaḥ padaṃ vindanti vidyuto vittaṃ me asya rodasī
RV arthamid vā u arthina ā jāyā yuvate patim
RV tuñjāte vṛṣṇyaṃ payaḥ paridāya rasaṃ duhe vittam
RV mo ṣu deva adaḥ svarava pādi divas pari
RV mā somyasya śambhuvaḥ śūne bhūma kadā cana vittam
RV yajñaṃ pṛchāmyavamaṃ sa tad dūto vi vocati
RV kva ṛtaṃ pūrvyaṃ gataṃ kastad bibharti nūtano vi
RV amī ye devā sthana triṣvā rocane divaḥ
RV kad va ṛtaṃ kadanṛtaṃ kva pratnā va āhutirvi
RV kad va ṛtasya dharṇasi kad varuṇasya cakṣaṇam
RV kadaryamṇo mahas pathāti krāmema dūḍhyo vi
RV aham so asmi yaḥ purā sute vadāmi kāni cit
RV taṃ mā vyantyādhyo vṛko na tṛṣṇajaṃ mṛgaṃ vi
RV saṃ mā tapantyabhitaḥ sapatnīriva parśavaḥ
RV mūṣo na śiśnā vyadanti mādhya stotāraṃ te śatakrato vi
RV amī ye sapta raśmayastatrā me nābhirātatā
RV tritastad vedāptyaḥ sa jāmitvāya rebhati vi
RV amī ye pañcokṣaṇo madhye tasthurmaho divaḥ
RV devatrā nu pravācyaṃ sadhrīcīnā ni vāvṛturvi
RV suparṇā eta āsate madhya ārodhane divaḥ
RV te sedhanti patho vṛkaṃ tarantaṃ yahvatīrapo vi
RV navyaṃ tadukthyaṃ hitaṃ devāsaḥ supravācanam
RV ṛtamarṣanti sindhavaḥ satyaṃ tātāna sūryo vi
RV agne tava tyadukthyaṃ deveṣvastyāpyam
RV sa naḥ satto manuṣvadā devān yakṣi viduṣṭaro vi
RV satto hotā manuṣvadā devānachā viduṣṭaraḥ
RV agnirhavyā suṣūdati devo deveṣu medhiro vi
RV brahmā kṛṇoti varuṇo gātuvidaṃ tamīmahe
RV vyūrṇoti hṛdā matiṃ navyo jāyatām ṛtaṃ vi
RV asau yaḥ panthā ādityo divi pravācyaṃ kṛtaḥ
RV na sa devā atikrame taṃ martāso na paśyatha vi
RV tritaḥ kūpe 'vahito devān havata ūtaye
RV tacchuśrāva bṛhaspatiḥ kṛṇvannaṃhūraṇāduru vi
RV aruṇo mā sakṛd vṛkaḥ pathā yantaṃ dadarśa hi
RV ujjihīte nicāyyā taṣṭeva pṛṣṭyāmayī vi
RV enāṅgūṣeṇa vayamindravanto 'bhi ṣyāma vṛjane sarvavīrāḥ
RV tan no 
RV indraṃ mitraṃ varuṇamagnimūtaye mārutaṃ śardho aditiṃhavāmahe
RV rathaṃ na durgād vasavaḥ sudānavo viśvasmān noaṃhaso niṣ pipartana
RV ta ādityā ā gatā sarvatātaye bhūta devā vṛtratūryeṣu śambhuvaḥ
RV rathaṃ 
RV avantu naḥ pitaraḥ supravācanā uta devī devaputre ṛtāvṛdhā
RV rathaṃ 
RV narāśaṃsaṃ vājinaṃ vājayanniha kṣayadvīraṃ pūṣaṇaṃ sumnairīmahe
RV rathaṃ 
RV bṛhaspate sadamin naḥ sugaṃ kṛdhi śaṃ yoryat te manurhitaṃ tadīmahe
RV rathaṃ 
RV indraṃ kutso vṛtrahaṇaṃ śacīpatiṃ kāṭe nibāḷha ṛṣirahvadūtaye
RV rathaṃ 
RV devairno devyaditirni pātu devastrātā trāyatāmaprayuchan
RV tan no 
RV yajño devānāṃ pratyeti sumnamādityāso bhavatā mṛḷayantaḥ
RV ā vo 'rvācī sumatirvavṛtyādaṃhościd yā varivovittarāsat
RV upa no devā avasā gamantvaṅgirasāṃ sāmabhiḥ stūyamānāḥ
RV indra indriyairmaruto marudbhirādityairno aditiḥ śarma yaṃsat
RV tan na indrastad varuṇastadagnistadaryamā tat savitācano dhāt
RV tan no 
RV ya indrāgnī citratamo ratho vāmabhi viśvāni bhuvanāni caṣṭe
RV tenā yātaṃ sarathaṃ tasthivāṃsāthā somasya pibataṃ sutasya
RV yāvadidaṃ bhuvanaṃ viśvamastyuruvyacā varimatā gabhīram
RV tāvānayaṃ pātave somo astvaramindrāgnī manase yuvabhyām
RV cakrāthe hi sadhryaṃ nāma bhadraṃ sadhrīcīnā vṛtrahaṇāuta sthaḥ
RV tāvindrāgnī sadhryañcā niṣadyā vṛṣṇaḥ somasya vṛṣaṇā vṛṣethām
RV samiddheṣvagniṣvānajānā yatasrucā barhiru tistirāṇā
RV tīvraiḥ somaiḥ pariṣiktebhirarvāgendrāgnī saumanasāya yātam
RV yānīndrāgnī cakrathurvīryāṇi yāni rūpāṇyuta vṛṣṇyāni
RV yā vāṃ pratnāni sakhyā śivāni tebhiḥ somasya pibataṃ sutasya
RV yadabravaṃ prathamaṃ vāṃ vṛṇāno 'yaṃ somo asurairno vihavyaḥ
RV tāṃ satyāṃ śraddhāmabhyā hi yātamathā somasya pibataṃ sutasya
RV yadindrāgnī madathaḥ sve duroṇe yad brahmaṇi rājani vāyajatrā
RV ataḥ pari vṛṣaṇāvā hi yātamathā somasya pibataṃ sutasya
RV yadindrāgnī yaduṣu turvaśeṣu yad druhyuṣvanuṣu pūruṣu sthaḥ
RV ataḥ 
RV yadindrāgnī avamasyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ madhyamasyāṃ paramasyāmuta sthaḥ
RV ataḥ 
RV yadindrāgnī paramasyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ madhyamasyāmavamasyāmuta sthaḥ
RV ataḥ 
RV yadindrāgnī divi ṣṭho yat pṛthivyāṃ yat parvateṣvoṣadhīṣvapsu
RV ataḥ 
RV yadindrāgnī uditā sūryasya madhye divaḥ svadhayā mādayethe
RV ataḥ 
RV evendrāgnī papivāṃsā sutasya viśvāsmabhyaṃ saṃ jayatandhanāni
RV tan no 
RV vi hyakhyaṃ manasā vasya ichannindrāgnī jñāsa uta vā sajātān
RV nānyā yuvat pramatirasti mahyaṃ sa vāṃ dhiyaṃ vājayantīmatakṣam
RV aśravaṃ hi bhūridāvattarā vāṃ vijāmāturuta vā ghā syālāt
RV athā somasya prayatī yuvabhyāmindrāgnī stomaṃ janayāmi navyam
RV mā chedma raśmīnriti nādhamānāḥ pitṝṇāṃ śaktīranuyachamānāḥ
RV indrāgnibhyāṃ kaṃ vṛṣaṇo madanti tā hyadrī dhiṣaṇāyā upasthe
RV yuvābhyāṃ devī dhiṣaṇā madāyendrāgnī somamuśatī sunoti
RV tāvaśvinā bhadrahastā supāṇī ā dhāvataṃ madhunā pṛṅktamapsu
RV yuvāmindrāgnī vasuno vibhāge tavastamā śuśrava vṛtrahatye
RV tāvāsadyā barhiṣi yajñe asmin pra carṣaṇī mādayethāṃ sutasya
RV pra carṣaṇibhyaḥ pṛtanāhaveṣu pra pṛthivyā riricāthe divaśca
RV pra sindhubhyaḥ pra giribhyo mahitvā prendrāgnī viśvā bhuvanātyanyā
RV ā bharataṃ śikṣataṃ vajrabāhū asmānindrāgnī avataṃ śacībhiḥ
RV ime nu te raśmayaḥ sūryasya yebhiḥ sapitvaṃ pitaro na āsan
RV purandarā śikṣataṃ vajrahastāsmānindrāgnī avataṃ bhareṣu
RV tan no 
RV tataṃ me apastadu tāyate punaḥ svādiṣṭhā dhītirucathāya śasyate
RV ayaṃ samudra iha viśvadevyaḥ svāhākṛtasya samu tṛpṇuta ṛbhavaḥ
RV ābhogayaṃ pra yadichanta aitanāpākāḥ prāñco mama ke cidāpayaḥ
RV saudhanvanāsaścaritasya bhūmanāgachata saviturdāśuṣo gṛham
RV tat savitā vo 'mṛtatvāmāsuvadagohyaṃ yacchravayanta aitana
RV tyaṃ ciccamasamasurasya bhakṣaṇamekaṃ santamakṛṇutā caturvayam
RV viṣṭvī śamī taraṇitvena vāghato martāsaḥ santo amṛtatvamānaśuḥ
RV saudhanvanā ṛbhavaḥ sūracakṣasaḥ saṃvatsare samapṛcyanta dhītibhiḥ
RV kṣetramiva vi mamustejanenamekaṃ pātram ṛbhavo jehamānam
RV upastutā upamaṃ nādhamānā amartyeṣu śrava ichamānāḥ
RV ā manīṣāmantarikṣasya nṛbhyaḥ sruceva ghṛtaṃ juhavāma vidmanā
RV taraṇitvā ye piturasya saścira ṛbhavo vājamaruhan divo rajaḥ
RV ṛbhurna indraḥ śavasā navīyān ṛbhurvājebhirvasubhirvasurdadiḥ
RV yuṣmākaṃ devā avasāhani priye 'bhi tiṣṭhemapṛtsutīrasunvatām
RV niścarmaṇa ṛbhavo gāmapiṃśata saṃ vatsenāsṛjatā mātaraṃ punaḥ
RV saudhanvanāsaḥ svapasyayā naro jivrī yuvānā pitarākṛṇotana
RV vājebhirno vājasātāvaviḍḍhy ṛbhumānindra citramā darṣi rādhaḥ
RV tan no 
RV takṣan rathaṃ suvṛtaṃ vidamnāpasastakṣan harī indravāhā vṛṣaṇvasū
RV takṣan pitṛbhyām ṛbhavo yuvad vayastakṣanvatsāya mātaraṃ sacābhuvam
RV ā no yajñāya takṣata ṛbhumad vayaḥ kratve dakṣāya suprajāvatīmiṣam
RV yathā kṣayāma sarvavīrayā viśā tan naḥśardhāya dhāsathā svindriyam
