RV ā takṣata sātimasmabhyam ṛbhavaḥ sātiṃ rathāya sātimarvate naraḥ
RV sātiṃ no jaitrīṃ saṃ maheta viśvahā jāmimajāmiṃ pṛtanāsu sakṣaṇim
RV ṛbhukṣaṇamindramā huva ūtaya ṛbhūn vājān marutaḥ somapītaye
RV ubhā mitrāvaruṇā nūnamaśvinā te no hinvantu sātaye dhiye jiṣe
RV ṛbhurbharāya saṃ śiśātu sātiṃ samaryajid vājo asmānaviṣṭu
RV tan no 
RV īḷe dyāvāpṛthivī pūrvacittaye 'gniṃ gharmaṃ surucaṃ yāmanniṣṭaye
RV yābhirbhare kāramaṃśāya jinvathastābhirū ṣu ūtibhiraśvinā gatam
RV yuvordānāya subharā asaścato rathamā tasthurvacasaṃ na mantave
RV yābhirdhiyo 'vathaḥkarmanniṣṭaye tābhir
RV yuvaṃ tāsāṃ divyasya praśāsane viśāṃ kṣayatho amṛtasyamajmanā
RV yābhirdhenumasvaṃ pinvatho narā tābhir
RV yābhiḥ parijmā tanayasya majmanā dvimātā tūrṣu taraṇirvibhūṣati
RV yābhistrimanturabhavad vicakṣaṇastābhir 
RV yābhī rebhaṃ nivṛtaṃ sitamadbhya ud vandanamairayataṃ svardṛśe
RV yābhiḥ kaṇvaṃ pra siṣāsantamāvataṃ tābhir
RV yābhirantakaṃ jasamānamāraṇe bhujyaṃ yābhiravyathibhirjijinvathuḥ
RV yābhiḥ karkandhuṃ vayyaṃ ca jinvathastābhir
RV yābhiḥ śucantiṃ dhanasāṃ suṣaṃsadaṃ taptaṃ gharmamomyāvantamatraye
RV yābhiḥ pṛṣniguṃ purukutsamāvataṃ tābhir
RV yābhiḥ śacībhirvṛṣaṇā parāvṛjaṃ prāndhaṃ śroṇaṃ cakṣasa etave kṛthaḥ
RV yābhirvartikāṃ grasitāmamuñcatantābhir
RV yābhiḥ sindhuṃ madhumantamasaścataṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ yābhirajarāvajinvatam
RV yābhiḥ kutsaṃ śrutaryaṃ naryamāvataṃ tābhir
RV yābhirviśpalāṃ dhanasāmatharvyaṃ sahasramīḷha ājāvajinvatam
RV yābhirvaśamaśvyaṃ preṇimāvataṃ tābhir
RV yābhiḥ sudānū auśijāya vaṇije dīrghaśravase madhu kośoakṣarat
RV kakṣīvantaṃ stotāraṃ yābhirāvataṃ tābhir 
RV yābhī rasāṃ kṣodasodnaḥ pipinvathuranaśvaṃ yābhī rathamāvataṃ jiṣe
RV yābhistriśoka usriyā udājata tābhir
RV yābhiḥ sūryaṃ pariyāthaḥ parāvati mandhātāraṃ kṣaitrapatyeṣvāvatam
RV yābhirvipraṃ pra bharadvājamāvataṃ tābhir
RV yābhirmahāmatithigvaṃ kaśojuvaṃ divodāsaṃ śambarahatyaāvatam
RV yābhiḥ pūrbhidye trasadasyumāvataṃ tābhir
RV yābhirvamraṃ vipipānamupastutaṃ kaliṃ yābhirvittajāniṃ duvasyathaḥ
RV yābhirvyaśvamuta pṛthimāvataṃ tābhir
RV yābhirnarā śayave yābhiratraye yābhiḥ purā manave gātumīṣathuḥ
RV yābhiḥ śārīrājataṃ syūmaraśmaye tābhir
RV yābhiḥ paṭharvā jaṭharasya majmanāgnirnādīdeccita iddho ajmannā
RV yābhiḥ śaryātamavatho mahādhane tābhir 
RV yābhiraṅgiro manasā niraṇyatho 'graṃ gachatho vivare goarṇasaḥ
RV yābhirmanuṃ śūramiṣā samāvataṃ tābhir
RV yābhiḥ patnīrvimadāya nyūhathurā gha vā yābhiraruṇīraśikṣatam
RV yābhiḥ sudāsa ūhathuḥ sudevyaṃ tābhir
RV yābhiḥ śantātī bhavatho dadāśuṣe bhujyuṃ yābhiravatho yābhiradhrigum
RV omyāvatīṃ subharām ṛtastubhaṃ tābhir
RV yābhiḥ kṛśānumasane duvasyatho jave yābhiryūno arvantamāvatam
RV madhu priyaṃ bharatho yat saraḍbhyastābhir
RV yābhirnaraṃ goṣuyudhaṃ nṛṣāhye kṣetrasya sātā tanayasya jinvathaḥ
RV yābhī rathānavatho yābhirarvatastābhir
RV yābhiḥ kutsamārjuneyaṃ śatakratū pra turvītiṃ pra ca dabhītimāvatam
RV yābhirdhvasantiṃ puruṣantimāvataṃ tābhir
RV apnasvatīmaśvinā vācamasme kṛtaṃ no dasrā vṛṣaṇā manīṣām
RV adyūtye 'vase ni hvaye vāṃ vṛdhe ca no bhavataṃ vājasātau
RV dyubhiraktubhiḥ pari pātamasmānariṣṭebhiraśvinā saubhagebhiḥ
RV tan no 
RV idaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ jyotiṣāṃ jyotirāgāccitraḥ praketo ajaniṣṭa vibhvā
RV yathā prasūtā savituḥ savayamevā rātryuṣase yonimāraik
RV ruśadvatsā ruśatī śvetyāgādāraigu kṛṣṇā sadanānyasyāḥ
RV samānabandhū amṛte anucī dyāvā varṇaṃ carata āmināne
RV samāno adhvā svasroranantastamanyānyā carato devaśiṣṭe
RV na methete na tasthatuḥ sumeke naktoṣāsā samanasā virūpe
RV bhāsvatī netrī sūnṛtānāmaceti citrā vi duro na āvaḥ
RV prārpyā jagad vyu no rāyo akhyaduṣā ajīgarbhuvanāni viśvā
RV jihmaśye caritave maghonyābhogaya iṣṭaye rāya u tvam
RV dabhraṃ paśyadbhya urviyā vicakṣa uṣā
RV kṣatrāya tvaṃ śravase tvaṃ mahīyā iṣṭaye tvamarthamivatvamityai
RV visadṛśā jīvitābhipracakṣa uṣā 
RV eṣā divo duhitā pratyadarśi vyuchantī yuvatiḥ śukravāsāḥ
RV viśvasyeśānā pārthivasya vasva uṣo adyeha subhagevyucha
RV parāyatīnāmanveti pātha āyatīnāṃ prathamā śaśvatīnām
RV vyuchantī jīvamudīrayantyuṣā mṛtaṃ kaṃ cana bodhayantī
RV uṣo yadagniṃ samidhe cakartha vi yadāvaścakṣasā sūryasya
RV yan mānuṣān yakṣyamāṇānajīgastad deveṣu cakṛṣe bhadramapnaḥ
RV kiyātyā yat samayā bhavāti yā vyūṣuryāśca nūnaṃvyuchān
RV anu pūrvāḥ kṛpate vāvaśānā pradīdhyānā joṣamanyābhireti
RV īyuṣ ṭe ye pūrvatarāmapaśyan vyuchantīmuṣasaṃ martyāsaḥ
RV asmābhirū nu praticakṣyābhūdo te yanti ye aparīṣu paśyān
RV yāvayaddveṣā ṛtapā ṛtejāḥ sumnāvarī sūnṛtā īrayantī
RV sumaṅgalīrbibhratī devavītimihādyoṣaḥ śreṣṭhatamāvyucha
RV śaśvat puroṣā vyuvāsa devyatho adyedaṃ vyāvo maghonī
RV atho vyuchāduttarānanu dyūnajarāmṛtā carati svadhābhiḥ
RV vyañjibhirdiva ātāsvadyaudapa kṛṣṇāṃ nirṇijaṃ devyāvaḥ
RV prabodhayantyaruṇebhiraśvairoṣā yāti suyujā rathena
RV āvahantī poṣyā vāryāṇi citraṃ ketuṃ kṛṇute cekitānā
RV īyuṣīṇāmupamā śaśvatīnāṃ vibhātīnāṃ prathamoṣā vyaśvait
RV udīrdhvaṃ jīvo asurna āgādapa prāgāt tama ā jyotireti
RV āraik panthāṃ yātave sūryāyāganma yatra pratiranta āyuḥ
RV syūmanā vāca udiyarti vahni stavāno rebha uṣaso vibhātīḥ
RV adyā taducha gṛṇate maghonyasme āyurni didīhi prajāvat
RV yā gomatīruṣasaḥ sarvavīrā vyuchanti dāśuṣe martyāya
RV vāyoriva sūnṛtānāmudarke tā aśvadā aśnavat somasutvā
RV mātā devānāmaditeranīkaṃ yajñasya keturbṛhatī vi bhāhi
RV praśastikṛd brahmaṇe no vyuchā no jane janaya viśvavāre
RV yaccitramapna uṣaso vahantījānāya śaśamānāya bhadram
RV tan no 
RV imā rudrāya tavase kapardine kṣayadvīrāya pra bharāmahe matīḥ
RV yathā śamasad dvipade catuṣpade viśvaṃ puṣṭaṃgrāme asminnanāturam
RV mṛḷā no rudrota no mayas kṛdhi kṣayadvīrāya namasā vidhemate
RV yacchaṃ ca yośca manurāyeje pitā tadaśyāma tavarudra praṇītiṣu
RV aśyāma te sumatiṃ devayajyayā kṣayadvīrasya tava rudra mīḍhvaḥ
RV sumnāyannid viśo asmākamā carāriṣṭavīrā juhavāma te haviḥ
RV tveṣaṃ vayaṃ rudraṃ yajñasādhaṃ vaṅkuṃ kavimavase nihvayāmahe
RV āre asmad daivyaṃ heḷo asyatu sumatimid vayamasyā vṛṇīmahe
RV divo varāhamaruṣaṃ kapardinaṃ tveṣaṃ rūpaṃ namasā nihvayāmahe
RV haste bibhrad bheṣajā vāryāṇi śarma varma chardirasmabhyaṃ yaṃsat
RV idaṃ pitre marutāmucyate vacaḥ svādoḥ svādīyo rudrāya vardhanam
RV rāsvā ca no amṛta martabhojanaṃ tmane tokā
RV mā no mahāntamuta mā no arbhakaṃ mā na ukṣantamuta māna ukṣitam
RV mā no vadhīḥ pitaraṃ mota mātaraṃ mā naḥ priyāstanvo rudra rīriṣaḥ
RV mā nastoke tanaye mā na āyau mā no goṣu mā no aśveṣurīriṣaḥ
RV vīrān mā no rudra bhāmito vadhīrhaviṣmantaḥsadamit tvā havāmahe
RV upa te stomān paśupā ivākaraṃ rāsvā pitarmarutāṃ sumnamasme
RV bhadrā hi te sumatirmṛḷayattamāthā vayamava itte vṛṇīmahe
RV āre te goghnamuta pūruṣaghnaṃ kṣayadvīra sumnamasme teastu
RV mṛḷā ca no adhi ca brūhi devādhā ca naḥ śarma yachadvibarhāḥ
RV avocāma namo asmā avasyavaḥ śṛṇotu no havaṃ rudro marutvān
RV tan no 
RV citraṃ devānāmudagādanīkaṃ cakṣurmitrasya varuṇasyāgneḥ
RV āprā dyāvāpṛthivī antarikṣaṃ sūrya ātmā jagatastasthuṣaśca
RV sūryo devīmuṣasaṃ rocamānāṃ maryo na yoṣāmabhyeti paścāt
RV yatrā naro devayanto yugāni vitanvate prati bhadrāya bhadram
RV bhadrā aśvā haritaḥ sūryasya citrā etagvā anumādyāsaḥ
RV namasyanto diva ā pṛṣṭhamasthuḥ pari dyāvāpṛthivī yanti sadyaḥ
RV tat sūryasya devatvaṃ tan mahitvaṃ madhyā kartorvitataṃ saṃ jabhāra
RV yadedayukta haritaḥ sadhasthādād rātrī vāsastanute simasmai
RV tan mitrasya varuṇasyābhicakṣe sūryo rūpaṃ kṛṇute dyorupasthe
RV anantamanyad ruśadasya pājaḥ kṛṣṇamanyad dharitaḥ saṃ bharanti
RV adyā devā uditā sūryasya niraṃhasaḥ pipṛtā naravadyāt
RV tan no 
RV nāsatyābhyāṃ barhiriva pra vṛñje stomāniyarmyabhriyeva vātaḥ
RV yāvarbhagāya vimadāya jāyāṃ senājuvā nyūhatūrathena
RV vīḷupatmabhirāśuhemabhirvā devānāṃ vā jūtibhiḥ śāśadānā
RV tad rāsabho nāsatyā sahasramājā yamasya pradhane jigāya
RV tugro ha bhujyumaśvinodameghe rayiṃ na kaścin mamṛvānavāhāḥ
RV tamūhathurnaubhirātmanvatībhirantarikṣaprudbhirapodakābhiḥ
RV tisraḥ kṣapastrirahātivrajadbhirnāsatyā bhujyumūhathuḥ pataṃgaiḥ
RV samudrasya dhanvannārdrasya pāre tribhī rathaiḥ śatapadbhiḥ ṣaḷaśvaiḥ
RV anārambhaṇe tadavīrayethāmanāsthāne agrabhaṇe samudre
RV yadaśvinā ūhathurbhujyumastaṃ śatāritrāṃ nāvamātasthivāṃsam
RV yamaśvinā dadathuḥ śvetamaśvamaghāśvāya śaśvaditsvasti
RV tad vāṃ dātraṃ mahi kīrtenyaṃ bhūt paidvo vājīsadamid dhavyo aryaḥ
RV yuvaṃ narā stuvate pajriyāya kakṣīvate aradataṃ purandhim
RV kārotarācchaphādaśvasya vṛṣṇaḥ śataṃ kumbhānasiñcataṃ surāyāḥ
RV himenāgniṃ ghraṃsamavārayethāṃ pitumatīmūrjamasmā adhattam
RV ṛbīse atrimaśvināvanītamun ninyathuḥ sarvagaṇaṃ svasti
RV parāvataṃ nāsatyānudethāmuccābudhnaṃ cakrathurjihmabāram
RV kṣarannāpo na pāyanāya rāye sahasrāya tṛṣyate gotamasya
RV jujuruṣo nāsatyota vavriṃ prāmuñcataṃ drāpimiva cyavānāt
RV prātirataṃ jahitasyāyurdasrādit patimakṛṇutaṃ kanīnām
RV tad vāṃ narā śaṃsyaṃ rādhyaṃ cābhiṣṭiman nāsatyā varūtham
RV yad vidvāṃsā nidhimivāpagūḷhamud darśatādūpathurvandanāya
RV tad vāṃ narā sanaye daṃsa ugramāviṣ kṛṇomi tanyaturnavṛṣṭim
RV dadhyaṃ ha yan madhvātharvaṇo vāmaśvasya śīrṣṇā pra yadīmuvāca
RV ajohavīn nāsatyā karā vāṃ mahe yāman purubhujā purandhiḥ
RV śrutaṃ tacchāsuriva vadhrimatyā hiraṇyahastamaśvināvadattam
RV āsno vṛkasya vartikāmabhīke yuvaṃ narā nāsatyāmumuktam
RV uto kaviṃ purubhujā yuvaṃ ha kṛpamāṇamakṛṇutaṃ vicakṣe
RV caritraṃ hi verivāchedi parṇamājā khelasya paritakmyāyām
RV sadyo jaṅghāmāyasīṃ viśpalāyai dhane hite sartavepratyadhattam
RV śataṃ meṣān vṛkye cakṣadānam ṛjrāśvaṃ taṃ pitāndhaṃcakāra
RV tasmā akṣī nāsatyā vicakṣa ādhattaṃ dasrā bhiṣajāvanarvan
RV ā vāṃ rathaṃ duhitā sūryasya kārṣmevātiṣṭhadarvatājayantī
RV viśve devā anvamanyata hṛdbhiḥ samu śriyā nāsatyā sacethe
RV yadayātaṃ divodāsāya vartirbharadvājāyāśvinā hayantā
RV revaduvāha sacano ratho vāṃ vṛṣabhaśca śiṃśumāraśca yuktā
RV rayiṃ sukṣatraṃ svapatyamāyuḥ suvīryaṃ nāsatyā vahantā
RV ā jahnāvīṃ samanasopa vājaistrirahno bhāgaṃ dadhatīmayātam
RV pariviṣṭaṃ jāhuṣaṃ viśvataḥ sīṃ sugebhirnaktamūhathū rajobhiḥ
RV vibhindunā nāsatyā rathena vi parvatānajarayū ayātam
RV ekasyā vastorāvataṃ raṇāya vaśamaśvinā sanaye sahasrā
RV nirahataṃ duchunā indravantā pṛthuśravaso vṛṣaṇāvarātīḥ
RV śarasya cidārcatkasyāvatādā nīcāduccā cakrathuḥ pātave vāḥ
RV śayave cin nāsatyā śacībhirjasuraye staryaṃ pipyathurgām
RV avasyate stuvate kṛṣṇiyāya ṛjūyate nāsatyā śacībhiḥ
RV paśuṃ na naṣṭamiva darśanāya viṣṇāpvaṃ dadathurviśvakāya
RV daśa rātrīraśivenā nava dyūnavanaddhaṃ śnathitamapsvantaḥ
RV viprutaṃ rebhamudani pravṛktamun ninyathuḥ somamiva sruveṇa
RV pra vāṃ daṃsāṃsyaśvināvavocamasya patiḥ syāṃ sugavaḥ suvīraḥ
RV uta paśyannaśnuvan dīrghamāyurastamivejjarimāṇaṃ jagamyām
RV madhvaḥ somasyāśvinā madāya pratno hotā vivāsate vām
RV barhiṣmatī rātirviśritā gīriṣā yātaṃ nāsatyopa vājaiḥ
RV yo vāmaśvinā manaso javīyān rathaḥ svaśvo viśa ājigāti
RV yena gachathaḥ sukṛto duroṇaṃ tena narā vartirasmabhyaṃ yātam
RV ṛṣiṃ narāvaṃhasaḥ pāñcajanyam ṛbīsādatriṃ muñcatho gaṇena
RV minantā dasyoraśivasya māyā anupūrvaṃ vṛṣaṇā codayantā
RV aśvaṃ na gūḷhamaśvinā durevairṛṣiṃ narā vṛṣaṇā rebhamapsu
RV saṃ taṃ riṇītho viprutaṃ daṃsobhirna vāṃ jūryanti pūrvyā kṛtāni
RV suṣupvāṃsaṃ na nirṛterupasthe sūryaṃ na dasrā tamasi kṣiyantam
RV śubhe rukmaṃ na darśataṃ nikhātamudūpathuraśvinā vandanāya
RV tad vāṃ narā śaṃsyaṃ pajriyeṇa kakṣīvatā nāsatyā parijman
RV śaphādaśvasya vājino janāya śataṃ kumbhānasiñcataṃ madhūnām
RV yuvaṃ narā stuvate kṛṣṇiyāya viṣṇāpvaṃ dadathurviśvakāya
RV ghoṣāyai cit pitṛṣade durone patiṃ jūryantyā aśvināvadattam
RV yuvaṃ śyāvāya ruśatīmadattaṃ mahaḥ kṣoṇasyāśvinā kaṇvāya
RV pravācyaṃ tad vṛṣaṇā kṛtaṃ vāṃ yan nārṣadāyaśravo adhyadhattam
RV purū varpāṃsyaśvinā dadhānā ni pedava ūhathurāśumaśvam
RV sahasrasāṃ vājinamapratītamahihanaṃ śravasyaṃ tarutram
RV etāni vāṃ śravasyā sudānū brahmāṅgūṣaṃ sadanaṃ rodasyoḥ
RV yad vāṃ pajrāso aśvinā havante yātamiṣā ca viduṣe ca vājam
RV sūnormānenāśvinā gṛṇānā vājaṃ viprāya bhuraṇā radantā
RV agastye brahmaṇā vāvṛdhānā saṃ viśpalāṃ nāsatyāriṇītam
RV kuha yāntā suṣṭutiṃ kāvyasya divo napātā vṛṣaṇā śayutrā
RV hiraṇyasyeva kalaśaṃ nikhātamudūpathurdaśame aśvināhan
RV yuvaṃ cyavānamaśvinā jarantaṃ punaryuvānaṃ cakrathuḥ śacībhiḥ
RV yuvo rathaṃ duhitā sūryasya saha śriyā nāsatyāvṛṇīta
RV yuvaṃ tugrāya pūrvyebhirevaiḥ punarmanyāvabhavataṃ yuvānā
RV yuvaṃ bhujyumarṇaso niḥ samudrād vibhirūhathurṛjrebhiraśvaiḥ
RV ajohavīdaśvinā taugryo vāṃ proḷhaḥ samudramavyathirjaganvān
RV niṣ ṭamūhathuḥ suyujā rathena manojavasā vṛṣaṇāsvasti
RV ajohavīdaśvinā vartikā vāmāsno yat sīmamuñcataṃ vṛkasya
RV vi jayuṣā yayathuḥ sānvadrerjātaṃ viṣvāco ahataṃ viṣeṇa
RV śataṃ meṣān vṛkye māmahānaṃ tamaḥ praṇītamaśivena pitrā
RV ākṣī ṛjrāśve aśvināvadhattaṃ jyotirandhāya cakrathurvicakṣe
RV śunamandhāya bharamahvayat sā vṛkīraśvinā vṛṣaṇā nareti
RV jāraḥ kanīna iva cakṣadāna ṛjrāśvaḥ śatamekaṃca meṣān
RV mahī vāmūtiraśvinā mayobhūruta srāmaṃ dhiṣṇyā saṃriṇīthaḥ
RV athā yuvāmidahvayat purandhirāgachataṃ sīṃ vṛṣaṇāvavobhiḥ
RV adhenuṃ dasrā staryaṃ viṣakṭāmapinvataṃ śayave aśvināgām
RV yuvaṃ śacībhirvimadāya jāyāṃ nyūhathuḥ purumitrasya yoṣām
RV yavaṃ vṛkeṇāśvinā vapanteṣaṃ duhantā manuṣāya dasrā
RV abhi dasyuṃ bakureṇā dhamantoru jyotiścakrathurāryāya
RV ātharvaṇāyāśvinā dadhīce 'śvyaṃ śiraḥ pratyairayatam
RV sa vāṃ madhu pra vocad ṛtāyan tvāṣṭraṃ yad dasrāvapikakṣyaṃ vām
RV sadā kavī sumatimā cake vāṃ viśvā dhiyo aśvinā prāvataṃ me
RV asme rayiṃ nāsatyā bṛhantamapatyasācaṃ śrutyaṃ rarāthām
RV hiraṇyahastamaśvinā rarāṇā putraṃ narā vadhrimatyā adattam
RV tridhā ha śyāvamaśvinā vikastamujjīvasa airayataṃsudānū
RV etāni vāmaśvinā vīryāṇi pra pūrvyāṇyāyavo 'vocan
RV brahmakṛṇvanto vṛṣaṇā yuvabhyāṃ suvīrāso vidathamā vadema
RV ā vāṃ ratho aśvinā śyenapatvā sumṛḷīkaḥ svavān yātvarvāṃ
RV yo martyasya manaso javīyān trivandhuro vṛṣaṇā vātaraṃhāḥ
RV trivandhureṇa trivṛtā rathena tricakreṇa suvṛtā yātamarvāk
RV pinvataṃ gā jinvatamarvato no vardhayatamaśvinā vīramasme
RV pravadyāmanā suvṛtā rathena dasrāvimaṃ śṛṇutaṃ ślokamadreḥ
RV kimaṅga vāṃ pratyavartiṃ gamiṣṭhāhurviprāsoaśvinā purājāḥ
RV ā vāṃ śyenāso aśvinā vahantu rathe yuktāsa āśavaḥ pataṃgāḥ
RV ye apturo divyāso na gṛdhrā abhi prayo nāsatyā vahanti
RV ā vāṃ rathaṃ yuvatistiṣṭhadatra juṣṭvī narā duhitāsūryasya
RV pari vāmaśvā vapuṣaḥ pataṃgā vayo vahantvaruṣā abhīke
RV ud vandanamairataṃ daṃsanābhirud rebhaṃ dasrā vṛṣaṇā śacībhiḥ
RV niṣ ṭaugryaṃ pārayathaḥ samudrāt punaścyavānaṃ cakrathuryuvānam
RV yuvamatraye 'vanītāya taptamūrjamomānamaśvināvadhattam
RV yuvaṃ kaṇvāyāpiriptāya cakṣuḥ pratyadhattaṃ suṣṭutiṃ jujuṣāṇā
RV yuvaṃ dhenuṃ śayave nādhitāyāpinvatamaśvinā pūrvyāya
RV amuñcataṃ vartikāmaṃhaso niḥ prati jaṅghāṃ viśpalāyā adhattam
RV yuvaṃ śvetaṃ pedava indrajūtamahihanamaśvinādattamaśvam
RV johūtramaryo abhibhūtimugraṃ sahasrasāṃ vṛṣaṇaṃ vīḍvaṅgam
RV tā vāṃ narā svavase sujātā havāmahe aśvinā nādhamānāḥ
RV ā na upa vasumatā rathena giro jusānā suvitāya yātam
RV ā śyenasya javasā nūtanenāsme yātaṃ nāsatyā sajoṣāḥ
RV have hi vāmaśvinā rātahavyaḥ śaśvattamāyā uṣaso vyuṣṭau
RV ā vāṃ rathaṃ purumāyaṃ manojuvaṃ jīrāśvaṃ yajñiyaṃ jīvase huve
RV sahasraketuṃ vaninaṃ śatadvasuṃ śruṣṭīvānaṃ varivodhāmabhi prayaḥ
RV ūrdhvā dhītiḥ pratyasya prayāmanyadhāyi śasman samayanta ā diśaḥ
RV svadāmi gharmaṃ prati yantyūtaya ā vāmūrjānī rathamaśvināruhat
RV saṃ yan mithaḥ paspṛdhānāso agmata śubhe makhā amitā jāyavo raṇe
RV yuvoraha pravaṇe cekite ratho yadaśvinā vahathaḥ sūrimā varam
RV yuvaṃ bhujyuṃ bhuramāṇaṃ vibhirgataṃ svayuktibhirnivahantā pitṛbhya ā
RV yāsiṣṭaṃ vartirvṛṣaṇā vijenyaṃ divodāsāya mahi ceti vāmavaḥ
RV yuvoraśvinā vapuṣe yuvāyujaṃ rathaṃ vāṇī yematurasya śardhyam
RV ā vāṃ patitvaṃ sakhyāya jagmuṣī yoṣāvṛṇītajenyā yuvāṃ patī
RV yuvaṃ rebhaṃ pariṣūteruruṣyatho himena gharmaṃ paritaptamatraye
RV yuvaṃ śayoravasaṃ pipyathurgavi pra dīrgheṇa vandanastāryāyuṣā
RV yuvaṃ vandanaṃ nirṛtaṃ jaraṇyayā rathaṃ na dasrā karaṇā saminvathaḥ
RV kṣetrādā vipraṃ janatho vipanyayā pra vāmatra vidhate daṃsanā bhuvat
RV agachataṃ kṛpamāṇaṃ parāvati pituḥ svasya tyajasā nibādhitam
RV svarvatīrita ūtīryuvoraha citrā abhīke abhavannabhiṣṭayaḥ
RV uta syā vāṃ madhuman makṣikārapan made somasyauśijo huvanyati
RV yuvaṃ dadhīco mana ā vivāsatho 'thā śiraḥ prati vāmaśvyaṃ vadat
RV yuvaṃ pedave puruvāramaśvinā spṛdhāṃ śvetaṃ tarutāranduvasyathaḥ
RV śaryairabhidyuṃ pṛtanāsu duṣṭaraṃ carkṛtyamindramiva carṣaṇīsaham
RV kā rādhad dhotrāśvinā vāṃ ko vāṃ joṣa ubhayoḥ
RV kathā vidhātyapracetāḥ
RV vidvāṃsāvid duraḥ pṛchedavidvānitthāparo acetāḥ
RV nū cin nu marte akrau
RV tā vidvāṃsā havāmahe vāṃ tā no vidvāṃsā manma vocetamadya
RV prārcad dayamāno yuvākuḥ
RV vi pṛchāmi pākyā na devān vaṣaṭkṛtasyādbhutasya dasrā
RV pātaṃ ca sahyaso yuvaṃ ca rabhyaso naḥ
RV pra yā ghoṣe bhṛgavāṇe na śobhe yayā vācā yajati pajriyo vām
RV praiṣayurna vidvān
RV śrutaṃ gāyatraṃ takavānasyāhaṃ cid dhi rirebhāśvinā vām
RV ākṣī śubhas patī dan
RV yuvaṃ hyāstaṃ maho ran yuvaṃ vā yan niratataṃsatam
RV tāno vasū sugopā syātaṃ pātaṃ no vṛkādaghāyoḥ
RV mā kasmai dhātamabhyamitriṇe no mākutrā no gṛhebhyo dhenavo guḥ
RV stanābhujo aśiśvīḥ
RV duhīyan mitradhitaye yuvāku rāye ca no mimītaṃ vājavatyai
RV iṣe ca no mimītaṃ dhenumatyai
RV aśvinorasanaṃ rathamanaśvaṃ vājināvatoḥ
RV tenāhaṃ bhūri cākana
RV ayaṃ samaha mā tanūhyāte janānanu
RV somapeyaṃ sukho rathaḥ
RV adha svapnasya nirvide 'bhuñjataśca revataḥ
RV ubhā tā basri naśyataḥ
RV kaditthā nṝnḥ pātraṃ devayatāṃ śravad giro aṅgirasāṃ turaṇyan
RV pra yadānaḍ viśa ā harmyasyoru kraṃsate adhvare yajatraḥ
RV stambhīd dha dyāṃ sa dharuṇaṃ pruṣāyad ṛbhurvājāya draviṇaṃ naro goḥ
RV anu svājāṃ mahiṣaścakṣata vrāṃ menāmaśvasya pari mātaraṃ goḥ
RV nakṣad dhavamaruṇīḥ pūrvyaṃ rāṭ turo viśāmaṅgirasāmanu dyūn
RV takṣad vajraṃ niyutaṃ tastambhad dyāṃ catuṣpade naryāya dvipāde
RV asya made svaryaṃ dā ṛtāyāpīvṛtamusriyāṇāmanīkam
RV yad dha prasarge trikakuṃ nivartadapa druho mānuṣasya duro vaḥ
RV tubhyaṃ payo yat pitarāvanītāṃ rādhaḥ suretasturaṇe bhuraṇyū
RV śuci yat te rekṇa āyajanta sabardughāyāḥ payausriyāyāḥ
RV adha pra jajñe taraṇirmamattu pra rocyasyā uṣaso na sūraḥ
RV induryebhirāṣṭa sveduhavyaiḥ sruveṇa siñcañ jaraṇābhi dhāma
RV svidhmā yad vanadhitirapasyāt sūro adhvare pari rodhanā goḥ
RV yad dha prabhāsi kṛtvyānanu dyūnanarviśe paśviṣeturāya
RV aṣṭā maho diva ādo harī iha dyumnāsāhamabhi yodhānautsam
RV hariṃ yat te mandinaṃ dukṣan vṛdhe gorabhasamadribhirvātāpyam
RV tvamāyasaṃ prati vartayo gordivo aśmānamupanītam ṛbhvā
RV kutsāya yatra puruhūta vanvañchuṣṇamanantaiḥ pariyāsi vadhaiḥ
RV purā yat sūrastamaso apītestamadrivaḥ phaligaṃ hetimasya
RV śuṣṇasya cit parihitaṃ yadojo divas pari sugrathitaṃ tadādaḥ
RV anu tvā mahī pājasī acakre dyāvākṣāmā madatāmindra karman
RV tvaṃ vṛtramāśayānaṃ sirāsu maho vajreṇa siṣvapovarāhum
RV tvamindra naryo yānavo nṝn tiṣṭhā vātasya suyujo vahiṣṭhān
RV yaṃ te kāvya uśanā mandinaṃ dād vṛtrahaṇaṃ pāryaṃ tatakṣa vajram
RV tvaṃ sūro harito rāmayo nṝn bharaccakrametaśo nāyamindra
RV prāsya pāraṃ navatiṃ nāvyānāmapi kartamavartayo'yajyūn
RV tvaṃ no asyā indra durhaṇāyāḥ pāhi vajrivo duritādabhīke
RV pra no vājān rathyo aśvabudhyāniṣe yandhi śravase sūnṛtāyai
RV mā sā te asmat sumatirvi dasad vājapramahaḥ samiṣo varanta
RV ā no bhaja maghavan goṣvaryo maṃhiṣṭhāste sadhamādaḥ syāma
RV pra vaḥ pāntaṃ raghumanyavo 'ndho yajñaṃ rudrāya mīḷhuṣe bharadvam
RV divo astoṣyasurasya vīrairiṣudhyeva maruto rodasyoḥ
RV patnīva pūrvahūtiṃ vāvṛdhadhyā uṣāsānaktā purudhā vidāne
RV starīr nātkaṃ vyutaṃ vasānā sūryasya śriyā sudṛśī hiraṇyaiḥ
RV mamattu naḥ parijmā vasarhā mamattu vāto apāṃ vṛṣaṇvān
RV śiśītamindrāparvatā yuvaṃ nastan no viśve varivasyantudevāḥ
RV uta tyā me yaśasā śvetanāyai vyantā pāntauśijo huvadhyai
RV pra vo napātamapāṃ kṛṇudhvaṃ pra mātarā rāspinasyāyoḥ
RV ā vo ruvaṇyumauśijo huvadhyai ghoṣeva śaṃsamarjunasya naṃśe
RV pra vaḥ pūṣṇe dāvana ānachā voceya vasutātimagneḥ
RV śrutaṃ me mitrāvaruṇā havemota śrutaṃ sadane viśvataḥ sīm
RV śrotu naḥ śroturātiḥ suśrotuḥ sukṣetrā sindhuradbhiḥ
RV stuṣe sā vāṃ varuṇa mitra rātirgavāṃ śatā pṛkṣayāmeṣu pajre
RV śrutarathe priyarathe dadhānāḥ sadyaḥ puṣṭiṃnirundhānāso agman
RV asya stuṣe mahimaghasya rādhaḥ sacā sanema nahuṣaḥ suvīrāḥ
RV jano yaḥ pajrebhyo vājinīvānaśvāvato rathino mahyaṃ sūriḥ
RV jano yo mitrāvaruṇāvabhidhrugapo na vāṃ sunotyakṣṇayādhruk
RV svayaṃ sa yakṣmaṃ hṛdaye ni dhatta āpa yadīṃ hotrābhirṛtāvā
RV sa vrādhato nahuṣo daṃsujūtaḥ śardhastaro narāṃ gūrtaśravāḥ
RV visṛṣṭarātiryāti bāḷhasṛtvā viśvāsu pṛtsu sadamicchūraḥ
RV adha gmantā nahuṣo havaṃ sūreḥ śrotā rājāno amṛtasya mandrāḥ
RV nabhojuvo yan niravasya rādhaḥ praśastaye mahinārathavate
RV etaṃ śardhaṃ dhāma yasya sūrerityavocan daśatayasya naṃśe
RV dyumnāni yeṣu vasutātī rāran viśve sanvantu prabhṛtheṣu vājam
RV mandāmahe daśatayasya dhāserdviryat pañca bibhrato yantyannā
RV kimiṣṭāśva iṣṭaraśmireta īśānāsastaruṣaṛñjate nṝn
RV hiraṇyakarṇaṃ maṇigrīvamarṇastan no viśve varivasyantu devāḥ
RV aryo giraḥ sadya ā jagmuṣīrosrāścākantūbhayeṣvasme
RV catvāro mā maśarśārasya śiśvastrayo rājña āyavasasyajiṣṇoḥ
RV ratho vāṃ mitrāvaruṇā dīrghāpsāḥ syūmagabhastiḥ sūro nādyaut
RV pṛthū ratho dakṣiṇāyā ayojyainaṃ devāso amṛtāso asthuḥ
RV kṛṣṇādudasthādaryā vihāyāścikitsantī mānuṣāyakṣayāya
RV pūrvā viśvasmād bhuvanādabodhi jayantī vājaṃ bṛhatī sanutrī
RV uccā vyakhyad yuvatiḥ punarbhūroṣā agan prathamā pūrvahūtau
RV yadadya bhāgaṃ vibhajāsi nṛbhya uṣo devi martyatrā sujāte
RV devo no atra savitā damūnā anāgaso vocati sūryāya
RV gṛhaṃgṛhamahanā yātyachā divedive adhi nāmā dadhānā
RV siṣāsantī dyotanā śaśvadāgādagramagramid bhajatevasūnām
RV bhagasya svasā varuṇasya jāmiruṣaḥ sūnṛte prathamā jarasva
RV paścā sa daghyā yo aghasya dhātā jayema taṃ dakṣiṇayā rathena
RV udīratāṃ sūnṛtā ut purandhīrudagnayaḥ śuśucānāsoasthuḥ
RV spārhā vasūni tamasāpagūḷhāviṣ kṛṇvantyuṣaso vibhātīḥ
RV apānyadetyabhyanyadeti viṣurūpe ahanī saṃ carete
RV parikṣitostamo anyā guhākaradyauduṣāḥ śośucatā rathena
RV sadṛśīradya sadṛśīridu śvo dīrghaṃ sacante varuṇasyadhāma
RV anavadyāstriṃśataṃ yojanānyekaikā kratuṃ pariyanti sadyaḥ
RV jānatyahnaḥ prathamasya nāma śukrā kṛṣṇādajaniṣṭa śvitīcī
RV ṛtasya yoṣā na mināti dhāmāhar aharniṣkṛtamācarantī
RV kanyeva tanvā śāśadānāneṣi devi devamiyakṣamāṇam
RV saṃsmayamānā yuvatiḥ purastādāvirvakṣāṃsi kṛṇuṣe vibhātī
RV susaṃkāśā mātṛmṛṣṭeva yoṣāvistanvaṃ kṛṇuṣe dṛśe kam
RV bhadrā tvamuṣo vitaraṃ vyucha na tat te anyā uṣasonaśanta
RV aśvāvatīrgomatīrviśvavārā yatamānā raśmibhiḥ sūryasya
RV parā ca yanti punarā ca yanti bhadrā nāma vahamānāuṣāsaḥ
RV ṛtasya raśmimanuyachamānā bhadrambhadraṃ kratumasmāsu dhehi
RV uṣo no adya suhavā vyuchāsmāsu rāyo maghavatsu ca syuḥ
RV uṣā uchantī samidhāne agnā udyan sūrya urviyā jyotiraśret
RV devo no atra savitā nvarthaṃ prāsāvīd dvipat pra catuṣpadityai
RV aminatī daivyāni vratāni praminatī manuṣyā yugāni
RV īyuṣīṇāmupamā śaśvatīnāmāyatīnāṃ prathamoṣā vyadyaut
RV eṣā divo duhitā pratyadarśi jyotirvasānā samanā purastāt
RV ṛtasya panthāmanveti sādhu prajānatīva na diśo mināti
RV upo adarśi śundhyuvo na vakṣo nodhā ivāvirakṛta priyāṇi
RV admasan na sasato bodhayantī śaśvattamāgāt punareyuṣīṇām
RV pūrve ardhe rajaso aptyasya gavāṃ janitryakṛta pra ketum
RV vyu prathate vitaraṃ varīya obhā pṛṇantī pitrorupasthā
RV evedeṣā purutamā dṛśe kaṃ nājāmiṃ na pari vṛṇakti jāmim
RV arepasā tanvā śāśadānā nārbhādīṣate na mahovibhātī
RV abhrāteva puṃsa eti pratīcī gartārugiva sanaye dhanānām
RV jāyeya patya uśatī suvāsā uṣā hasreva ni riṇīte apsaḥ
RV svasā svasre jyāyasyai yonimāraigapaityasyāḥ praticakṣyeva
RV vyuchantī raśmibhiḥ sūryasyāñjyaṅkte samanagā ivavrāḥ
RV āsāṃ pūrvāsāmahasu svasṝṇāmaparā pūrvāmabhyeti paścāt
RV tāḥ pratnavan navyasīrnūnamasme revaduchantu sudinā uṣāsaḥ
RV pra bodhayoṣaḥ pṛṇato maghonyabudhyamānāḥ paṇayaḥ sasantu
RV revaducha maghavadbhyo maghoni revat stotre sūnṛte jārayantī
RV aveyamaśvaid yuvatiḥ purastād yuṅkte gavāmaruṇānāmanīkam
RV vi nūnamuchādasati pra keturgṛhaṃgṛhamupa tiṣṭhāte agniḥ
RV ut te vayaścid vasaterapaptan naraśca ye pitubhājo vyuṣṭau
RV amā sate vahasi bhūri vāmamuṣo devi dāśuṣe martyāya
RV astoḍhvaṃ stomyā brahmaṇā me 'vīvṛdhadhvamuśatīruṣāsaḥ
RV yuṣmākaṃ devīravasā sanema sahasriṇaṃ ca śatinaṃ cavājam
RV prātā ratnaṃ prātaritvā dadhāti taṃ cikitvān pratigṛhyāni dhatte
RV tena prajāṃ vardhayamāna āyū rāyas poṣeṇa sacate suvīraḥ
RV sugurasat suhiraṇyaḥ svaśvo bṛhadasmai vaya indro dadhāti
RV yastvāyantaṃ vasunā prātaritvo mukṣījayeva padimutsināti
RV āyamadya sukṛtaṃ prātarichanniṣṭeḥ putraṃ vasumatā rathena
RV aṃśoḥ sutaṃ pāyaya matsarasya kṣayadvīraṃ vardhaya sūnṛtābhiḥ
RV upa kṣaranti sindhavo mayobhuva ījānaṃ ca yakṣyamāṇaṃ cadhenavaḥ
RV pṛṇantaṃ ca papuriṃ ca śravasyavo ghṛtasya dhārā upa yanti viśvataḥ
RV nākasya pṛṣṭhe adhi tiṣṭhati śrito yaḥ pṛṇāti sa ha deveṣu gachati
RV tasmā āpo ghṛtamarṣanti sindhavastasmā iyaṃ dakṣiṇā pinvate sadā
RV dakṣiṇāvatāmidimāni citrā dakṣiṇāvatāṃ divi sūryāsaḥ
RV dakṣiṇāvanto amṛtaṃ bhajante dakṣiṇāvantaḥ pra tiranta āyuḥ
RV mā pṛṇanto duritamena āran mā jāriṣuḥ sūrayaḥ suvratāsaḥ
RV anyasteṣāṃ paridhirastu kaścidapṛṇantamabhi saṃ yantu śokāḥ
RV amandān stomān pra bhare manīṣā sindhāvadhi kṣiyato bhāvyasya
RV yo me sahasramamimīta savānatūrto rājā śravaichamānaḥ
RV śataṃ rājño nādhamānasya niṣkāñchatamaśvān prayatān sadya ādam
RV śataṃ kakṣīvānasurasya gonāṃ divi śravo 'jaramā tatāna
RV upa mā śyāvāḥ svanayena dattā vadhūmanto daśa rathāsoasthuḥ
RV ṣaṣṭiḥ sahasramanu gavyamāgāt sanat kakṣīvānabhipitve ahnām
RV catvāriṃśad daśarathasya śoṇāḥ sahasrasyāgre śreṇiṃnayanti
RV madacyutaḥ kṛśanāvato atyān kakṣīvanta udamṛkṣanta pajrāḥ
RV pūrvāmanu prayatimā dade vastrīn yuktānaṣṭāvaridhāyaso gāḥ
RV subandhavo ye viśyā iva vrā anasvantaḥ śrava aiṣanta pajrāḥ
RV āgadhitā parigadhitā yā kaśīkeva jaṅgahe
RV dadāti mahyaṃ yāduri yāśūnāṃ bhojyā śatā
RV upopa me parā mṛśa mā me dabhrāṇi manyathāḥ
RV sarvāhamasmi romaśā gandhārīṇāmivāvikā
RV agniṃ hotāraṃ manye dāsvantaṃ vasuṃ sūnuṃ sahaso jātavedasaṃ vipraṃ na jātavedasam 
ya ūrdhvayā svadhvaro devo devācyā kṛpā
RV ghṛtasya vibhrāṣṭimanu vaṣṭi śociṣājuhvānasya sarpiṣaḥ
RV yajiṣṭhaṃ tvā yajamānā huvema jyeṣṭhamaṅgirasāṃ vipramanmabhirviprebhiḥ śukra manmabhiḥ 
parijmānamiva dyāṃ hotāraṃ carṣaṇīnām
RV śociṣkeśaṃ vṛṣaṇaṃ yamimā viśaḥ prāvantu jūtaye viśaḥ
RV sa hi purū cidojasā virukmatā dīdyāno bhavati druhantaraḥ paraśurna druhantaraḥ 
vīḷu cid yasya samṛtau śruvad vaneva yat sthiram
RV niḥṣahamāṇo yamate nāyate dhanvāsahā nāyate
RV dṛlḥā cidasmā anu duryathā vide tejiṣṭhābhiraraṇibhirdāṣṭyavase 'gnaye dāṣṭyavase 
pra yaḥ purūṇi gāhate takṣad vaneva śociṣā
RV sthirā cidannā ni riṇātyojasā ni sthirāṇi cidojasā
RV tamasya pṛkṣamuparāsu dhīmahi naktaṃ yaḥ sudarśataro divātarādaprāyuṣe divātarāt 
ādasyāyurgrabhaṇavad vīḷu śarma na sūnave
RV bhaktamabhaktamavo vyanto ajarā agnayo vyanto ajarāḥ
RV sa hi śardho na mārutaṃ tuviṣvaṇirapnasvatīṣūrvarāsviṣṭanirārtanāsviṣṭaniḥ 
ādad dhavyānyādadiryajñasya keturarhaṇā
RV adha smāsya harṣato hṛṣīvato viśve juṣanta panthāṃ naraḥ śubhe na panthām
RV dvitā yadīṃ kīstāso abhidyavo namasyanta upavocanta bhṛgavo mathnanto dāsā bhṛgavaḥ 
agnirīśe vasūnāṃ śuciryo dharṇireṣām
RV priyānapidhīnrvaniṣīṣṭa medhira ā vaniṣīṣṭa medhirah
RV viśvāsāṃ tvā viśāṃ patiṃ havāmahe sarvāsāṃ samānandampatiṃ bhuje satyagirvāhasaṃ bhuje 
atithiṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ piturna yasyāsayā
RV amī ca viśve amṛtāsa ā vayo havyādeveṣvā vayaḥ
RV tvamagne sahasā sahantamaḥ śuṣmintamo jāyase devatātaye rayirna devatātaye 
śuṣmintamo hi te mado dyumnintama uta kratuḥ
RV adha smā te pari carantyajara śruṣṭīvāno nājara
RV pra vo mahe sahasā sahasvata uṣarbudhe paśuṣe nāgnaye stomo babhūtvagnaye 
prati yadīṃ haviṣmān viśvāsu kṣāsu joguve
RV agre rebho na jarata ṛṣūṇāṃ jūrṇirhota ṛṣūṇām
RV sa no nediṣṭhaṃ dadṛśāna ā bharāgne devebhiḥ sacanāḥsucetunā maho rāyāḥ sucetunā 
mahi śaviṣṭha nas kṛdhi saṃcakṣe bhuje asyai
RV mahi stotṛbhyo maghavan suvīryaṃ mathīrugro na śavasā
RV ayaṃ jāyata manuṣo dharīmaṇi hotā yajiṣṭha uśijāmanuvratamagniḥ svamanu vratam 
viśvaśruṣṭiḥ sakhīyate rayiriva śravasyate
RV adabdho hotā ni ṣadadiḷas pade parivīta iḷas pade
RV taṃ yajñasādhamapi vātayāmasy ṛtasya pathā namasā haviṣmatā devatātā haviṣmatā 
sa na ūrjāmupābhṛtyayā kṛpā na jūryati
RV yaṃ mātariśvā manave parāvato devaṃ bhāḥ parāvataḥ
RV evena sadyaḥ paryeti pārthivaṃ muhurgī reto vṛṣabhaḥ kanikradad dadhad retah kanikradat 
śataṃ cakṣāṇo akṣabhirdevo vaneṣu turvaṇiḥ
RV sado dadhāna upareṣu sānuṣvagniḥ pareṣu sānuṣu
RV sa sukratuḥ purohito dame dame 'gniryajñasyādhvarasya cetati kratvā yajñasya cetati 
kratvā vedhā iṣūyate viśvā jātāni paspaśe
RV yato ghṛtaśrīratithirajāyata vahnirvedhā ajāyata
RV kratvā yadasya taviṣīṣu pṛñcate 'gneraveṇa marutāṃ na bhojyeṣirāya na bhojyā 
sa hi ṣmā dānaminvati vasūnāṃ ca majmanā
RV sa nastrāsate duritādabhihrutaḥ śaṃsādaghādabhihrutaḥ
RV viśvo vihāyā aratirvasurdadhe haste dakṣiṇe taraṇirnaśiśrathacchravasyayā na śiśrathat 
viśvasmā idiṣudhyate devatrā havyamohiṣe
RV viśvasmā it sukṛte vāram ṛṇvatyagnirdvārā vy ṛṇvati
RV sa mānuṣe vṛjane śantamo hito 'gniryajñeṣu jenyo na viśpatiḥ priyo yajñeṣu viśpatiḥ 
sa havyā mānuṣāṇāmiḷā kṛtāni patyate
RV sa nastrāsate varuṇasya dhūrtermahodevasya dhūrteḥ
RV agniṃ hotāramīḷate vasudhitiṃ priyaṃ cetiṣṭhamaratiṃ nyerire havyavāhaṃ nyerire 
viśvāyuṃ viśvavedasaṃ hotāraṃ yajataṃ kavim
RV devāso raṇvamavase vasūyavo gīrbhīraṇvaṃ vasūyavaḥ
RV yaṃ tvaṃ rathamindra medhasātaye 'pākā santamiṣira praṇayasi prānavadya nayasi 
sadyaścit tamabhiṣṭaye karo vaśaśca vājinam
RV sāsmākamanavadya tūtujāna vedhasāmimāṃ vācaṃ na vedhasām
RV sa śrudhi yaḥ smā pṛtanāsu kāsu cid dakṣāyya indra bharahūtaye nṛbhirasi pratūrtaye nṛbhiḥ 
yaḥ śūraiḥ svaḥ sanitā yo viprairvājaṃ tarutā
RV tamīśānāsa iradhanta vājinaṃ pṛkṣamatyaṃ na vājinam
RV dasmo hi ṣmā vṛṣaṇaṃ pinvasi tvacaṃ kaṃ cid yāvīrararuṃ śūra martyaṃ parivṛṇakṣi martyam 
indrota tubhyaṃ taddive tad rudrāya svayaśase
RV mitrāya vocaṃ varuṇāya saprathaḥ sumṛḷīkāya saprathaḥ
RV asmākaṃ va indramuśmasīṣṭaye sakhāyaṃ viśvāyuṃ prāsahaṃ yujaṃ vājeṣu prāsahaṃ yujam 
asmākaṃbrahmotye 'vā pṛtsuṣu kāsu cit
RV nahi tvā śatru starate stṛṇoṣi yaṃviśvaṃ śatruṃ stṛṇoṣi yam
RV ni ṣū namātimatiṃ kayasya cit tejiṣṭhābhiraraṇibhirnotibhirugrābhirugrotibhiḥ 
neṣi ṇo yathā purānenāḥ śūra manyase
RV viśvāni pūrorapa parṣi vahnirāsā vahnirno acha
RV pra tad voceyaṃ bhavyāyendave havyo na ya iṣavān manma rejati rakṣohā manma rejati 
svayaṃ so asmadā nido vadhairajeta durmatim
RV ava sravedaghaśaṃso 'vataramava kṣudramiva sravet
RV vanema tad dhotrayā citantyā vanema rayiṃ rayivaḥ suvīryaṃ raṇvaṃ santaṃ suvīryam 
durmanmānaṃ sumantubhiremiṣā pṛcīmahi
RV ā satyābhirindraṃ dyumnahūtibhiryajatraṃ dyumnahūtibhiḥ
RV praprā vo asme svayaśobhirūtī parivarga indro durmatīnāṃ darīman durmatīnām 
svayaṃ sā riṣayadhyai yā na upeṣe atraiḥ
RV hatemasan na vakṣati kṣiptā jūrṇirna vakṣati
RV tvaṃ na indra rāyā parīṇasā yāhi pathananehasā puro yāhyarakṣasā 
sacasva naḥ parāka ā sacasvāstamīka ā
RV pāhi no dūrādārādabhiṣṭibhiḥ sadā pāhyabhiṣṭibhiḥ
RV tvaṃ na indra rāyā tarūṣasograṃ cit tvā mahimā sakṣadavase mahe mitraṃ nāvase 
ojiṣṭha trātaravitā rathaṃ kaṃ cidamartya
RV anyamasmad ririṣeḥ kaṃ cidadrivo ririkṣantaṃ cidadrivaḥ
RV pāhi na indra suṣṭuta sridho 'vayātā sadamid durmatīnāndevaḥ san durmatīnām 
hantā pāpasya rakṣasastrātā viprasya māvataḥ
RV adhā hi tvā janitā jījanad vaso rakṣohaṇaṃ tvā jījanad vaso
RV endra yāhyupa naḥ parāvato nāyamachā vidathānīva satpatirastaṃ rājeva satpatiḥ 
havāmahe tvā vayaṃ prayasvantaḥ sute sacā
RV putrāso na pitaraṃ vājasātaye maṃhiṣṭhaṃ vājasātaye
RV pibā somamindra suvānamadribhiḥ kośena siktamavataṃ navaṃsagastātṛṣāṇo na vaṃsagaḥ 
madāya haryataya te tuviṣṭamāya dhāyase
RV ā tvā yachantu harito na sūryamahāviśveva sūryam
RV avindad divo nihitaṃ guhā nidhiṃ verna garbhaṃ parivītamaśmanyanante antaraśmani 
vrajaṃ vajri
gavāmiva siṣāsannaṅgirastamaḥ
RV apāvṛṇodiṣa indraḥ parīvṛtā dvāra iṣaḥ parīvṛtāḥ
RV dādṛhāṇo vajramindro gabhastyoḥ kṣadmeva tigmamasanāyasaṃ śyadahihatyāya saṃ śyat 
saṃvivyāna ojasā śavobhirindra majmanā
RV taṣṭeva vṛkṣaṃ vanino ni vṛścasi paraśveva ni vṛścasi
RV tvaṃ vṛthā nadya indra sartave 'chā samudramasṛjo rathāniva vājayato rathāniva 
ita ūtīrayuñjata samānamarthamakṣitam
RV dhenūriva manave viśvadohaso janāya viśvadohasaḥ
RV imāṃ te vācaṃ vasūyanta āyavo rathaṃ na dhīraḥ svapāatakṣiṣuḥ sumnāya tvāmatakṣiṣuḥ 
śumbhanto jenyaṃ yathā vājeṣu vipra vājinam
RV atyamiva śavase sātaye dhanā viśvā dhanāni sātaye
RV bhinat puro navatimindra pūrave divodāsāya mahi dāśuṣe nṛto vajreṇa dāśuṣe nṛto 
atithigvāya śambaraṃ girerugroavābharat
RV maho dhanāni dayamāna ojasā viśvā dhanānyojasā
RV indraḥ samatsu yajamānamāryaṃ prāvad viśveṣu śatamūtirājiṣu svarmīḷheṣvājiṣu 
manave śāsadavratān tvacaṃ kṛṣṇāmarandhayat
RV dakṣan na viśvaṃ tatṛṣāṇamoṣatinyarśasānamoṣati
RV sūraścakraṃ pra vṛhajjāta ojasā prapitve vācamaruṇo muṣāyatīśāna ā muṣāyati 
uśanā yat parāvato 'jagannūtaye kave
RV sumnāni viśvā manuṣeva turvaṇirahā viśvevaturvaṇiḥ
RV sa no navyebhirvṛṣakarmannukthaiḥ purāṃ dartaḥ pāyubhiḥpāhi śagmaiḥ
RV divodāsebhirindra stavāno vāvṛdhīthā ahobhiriva dyauḥ
RV indrāya hi dyaurasuro anamnatendrāya mahī pṛthivī varīmabhirdyumnasātā varīmabhiḥ 
indraṃ viśve sajoṣaso devāso dadhire puraḥ
RV indrāya viśvā savanāni mānuṣā rātāni santu mānuṣā
RV viśveṣu hi tvā savaneṣu tuñjate samānamekaṃ vṛṣamaṇyavaḥ pṛthak svaḥ saniṣyavaḥ pṛthak 
taṃ tvā nāvaṃ na parṣaṇiṃ śūṣasya dhuri dhīmahi
RV indraṃ na yajñaiścitayanta āyava stomebhirindramāyavaḥ
RV vi tvā tatasre mithunā avasyavo vrajasya sātā gavyasya niḥsṛjaḥ sakṣanta indra niḥsṛjaḥ 
yad gavyantā dvā janā svaryantā samūhasi
RV āviṣ karikrad vṛṣaṇaṃ sacābhuvaṃ vajramindra sacābhuvam
RV viduṣ ṭe asya vīryasya pūravaḥ puro yadindra śāradīravātiraḥ sāsahāno avātiraḥ 
śāsastamindra martyamayajyuṃ śavasas pate
RV mahīmamuṣṇāḥ pṛthivīmimā apo mandasāna imā apaḥ
RV ādit te asya vīryasya carkiran madeṣu vṛṣannuśijo yadāvitha sakhīyato yadāvitha 
cakartha kāramebhyaḥ pṛtanāsu pravantava
RV te anyāmanyāṃ nadyaṃ saniṣṇata śravasyantaḥ saniṣṇata
RV uto no asyā uṣaso juṣeta hyarkasya bodhi haviṣo havīmabhiḥ svarṣātā havīmabhiḥ 
yadindra hantave mṛdho vṛṣā vajriñciketasi
RV ā me asya vedhaso navīyaso manma śrudhi navīyasaḥ
RV tvaṃ tamindra vāvṛdhāno asmayuramitrayantaṃ tuvijāta martyaṃ vajreṇa śūra martyam 
jahi yo no aghāyati śṛṇuṣva suśravastamaḥ
RV riṣṭaṃ na yāmannapa bhūtu durmatirviśvāpa bhūtu durmatiḥ
RV tvayā vayaṃ maghavan pūrvye dhana indratvotāḥ sāsahyāma pṛtanyato vanuyāma vanuṣyataḥ 
nediṣṭhe asminnahanyadhi vocā nu sunvate
RV asmin yajñe vi cayemā bhare kṛtaṃ vājayanto bhare kṛtam
RV svarjeṣe bhara āprasya vakmanyuṣarbudhaḥ svasminnañjasikrāṇasya svasminnañjasi 
ahannindro yathā vide śīrṣṇāśīrṣṇopavācyaḥ
RV asmatrā te sadhryak santu rātayo bhadrā bhadrasya rātayaḥ
RV tat tu prayaḥ pratnathā te śuśukvanaṃ yasmin yajñe vāramakṛṇvata kṣayam ṛtasya vārasi kṣayam 
vi tad voceradha dvitāntaḥ paśyanti raśmibhiḥ
RV sa ghā vide anvindro gaveṣaṇo bandhukṣidbhyo gaveṣaṇaḥ
RV nū itthā te pūrvathā ca pravācyaṃ yadaṅgirobhyo 'vṛṇorapa vrajamindra śikṣannapa vrajam 
aibhyaḥ samānyā diśāsmabhyaṃ jeṣi yotsi ca
RV sunvadbhyo randhayā kaṃ cidavrataṃ hṛṇāyantaṃ cidavratam
RV saṃ yajjanān kratubhiḥ śūra īkṣayad dhane hite taruṣanta śravasyavaḥ pra yakṣanta śravasyavaḥ 
tasmā āyuḥ prajāvadid bādhe arcantyojasā
RV indra okyaṃ didhiṣanta dhītayo devānachā na dhītayaḥ
RV yuvaṃ tamindrāparvatā puroyudhā yo naḥ pṛtanyādapa taṃtamid dhataṃ vajre
a taṃtamid dhatam 
dūre cattāya chantsad gahanaṃ yadinakṣat
RV asmākaṃ śatrūn pari śūra viśvato darmā darṣīṣṭa viśvataḥ
RV ubhe punāmi rodasī ṛtena druho dahāmi saṃ mahīranindrāḥ
RV abhivlagya yatra hatā amitrā vailasthānaṃ pari tṛḷhā aśeran
RV abhivlagyā cidadrivaḥ śīrṣā yātumatīnām
RV chindhi vaṭūriṇā padā mahāvaṭūriṇā padā
RV avāsāṃ maghavañ jahi śardho yātumatīnām
RV vailasthānake armake mahāvailasthe armake
RV yāsāṃ tisraḥ pañcāśato 'bhivlaṅgairapāvapaḥ
RV tat sute manāyati takat su te manāyati
RV piśaṅgabhṛṣṭimambhṛṇaṃ piśācimindra saṃ mṛṇa
RV sarvaṃrakṣo ni barhaya
RV avarmaha indra dādṛhi śrudhī naḥ śuśoca hi dyauḥ kṣāna bhīṣānadrivo ghṛṇān na bhīṣānadrivaḥ 
śuṣmintamo hi śuṣmibhirvadhairugrebhirīyase
RV apūruṣaghno apratīta śūra satvabhistrisaptaiḥ śūra satvabhiḥ
RV vanoti hi sunvan kṣayaṃ parīṇasaḥ sunvāno hi ṣmā yajatyava dviṣo devānāmava dviṣaḥ 
sunvāna it siṣāsati sahasrā vājyavṛtaḥ
RV sunvānāyendro dadātyābhuvaṃ rayiṃ dadātyābhuvam
RV ā tvā juvo rārahāṇā abhi prayo vāyo vahantviha pūrvapītaye somasya pūrvapītaye 
ūrdhvā te anu sūnṛtā manastiṣṭhatu jānatī
RV niyutvatā rathenā yāhi dāvane vāyo makhasya dāvane
RV mandantu tvā mandino vāyavindavo 'smat krāṇāsaḥ sukṛtā abhidyavo gobhiḥ krāṇā abhidyavaḥ 
yad dha krāṇā iradhyai dakṣaṃ sacanta ūtayaḥ
RV sadhrīcīnā niyuto dāvane dhiya upa bruvata īṃ dhiyaḥ
RV vāyuryuṅkte rohitā vāyuraruṇā vāyū rathe ajirā dhuri voḷhave vahiṣṭhā dhuri voḷhave 
pra bodhayā purandhiṃjāra ā sasatīmiva
RV pra cakṣaya rodasī vāsayoṣasaḥ śravase vāsayoṣasaḥ
RV tubhyamuṣāsaḥ śucayaḥ parāvati bhadrā vastrā tanvate daṃsu raśmiṣu citrā navyeṣu raśmiṣu 
tubhyaṃ dhenuḥ sabardughā viśvā vasūni dohate
RV ajanayo maruto vakṣaṇābhyodiva ā vakṣaṇābhyaḥ
RV tubhyaṃ śukrāsaḥ śucayasturaṇyavo madeṣūgrā iṣaṇantabhurvaṇyapāmiṣanta bhurvaṇi 
tvāṃ tsārī dasamāno bhagamīṭṭe takvavīye
RV tvāṃ viśvasmād bhuvanāt pāsi dharmaṇāsuryāt pāsi dharmaṇa
RV tvaṃ no vāyaveṣāmapūrvyaḥ somānāṃ prathamaḥ pītimarhasi sutānāṃ pītimarhasi 
uto vihutmatīnāṃ viśāṃ vavarjuṣīṇām
RV viśvā it te dhenavo duhra āśiraṃ ghṛtaṃ duhrata āśiram
RV stīrṇaṃ barhirupa no yāhi vītaye sahasreṇa niyutā niyutvate śatinībhirniyutvate 
tubhyaṃ hi pūrvapītaye devā devāya yemire
RV pra te sutāso madhumanto asthiran madāya kratve asthiran
RV tubhyāyaṃ somaḥ paripūto adribhi spārhā vasānaḥ pari kośamarṣati śukrā vasāno arṣati 
tavāyaṃ bhāga āyuṣusomo deveṣu hūyate
RV vaha vāyo niyuto yāhyasmayurjuṣāṇo yāhyasmayuḥ
RV ā no niyudbhiḥ śatinībhiradhvaraṃ sahasriṇībhirupa yāhi vītaye vāyo havyāni vītaye 
tavāyaṃ bhāga ṛtviyaḥ saraśmiḥ sūrye sacā
RV adhvaryubhirbharamāṇā ayaṃsata vāyo śukrā ayaṃsata
RV ā vāṃ ratho niyutvān vakṣadavase 'bhi prayāṃsi sudhitāni vītaye vāyo havyāni vītaye 
pibataṃ madhvo andhasaḥ pūrvapeyaṃ hi vāṃ hitam
RV vāyavā candreṇa rādhasā gatamindraśca rādhasā gatam
RV ā vāṃ dhiyo vavṛtyuradhvarānupemaminduṃ marmṛjanta vājinamāśumatyaṃ na vājinam 
teṣāṃ pibatamasmayū ā no gantamihotyā
RV indravāyū sutānāmadribhiryuvaṃ madāya vājadā yuvam
RV ime vāṃ somā apsvā sutā ihādhvaryubhirbharamāṇā ayaṃsata vāyo śukrā ayaṃsata 
ete vāmabhyasṛkṣata tiraḥ pavitramāśavaḥ
RV yuvāyavo 'ti romāṇyavyayā somāso atyavyayā
RV ati vāyo sasato yāhi śaśvato yatra grāvā vadati tatra gachataṃ gṛhamindraśca gachatam
RV vi sūnṛtā dadṛśe rīyate ghṛtamā pūrṇayā niyutā yātho adhvaramindraśca yātho adhvaram
RV atrāha tad vahethe madhva āhutiṃ yamaśvatthamupatiṣṭhanta jāyavo 'sme te santu jāyavaḥ
RV sākaṃ gāvaḥ suvate pacyate yavo na te vāya upa dasyanti dhenavo nāpa dasyanti dhenavaḥ
RV ime ye te su vāyo bāhvojaso 'ntarnadī te patayantyukṣaṇo mahi vrādhanta ukṣaṇaḥ 
dhanvañcid ye anāśavo jīrāścidagiraukasaḥ
RV sūryasyeva raśmayo durniyantavo hastayordurniyantavaḥ
RV pra su jyeṣṭhaṃ nicirābhyāṃ bṛhan namo havyaṃ matiṃ bharatā mṛḷayadbhyāṃ svādiṣṭhaṃ mṛḷayadbhyām 
tā samrājāghṛtāsutī yajñeyajña upastutā
RV athainoḥ kṣatraṃ na kutaścanādhṛṣe devatvaṃ nū cidādhṛṣe
RV adraśi gātururave varīyasī panthā ṛtasya samayaṃsta raśmibhiścakṣurbhagasya raśmibhiḥ 
dyukṣaṃ mitrasya sādanamaryamṇo varuṇasya ca
RV athā dadhāte bṛhaduktyhaṃ vayaupastutyaṃ bṛhad vayaḥ
RV jyotiṣmatīmaditiṃ dhārayatkṣitiṃ svarvatīmā sacete divedive jāgṛvāṃsā divedive 
jyotiṣmat kṣatramāśāte ādityā dānunas patī
RV mitrastayorvaruṇo yātayajjano 'ryamā yātayajjanaḥ
RV ayaṃ mitrāya varuṇāya śantamaḥ somo bhūtvavapāneṣvābhago devo deveṣvābhagaḥ 
taṃ devāso juṣerata viśve adya sajoṣasaḥ
RV tathā rājānā karatho yadimaha ṛtāvānā yadīmahe
RV yo mitrāya varuṇāyāvidhajjano 'narvāṇaṃ taṃ pari pātoaṃhaso dāśvāṃsaṃ martamaṃhasaḥ 
tamaryamābhi rakṣaty ṛjūyantamanu vratam
RV ukthairya enoḥ paribhūṣati vrataṃ stomairābhūṣati vratam
RV namo dive bṛhate rodasībhyāṃ mitrāya vocaṃ varuṇāya mīḷhuṣe sumṛḷīkāya mīḷhuṣe 
indramagnimupa stuhi dyukṣamaryamaṇaṃ bhagam
RV jyog jīvantaḥ prajayā sacemahi somasyotī sacemahi
RV ūtī devānāṃ vayamindravanto maṃsīmahi svayaśaso marudbhiḥ
RV agnirmitro varuṇaḥ śarma yaṃsan tadaśyāma maghavāno vayaṃ ca
RV suṣumā yātamadribhirgośrītā matsarā ime somāso matsarā ime 
ā rājānā divispṛśāsmatrā gantamupa naḥ
RV ime vāṃ mitrāvaruṇā gavāśiraḥ somāḥ śukrā gavāśiraḥ
RVxx ima ā yātam indavaḥ somāso dadhyāśiraḥ sutāso dadhyāśiraḥ 
RVxx uta vām uṣaso budhi sākaṃ sūryasya raśmibhiḥ 
RVxx suto mitrāya varuṇāya pītaye cārur ṛtāya pītaye 
RVxx tāṃ vāṃ dhenuṃ na vāsarīm aṃśuṃ duhanty adribhiḥ somaṃ duhanty adribhiḥ 
RVxx asmatrā gantam upa no 'rvāñcā somapītaye 
RVxx ayaṃ vām mitrāvaruṇā nṛbhiḥ sutaḥ soma ā pītaye sutaḥ 
RVxx prapra pūṣṇas tuvijātasya śasyate mahitvam asya tavaso na tandate stotram asya na tandate 
RVxx arcāmi sumnayann aham antyūtim mayobhuvam 
RVxx viśvasya yo mana āyuyuve makho deva āyuyuve makhaḥ 
RVxx pra hi tvā pūṣann ajiraṃ na yāmani stomebhiḥ kṛṇva ṛṇavo yathā mṛdha uṣṭro na pīparo mṛdhaḥ 
RVxx huve yat tvā mayobhuvaṃ devaṃ sakhyāya martyaḥ 
RVxx asmākam āṅgūṣān dyumninas kṛdhi vājeṣu dyumninas kṛdhi 
RVxx yasya te pūṣan sakhye vipanyavaḥ kratvā cit santo 'vasā bubhujrira iti kratvā bubhujrire 
RVxx tām anu tvā navīyasīṃ niyutaṃ rāya īmahe 
RVxx aheḷamāna uruśaṃsa sarī bhava vājevāje sarī bhava 
RVxx asyā ū ṣu ṇa upa sātaye bhuvo 'heḷamāno rarivāṃ ajāśva śravasyatām ajāśva 
RVxx o ṣu tvā vavṛtīmahi stomebhir dasma sādhubhiḥ 
RVxx nahi tvā pūṣann atimanya āghṛṇe na te sakhyam apahnuve 
RVxx astu śrauṣaṭ puro agnīṃ dhiyā dadha ā nu tac chardho divyaṃ vṛṇīmaha indravāyū vṛṇīmahe 
RVxx yad dha krāṇā vivasvati nābhā saṃdāyi navyasī 
RVxx adha pra sū na upa yantu dhītayo devāṃ achā na dhītayaḥ 
RVxx yad dha tyan mitrāvaruṇāv ṛtād adhy ādadāthe anṛtaṃ svena manyunā dakṣasya svena manyunā 
RVxx yuvor itthādhi sadmasv apaśyāma hiraṇyayam 
RVxx dhībhiś cana manasā svebhir akṣabhiḥ somasya svebhir akṣabhiḥ 
RVxx yuvāṃ stomebhir devayanto aśvināśrāvayanta iva ślokam āyavo yuvāṃ havyābhy āyavaḥ 
RVxx yuvor viśvā adhi śriyaḥ pṛkṣaś ca viśvavedasā 
RVxx pruṣāyante vām pavayo hiraṇyaye rathe dasrā hiraṇyaye 
RVxx aceti dasrā vy  nākam ṛṇvatho yuñjate vāṃ rathayujo diviṣṭiṣv adhvasmāno diviṣṭiṣu 
RVxx adhi vāṃ sthāma vandhure rathe dasrā hiraṇyaye 
RVxx patheva yantāv anuśāsatā rajo 'ñjasā śāsatā rajaḥ 
RVxx śacībhir naḥ śacīvasū divā naktaṃ daśasyatam 
RVxx mā vāṃ rātir upa dasat kadā canāsmad rātiḥ kadā cana 
RVxx vṛṣann indra vṛṣapāṇāsa indava ime sutā adriṣutāsa udbhidas tubhyaṃ sutāsa udbhidaḥ 
RVxx te tvā mandantu dāvane mahe citrāya rādhase 
RVxx gīrbhir girvāha stavamāna ā gahi sumṛḷīko na ā gahi 
RVxx o ṣū ṇo agne śṛṇuhi tvam īḷito devebhyo bravasi yajñiyebhyo rājabhyo yajñiyebhyaḥ 
RVxx yad dha tyām aṅgirobhyo dhenuṃ devā adattana 
RVxx vi tāṃ duhre aryamā kartarī sacāṃ eṣa tāṃ veda me sacā 
RVxx mo ṣu vo asmad abhi tāni pauṃsyā sanā bhūvan dyumnāni mota jāriṣur asmat purota jāriṣuḥ 
RVxx yad vaś citraṃ yugeyuge navyaṃ ghoṣād amartyam 
RVxx asmāsu tan maruto yac ca duṣṭaraṃ didhṛtā yac ca duṣṭaram 
RVxx dadhyaṅ ha me januṣam pūrvo aṅgirāḥ priyamedhaḥ kaṇvo atrir manur vidus te me pūrve manur viduḥ 
RVxx teṣāṃ deveṣv āyatir asmākaṃ teṣu nābhayaḥ 
RVxx teṣām padena mahy ā name girendrāgnī ā name girā 
RVxx hotā yakṣad vanino vanta vāryam bṛhaspatir yajati vena ukṣabhiḥ puruvārebhir ukṣabhiḥ 
RVxx jagṛbhmā dūraādiśaṃ ślokam adrer adha tmanā 
RVxx adhārayad ararindāni sukratuḥ purū sadmāni sukratuḥ 
RVxx ye devāso divy ekādaśa stha pṛthivyām adhy ekādaśa stha 
RVxx apsukṣito mahinaikādaśa stha te devāso yajñam imaṃ juṣadhvam 
RVxx vediṣade priyadhāmāya sudyute dhāsim iva pra bharā yonim agnaye 
RVxx vastreṇeva vāsayā manmanā śuciṃ jyotīrathaṃ śukravarṇaṃ tamohanam 
RV abhi dvijanmā trivṛdannam ṛjyate saṃvatsare vāvṛdhe jagdhamī punaḥ
RV anyasyāsā jihvaya jenyo vṛṣā nyanyena vaninomṛṣṭa varaṇaḥ
RV kṛṣṇaprutau vevije asya sakṣitā ubhā tarete abhi matarā śiśum
RV prācajihvaṃ dhvasayantaṃ tṛṣucyutamā sācyaṃ kupayaṃ vardhanaṃ pituḥ
RV mumukṣvo manave manavasyate raghudruvaḥ kṛṣṇasītāsa ū juvaḥ
RV asamanā ajirāso raghuṣyado vātajūtā upa yujyanta āśavaḥ
RV ādasya te dhvasayanto vṛtherate kṛṣṇamabhvaṃ mahi varpaḥkarikrataḥ
RV yat sīṃ mahīmavaniṃ prābhi marmṛśadabhiśvasan stanayanneti nānadat
RV bhūṣan na yo 'dhi babhrūṣu namnate vṛṣeva patnīrabhyeti roruvat
RV ojāyamānastanvaśca śumbhate bhīmo na śṛngādavidhava durgṛbhiḥ
RV sa saṃstiro viṣṭiraḥ saṃ gṛbhayati jananneva jānatīrnitya ā śaye
RV punarvardhante api yanti devyamanyad varpaḥ pitroḥ kṛṇvate sacā
RV tamagruvaḥ keśinīḥ saṃ hi rebhira ūrdhvāstasthurmamruṣīḥ prāyave punaḥ
RV tāsāṃ jarāṃ pramuñcanneti nānadadasuṃ paraṃ janayañ jīvamastṛtam
RV adhīvasaṃ pari matu rihannaha tuvigrebhiḥ satvabhiryāti vi jrayaḥ
RV vayo dadhat padvate rerihat sadānu śyenī sacatevartanīraha
RV asmākamagne maghavatsu dīdihyadha śvasīvān vṛṣabho damūnāḥ
RV avāsyā śiśumatīradīdervarmeva yutsu parijarbhurāṇaḥ
RV idamagne sudhitaṃ durdhitādadhi priyādu cin manmanaḥ preyo astu te
RV yat te śukraṃ tanvo rocate śuci tenāsmabhyaṃvanase ratnamā tvam
RV rathāya nāvamuta no gṛhāya nityāritrāṃ padvatīṃ rāsyagne
RV asmākaṃ vīrānuta no maghono janāṃśca yā pārayāccharma yā ca
RV abhī no agna ukthamijjuguryā dyāvākṣāmā sindhavaśca svagūrtāḥ
RV gavyaṃ yavyaṃ yanto dīrghāheṣaṃ varamaruṇyo varanta
RV baḷ itthā tad vapuṣe dhāyi darśataṃ devasya bhargaḥ sahaso yato jani
RV yadīmupa hvarate sādhate matirṛtasya dhena anayanta sasrutaḥ
RV pṛkṣo vapuḥ pitumān nitya ā śaye dvitīyamā saptaśivāsu mātṛṣu
RV tṛtīyamasya vṛṣabhasya dohase daśapramatiṃ janayanta yoṣaṇaḥ
RV niryadīṃ budhnān mahiṣasya varpasa īśānāsaḥ śavasākranta sūrayaḥ
RV yadīmanu pradivo madhva ādhave guhā santaṃ mātariśvā mathāyati
RV pra yat pituḥ paramān nīyate paryā pṛkṣudho vīrudho daṃsu rohati
RV ubhā yadasya januṣaṃ yadinvata ādid yaviṣṭho abhavad ghṛṇā śuciḥ
RV ādin mātṝrāviśad yāsvā śucirahiṃsyamāna urviyāvi vāvṛdhe
RV anu yat pūrvā aruhat sanājuvo ni navyasīṣvavarāsu dhāvate
RV ādid dhotāraṃ vṛṇate diviṣṭiṣu bhagamiva papṛcānāsa ṛñjate
RV devān yat kratvā majmanā puruṣṭuto martaṃ saṃsaṃ viśvadhā veti dhāyase
RV vi yadasthād yajato vātacodito hvāro na vakvā jaraṇā anākṛtaḥ
RV tasya patman dakṣuṣaḥ kṛṣṇajaṃhasaḥ śucijanmano raja ā vyadhvanaḥ
RV ratho na yātaḥ śikvabhiḥ kṛto dyāmaṅgebhiraruṣebhirīyate
RV ādasya te kṛṣṇāso dakṣi sūrayaḥ śūrasyeva tveṣathādīṣate vayaḥ
RV tvayā hyagne varuṇo dhṛtavrato mitraḥ śāśadre aryamā sudānavaḥ
RV yat sīmanu kratunā viśvathā vibhurarān na nemiḥ paribhūrajāyathāḥ
RV tvamagne śaśamānāya sunvate ratnaṃ yaviṣṭha devatātiminvasi
RV taṃ tvā nu navyaṃ sahaso yuvan vayaṃ bhagaṃ na kāremahiratna dhīmahi
RV asme rayiṃ na svarthaṃ damūnasaṃ bhagaṃ dakṣaṃ na papṛcāsi dharṇasim
RV raśmīnriva yo yamati janmanī ubhe devānāṃ śaṃsam ṛta ā ca sukratuḥ
RV uta naḥ sudyotmā jīrāśvo hotā mandraḥ śṛṇavaccandrarathaḥ
RV sa no neṣan neṣatamairamūro 'gnirvāmaṃ suvitaṃ vasyo acha
RV astāvyagniḥ śimīvadbhirarkaiḥ sāmrājyāya prataraṃ dadhānaḥ
RV amī ca ye maghavāno vayaṃ ca mihaṃ na sūro atiniṣ ṭatanyuḥ
RV samiddho agna ā vaha devānadya yatasruce
RV tantuṃ tanuṣva pūrvyaṃ sutasomāya dāśuṣe
RV ghṛtavantamupa māsi madhumantaṃ tanūnapāt
RV yajñaṃ viprasya māvataḥ śaśamānasya dāśuṣaḥ
RV śuciḥ pāvako adbhuto madhvā yajñaṃ mimikṣati
RV narāśaṃsaḥ trirā divo devo deveṣu yajñiyaḥ
RV īḷito agna ā vahendraṃ citramiha priyam
RV iyaṃ hi tvā matirmamāchā sujihva vacyate
RV stṛṇānāso yatasruco barhiryajñe svadhvare
RV vṛñje devavyacastamamindrāya śarma saprathaḥ
RV vi śrayantām ṛtāvṛdhaḥ prayai devebhyo mahīḥ
RV pāvakāsaḥ puruspṛho dvāro devīrasaścataḥ
RV ā bhandamāne upāke naktoṣāsā supeśasā
RV yahvī ṛtaśyamātarā sīdatāṃ barhirā sumat
RV mandrajihvā jugurvaṇī hotārā daivyā kavī
RV yajñaṃ no yakṣatāmimaṃ sidhramadya divispṛśam
RV śucirdeveṣvarpitā hotrā marutsu bhāratī
RV iḷā sarasvatī mahī barhiḥ sīdantu yajñiyāḥ
RV tan nasturīpamadbhutaṃ puru vāraṃ puru tmanā
RV tvaṣṭāpoṣāya vi ṣyatu rāye nābhā no asmayuḥ
RV avasṛjannupa tmanā devān yakṣi vanaspate
RV agnirhavyā suṣūdati devo deveṣu medhiraḥ
RV pūṣaṇvate marutvate viśvadevāya vāyave
RV svāhā gāyatravepase havyamindrāya kartana
RV svāhākṛtānyā gahyupa havyāni vītaye
RV indrā gahi śrudhī havaṃ tvāṃ havante adhvare
RV pra tavyasīṃ navyasīṃ dhītimagnaye vāco matiṃ sahasaḥsūnave bhare
RV apāṃ napād yo vasubhiḥ saha priyo hotā pṛthivyāṃ nyasīdad ṛtviyaḥ
RV sa jāyamānaḥ parame vyomanyāviragnirabhavan mātariśvane
RV asya kratvā samidhānasya majmanā pra dyāvā śociḥ pṛthivī arocayat
RV asya tveṣā ajarā asya bhānavaḥ susandṛśaḥ supratīkasyasudyutaḥ
RV bhātvakṣaso atyakturna sindhavo 'gne rejante asasanto ajarāḥ
RV yamerire bhṛgavo viśvavedasaṃ nābhā pṛthivyā bhuvanasya majmanā
RV agniṃ taṃ gīrbhirhinuhi sva ā dame ya eko vasvo varuṇo na rājati
RV na yo varāya marutāmiva svanaḥ seneva sṛṣṭā divyā yathāśaniḥ
RV agnirjambhaistigitairatti bharvati yodho na śatrūn sa vanā ny ṛñjate
RV kuvin no agnirucathasya vīrasad vasuṣ kuvid vasubhiḥ kāmamāvarat
RV codaḥ kuvit tutujyāt sātaye dhiyaḥ śucipratīkaṃ tamayā dhiyā gṛṇe
RV ghṛtapratīkaṃ va ṛtasya dhūrṣadamagniṃ mitraṃ na samidhāna ṛñjate
RV indhāno akro vidatheṣu dīdyacchukravarṇāmudu no yaṃsate dhiyam
RV aprayuchannaprayuchadbhiragne śivebhirnaḥ pāyubhiḥ pāhi śagmaiḥ
RV adabdhebhiradṛpitebhiriṣṭe 'nimiṣadbhiḥ pari pāhi no jāḥ
RV eti pra hotā vratamasya māyayordhvāṃ dadhānaḥ śucipeśasaṃ dhiyam
RV abhi srucaḥ kramate dakṣiṇāvṛto yā asya dhāma prathamaṃ ha niṃsate
RV abhīm ṛtasya dohanā anūṣata yonau devasya sadane parīvṛtāḥ
RV apāmupasthe vibhṛto yadāvasadadha svadhā adhayad yābhirīyate
RV yuyūṣataḥ savayasā tadid vapuḥ samānamarthaṃ vitaritratā mithaḥ
RV ādīṃ bhago na havyaḥ samasmadā voḷhurna raśmīn samayaṃsta sārathiḥ
RV yamīṃ dvā savayasā saparyataḥ samāne yonā mithunā samokasā
RV divā na naktaṃ palito yuvājani purū carannajaro mānuṣā yugā
RV tamīṃ hinvanti dhītayo daśa vriśo devaṃ martāsa ūtaye havāmahe
RV dhanoradhi pravata ā sa ṛṇvatyabhivrajadbhirvayunā navādhita
RV tvaṃ hyagne divyasya rājasi tvaṃ pārthivasya paśupā iva tmanā
RV enī ta ete bṛhatī abhiśriyā hiraṇyayī vakvarī barhirāśāte
RV agne juṣasva prati harya tad vaco mandra svadhāva ṛtajāta sukrato
RV yo viśvataḥ partyaṃṃ asi darśato raṇvaḥ sandṛṣṭau pitumāniva kṣayaḥ
RV taṃ pṛchatā sa jagāmā sa veda sa cikitvānīyate sā nvīyate
RV tasmin santi praśiṣastasminniṣṭayaḥ sa vājasya śavasaḥ śuṣmiṇas patiḥ
RV tamit pṛchanti na simo vi pṛchati sveneva dhīro manasā yadagrabhīt
RV na mṛṣyate prathamaṃ nāparaṃ vaco 'sya kratvasacate apradṛpitaḥ
RV tamid gachanti juhvastamarvatīrviśvānyekaḥ śṛṇavad vacāṃsi me
RV purupraiṣastaturiryajñasādhano 'chidrotiḥ śiśurādatta saṃ rabhaḥ
RV upasthāyaṃ carati yat samārata sadyo jātastatsāra yujyebhiḥ
RV abhi śvāntaṃ mṛśate nāndye mude yadīṃ gachantyuśatīrapiṣṭhitam
RV sa īṃ mṛgo apyo vanargurupa tvacyupamasyāṃ ni dhāyi
RV vyabravīd vayunā martyebhyo 'gnirvidvān ṛtacid dhi satyaḥ
RV trimūrdhānaṃ saptaraśmiṃ gṛṇīṣe 'nūnamagniṃ pitrorupasthe
RV niṣattamasya carato dhruvasya viśvā divo rocanāpaprivāṃsam
RV ukṣā mahānabhi vavakṣa ene ajarastasthāvitaūtirṛṣvaḥ
RV urvyāḥ pado ni dadhāti sānau rihantyūdho aruṣāso asya
RV samānaṃ vatsamabhi saṃcarantī viṣvag dhenū vi carataḥ sumeke
RV anapavṛjyānadhvano mimāne viśvān ketānadhi mahodadhāne
RV dhīrāsaḥ padaṃ kavayo nayanti nānā hṛdā rakṣamāṇā ajuryam
RV siṣāsantaḥ paryapaśyanta sindhumāvirebhyo abhavatsūryo nṝn
RV didṛkṣeṇyaḥ pari kāṣṭhāsu jenya īḷenyo maho arbhāya jīvase
RV purutrā yadabhavat sūrahaibhyo garbhebhyo maghavā viśvadarśataḥ
RV kathā te agne śucayanta āyordadāśurvājebhirāśuṣāṇāḥ
RV ubhe yat toke tanaye dadhānā ṛtasya sāman raṇayantadevāḥ
RV bodhā me asya vacaso yaviṣṭha maṃhiṣṭhasya prabhṛtasya svadhāvaḥ
RV pīyati tvo anu tvo gṛṇāti vandāruste tanvaṃ vandeagne
RV ye pāyavo māmateyaṃ te agne paśyanto andhaṃ duritādarakṣan
RV rarakṣa tān sukṛto viśvavedā dipsanta id ripavo nāha debhuḥ
RV yo no agne ararivānaghāyurarātīvā marcayati dvayena
RV mantro guruḥ punarastu so asmā anu mṛkṣīṣṭa tanvaṃ duruktaiḥ
RV uta vā yaḥ sahasya pravidvān marto martaṃ marcayati dvayena
RV ataḥ pāhi stavamāna stuvantamagne mākirno duritāya dhāyīḥ
RV mathīd yadīṃ viṣṭo mātariśvā hotāraṃ viśvāpsuṃ viśvadevyam
RV ni yaṃ dadhurmanuṣyāsu vikṣu svarṇa citraṃ vapuṣe vibhāvam
RV dadānamin na dadabhanta manmāgnirvarūthaṃ mama tasya cākan
RV juṣanta viśvanyasya karmopastutiṃ bharamāṇasya kāroḥ
RV nitye cin nu yaṃ sadane jagṛbhre praśastibhirdadhire yajñiyasaḥ
RV pra sū nayanta gṛbhayanta iṣṭāvaśvāso na rathyorarahaṇāḥ
RV purūṇi dasmo ni riṇāti jambhairād rocate vana ā vibhāvā
RV ādasya vāto anu vāti śocirasturna śaryāmasanāmanu dyūn
RV na yaṃ ripavo na riṣaṇyavo garbhe santaṃ reṣaṇā reṣayanti
RV andhā apaśyā na dabhannabhikhyā nityāsa īṃ pretāro arakṣan
RV mahaḥ sa rāya eṣate patirdannina inasya vasunaḥ pada ā
RV upa dhrajantamadrayo vidhannit
RV sa yo vṛṣā narāṃ na rodasyoḥ śravobhirasti jīvapītasargaḥ
RV pra yaḥ sasrāṇaḥ śiśrīta yonau
RV ā yaḥ puraṃ nārmiṇīmadīdedatyaḥ kavirnabhanyo nārva
RV sūro na rurukvāñchatātmā
RV abhi dvijanmā trī rocanāni viśva rajāṃsi śuśucano asthāt
RV hotā yajiṣṭho apāṃ sadhasthe
RV ayaṃ sa hota yo dvijanmā viśvā dadhe vāryāṇi śravasyā
RV marto yo asmai sutuko dadāśa
RV puru tva dāśvān voce 'riragne tava svidā
RV todasyeva śaraṇa ā mahasya
RV vyaninasya dhaninaḥ prahoṣe cidararuṣaḥ
RV kadā cana prajigato adevayoḥ
RV sa candro vipra martyo maho vrādhantamo divi
RV prapret te agne vanuṣaḥ syāma
RV mitraṃ na yaṃ śimyā goṣu gavyavaḥ svādhyo vidathe apsujījanan
RV arejetāṃ rodasī pājasā girā prati priyaṃ yajataṃ januṣamavaḥ
RV yad dha tyad vāṃ purumīḷhasya sominaḥ pra mitrāso na dadhire svābhuvaḥ
RV adha kratuṃ vidataṃ gatumarcata uta śrutaṃ vṛṣaṇā pastyāvataḥ
RV ā vāṃ bhūṣan kṣitayo janma rodasyoḥ pravācyaṃ vṛṣaṇā dakṣase mahe
RV yadīm ṛtāya bharatho yadarvate pra hotrayā śimya vītho adhvaram
RV pra sā kṣitirasura yā mahi priya ṛtāvānāv ṛtamā ghoṣatho bṛhat
RV yuvaṃ divo bṛhato dakṣamabhuvaṃ gāṃ na dhuryupa yuñjāthe apaḥ
RV mahī atra mahinā vāram ṛṇvatho 'reṇavastuja ā sadman dhenavaḥ
RV svaranti tā uparatāti sūryamā nimruca uṣasastakvavīriva
RV ā vam ṛtāya keśinīranuṣata mitra yatra varuṇa gātumarcathaḥ
RV ava tmana sṛjataṃ pinvataṃ dhiyo yuvaṃ viprasya manmanamirajyathaḥ
RV yo vāṃ yajñaiḥ śaśamāno ha dāśati kavirhotā yajati manmasādhanaḥ
RV upāha taṃ gachatho vītho adhvaramachā giraḥ sumatiṃ gantamasmayu
RV yuvāṃ yajñaiḥ prathamā gobhirañjata ṛtāvanā manaso naprayuktiṣu
RV bharanti vāṃ manmanā saṃyatā giro 'dṛpyatā manasa revadaśāthe
RV revad vayo dadhāthe revadāśathe narā mayābhiritauti mahinam
RV na vaṃ dyāvo 'habhirnota sindhavo na devatvaṃ paṇayo nānaśurmagham
RV yuvaṃ vastraṇi puvasā vasāthe yuvorachidrā mantavo ha sargāḥ
RV avātiratamanṛtāni viśva ṛtena mitrāvaruṇā sacethe
RV etaccana tvo vi ciketadeṣāṃ satyo mantraḥ kaviśasta ṛghāvān
RV triraśriṃ hanti caturaśrirugro devanido ha prathamāajūryan
RV apādeti prathamā padvatīnāṃ kastad vāṃ mitrāvaruṇā ciketa
RV garbho bhāraṃ bharatyā cidasya ṛtaṃ pipartyanṛtaṃ ni tārīt
RV prayantamit pari jāraṃ kanīnāṃ paśyāmasi nopanipadyamānam
RV anavapṛgṇā vitatā vasānaṃ priyaṃ mitrasya varuṇasya dhāma
RV anaśvo jāto anabhīśurarvā kanikradat patayadūrdhvasānuḥ
RV acittaṃ brahma jujuṣuryuvānaḥ pra mitre dhāma varuṇegṛṇantaḥ
RV ā dhenavo māmateyamavantīrbrahmapriyaṃ pīpayan sasminnūdhan
RV pitvo bhikṣeta vayunāni vidvānāsāvivāsannaditimuruṣyet
RV ā vāṃ mitrāvaruṇā havyajuṣṭiṃ namasā devāvavasā vavṛtyām
RV asmākaṃ brahma pṛtanāsu sahyā asmākaṃ vṛṣṭirdivyāsupārā
RV yajāmahe vāṃ mahaḥ sajoṣā havyebhirmitrāvaruṇā namobhiḥ
RV ghṛtairghṛtasnū adha yad vāmasme adhvaryavo na dhītibhirbharanti
RV prastutirvāṃ dhāma na prayuktirayāmi mitrāvaruṇā suvṛktiḥ
RV anakti yad vāṃ vidatheṣu hotā sumnaṃ vāṃ sūrirvṛṣaṇāviyakṣan
RV pīpāya dhenuraditirṛtāya janāya mitrāvaruṇā havirde
RV hinoti yad vāṃ vidathe saparyan sa rātahavyo mānuṣo na hotā
RV uta vāṃ vikṣu madyāsvandho gāva āpaśca pīpayanta devīḥ
RV uto no asya pūrvyaḥ patirdan vītaṃ pātaṃ payasa usriyāyāḥ
RV viṣṇornu kaṃ vīryāṇi pra vocaṃ yaḥ pārthivāni vimamerajāṃsi
RV yo askabhāyaduttaraṃ sadhasthaṃ vicakramāṇastredhorugāyaḥ
RV pra tad viṣṇu stavate vīryeṇa mṛgo na bhīmaḥ kucaro giriṣṭhāḥ
RV yasyoruṣu triṣu vikramaṇeṣvadhikṣiyanti bhuvanāni viśvā
RV pra viṣṇave śūṣametu manma girikṣita urugāyāya vṛṣṇe
RV ya idaṃ dīrghaṃ prayataṃ sadhasthameko vimame tribhirit padebhiḥ
RV yasya trī pūrṇā madhunā padānyakṣīyamāṇā svadhayāmadanti
RV ya u tridhātu pṛtivīmuta dyāmeko dādhāra bhuvanāni viśvā
RV tadasya priyamabhi pātho aśyāṃ naro yatra devayavo madanti
RV urukramasya sa hi bandhuritthā viṣṇoḥ pade parame madhva utsaḥ
RV tā vaṃ vāstūnyuśmasi gamadhyai yatra gāvo bhūriśṛṅgāayāsaḥ
RV atrāha tadurugāyasya vṛṣṇaḥ paramaṃ padamava bhāti bhūri
RV pra vaḥ pāntamandhaso dhiyāyate mahe śūrāya viṣṇave cārcata
RV yā sānuni parvatānāmadābhyā mahastasthaturarvateva sādhunā
RV tveṣamitthā samaraṇaṃ śimīvatorindrāviṣṇū sutapā vāmuruṣyati
RV yā martyāya pratidhīyamānamit kṛśānorasturasanāmuruṣyathaḥ
RV tā īṃ vardhanti mahyasya pauṃsyaṃ ni mātarā nayati retase bhuje
RV dadhāti putro 'varaṃ paraṃ piturnāma tṛtīyamadhi rocane divaḥ
RV tattadidasya pauṃsyaṃ gṛṇīmasīnasya traturavṛkasya mīḷhuṣaḥ
RV yaḥ pārthivāni tribhirid vigāmabhiruru kramiṣṭorugāyāya jīvase
RV dve idasya kramaṇe svardṛśo 'bhikhyāya martyo bhuraṇyati
RV tṛtīyamasya nakirā dadharṣati vayaścana patayantaḥ patatriṇaḥ
RV caturbhiḥ sākaṃ navatiṃ ca nāmabhiścakraṃ na vṛttaṃ vyatīnravīvipat
RV bṛhaccharīro vimimāna ṛkvabhiryuvākumāraḥ pratyetyāhavam
RV bhavā mitro na śevyo ghṛtāsutirvibhūtadyumna evayā u saprathāḥ
RV adhā te viṣṇo viduṣā cidardhya stomo yajñaścarādhyo haviṣmatā
RV yaḥ pūrvyāya vedhase navīyase sumajjānaye viṣṇave dadāśati
RV yo jātamasya mahato mahi bravat sedu śravobhiryujyaṃ cidabhyasat
RV tamu stotāraḥ pūrvyaṃ yathā vida ṛtasya garbhaṃ januṣāpipartana
RV āsya jānanto nāma cid vivaktana mahaste viṣṇo sumatiṃ bhajāmahe
RV tamasya rājā varuṇastamaśvinā kratuṃ sacanta mārutasya vedhasaḥ
RV dādhāra dakṣamuttamamaharvidaṃ vrajaṃ ca viṣṇuḥ sakhivānaporṇute
RV ā yo vivāya sacathāya daivya indrāya viṣṇuḥ sukṛte sukṛttaraḥ
RV vedhā ajinvat triṣadhastha āryam ṛtasya bhāge yajamānamābhajat
RV abodhyagnirjma udeti sūryo vyuṣāścandrā mahyāvo arciṣā
RV āyukṣātāmaśvinā yātave rathaṃ prāsāvīd devaḥ savitā jagat pṛthak
RV yad yuñjāthe vṛṣaṇamaśvinā rathaṃ ghṛtena no madhunā kṣatramukṣatam
RV asmākaṃ brahma pṛtanāsu jinvataṃ vayaṃ dhanā śūrasātā bhajemahi
RV arvāṃ tricakro madhuvāhano ratho jīrāśvo aśvinoryātu suṣṭutaḥ
RV trivandhuro maghavā viśvasaubhagaḥ śaṃ na ā vakṣad dvipade catuṣpade
RV ā na ūrjaṃ vahatamaśvinā yuvaṃ madhumatyā naḥ kaśayā mimikṣatam
RV prāyustāriṣṭaṃ nī rapāṃsi mṛkṣataṃ sedhataṃ dveṣo bhavataṃ sacābhuvā
RV yuvaṃ ha garbhaṃ jagatīṣu dhattho yuvaṃ viśveṣu bhuvaneṣvantaḥ
RV yuvamagniṃ ca vṛṣaṇāvapaśca vanaspatīnraśvināvairayethām
RV yuvaṃ ha stho bhiṣajā bheṣajebhiratho ha stho rathyā rāthyebhiḥ
RV atho ha kṣatramadhi dhattha ugrā yo vāṃ haviṣmānmanasā dadāśa
RV vasū rudrā purumantū vṛdhantā daśasyataṃ no vṛṣaṇāvabhiṣṭau
RV dasrā ha yad rekṇa aucathyo vāṃ pra yat sasrātheakavābhirūtī
RV ko vāṃ dāśat sumataye cidasyai vasū yad dhethe namasā pade goḥ
RV jigṛtamasme revatīḥ purandhīḥ kāmapreṇeva manasā carantā
RV yukto ha yad vāṃ taugryāya perurvi madhye arṇaso dhāyi pajraḥ
RV upa vāmavaḥ śaraṇaṃ gameyaṃ śūro nājma patayadbhirevaiḥ
RV upastutiraucathyamuruṣyen mā māmime patatriṇī vi dugdhām
RV mā māmedho daśatayaścito dhāk pra yad vāṃ baddhastmani khādati kṣām
RV na mā garan nadyo mātṛtamā dāsā yadīṃ susamubdhamavādhuḥ
RV śiro yadasya traitano vitakṣat svayaṃ dāsa uro aṃsāvapi gdha
RV dīrghatamā māmateyo jujurvān daśame yuge
RV apāmarthaṃ yatīnāṃ brahmā bhavati sārathiḥ
RV pra dyāvā yajñaiḥ pṛthivī ṛtāvṛdhā mahī stuṣe vidatheṣu pracetasā
RV devebhirye devaputre sudaṃsasetthā dhiyā vāryāṇi prabhūṣataḥ
RV uta manye pituradruho mano māturmahi svatavastad dhavīmabhiḥ
RV suretasā pitarā bhūma cakratururu prajāyā amṛtaṃvarīmabhiḥ
RV te sūnavaḥ svapasaḥ sudaṃsaso mahī jajñurmātarā pūrvacittaye
RV sthātuśca satyaṃ jagataśca dharmaṇi putrasya pāthaḥ padamadvayāvinaḥ
RV te māyino mamire supracetaso jāmī sayonī mithunā samokasā
RV navyaṃnavyaṃ tantumā tanvate divi samudre antaḥ kavayaḥ sudītayaḥ
RV tad rādho adya saviturvareṇyaṃ vayaṃ devasya prasave manāmahe
RV asmabhyaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī sucetunā rayiṃ dhattaṃ vasumantaṃ śatagvinam
RV te hi dyāvāpṛthivī viśvaśambhuva ṛtāvarī rajaso dhārayatkavī
RV sujanmanī dhiṣaṇe antarīyate devo devī dharmaṇā sūryaḥ śuciḥ
RV uruvyacasā mahinī asaścatā pitā mātā ca bhuvanāni rakṣataḥ
RV sudhṛṣṭame vapuṣye na rodasī pitā yat sīmabhi rūpairavāsayat
RV sa vahniḥ putraḥ pitroḥ pavitravān punāti dhīro bhuvanāni māyayā
RV dhenuṃ ca pṛśniṃ vṛṣabhaṃ suretasaṃ viśvāhā śukraṃ payo asya dukṣata
RV ayaṃ devānāmapasāmapastamo yo jajāna rodasī viśvaśambhuvā
RV vi yo mame rajasī sukratūyayājarebhi skambhanebhiḥsamānṛce
RV te no gṛṇāne mahinī mahi śravaḥ kṣatraṃ dyāvāpṛthivī dhāsatho bṛhat
RV yenābhi kṛṣṭīstatanāma viśvahā panāyyamojo asme saminvatam
RV kimu śreṣṭhaḥ kiṃ yaviṣṭho na ājagan kimīyate dūtyaṃ kad yadūcima
RV na nindima camasaṃ yo mahākulo 'gne bhrātardruṇa id bhūtimūdima
RV ekaṃ camasaṃ caturaḥ kṛṇotana tad vo devā abruvan tad va āgamam
RV saudhanvanā yadyevā kariṣyatha sākaṃ devairyajñiyāso bhaviṣyatha
RV agniṃ dūtaṃ prati yadabravītanāśvaḥ kartvo ratha uteha kartvaḥ
RV dhenuḥ kartvā yuvaśā kartvā dvā tāni bhrātaranu vaḥ kṛtvyemasi
RV cakṛvāṃsa ṛbhavastadapṛchata kvedabhūd yaḥ sya dūto na ājagan
RV yadāvākhyaccamasāñcaturaḥ kṛtānādit tvaṣṭā gnāsvantarnyānaje
RV hanāmaināniti tvaṣṭā yadabravīccamasaṃ ye devapānamanindiṣuḥ
RV anyā nāmāni kṛṇvate sute sacānanyairenānkanyā nāmabhi sparat
RV indro harī yuyuje aśvinā rathaṃ bṛhaspatirviśvarūpāmupājata
RV ṛbhurvibhvā vājo devānagachata svapaso yajñiyambhāgamaitana
RV niścarmaṇo gāmariṇīta dhītibhiryā jarantā yuvaśā tākṛṇotana
RV saudhanvanā aśvādaśvamatakṣata yuktvā rathamupa devānayātana
RV idamudakaṃ pibatetyabravītanedaṃ vā ghā pibatā muñjanejanam
RV saudhanvanā yadi tan neva haryatha tṛtīye gha savane mādayādhvai
RV āpo bhūyiṣṭhā ityeko abravīdagnirbhūyiṣṭha ityanyo abravīt
RV vadharyantīṃ bahubhyaḥ praiko abravīd ṛtā vadantaścamasānapiṃśata
RV śroṇāmeka udakaṃ gāmavajati māṃsamekaḥ piṃśati sūnayābhṛtam
RV ā nimrucaḥ śakṛdeko apabharat kiṃ svit putrebhyaḥ pitarā upāvatuḥ
RV udvatsvasmā akṛṇotana tṛṇaṃ nivatsvapaḥ svapasyaya naraḥ
RV agohyasya yadasastanā gṛhe tadadyedam ṛbhavo nānu gachatha
RV sammīlya yad bhuvanā paryasarpata kva svit tātyā pitara vaasatuḥ
RV aśapata yaḥ karasnaṃ va adade yaḥ prābravīt protasma abravītana
RV suṣupvāṃsa ṛbhavastadapṛchatāgohya ka idaṃ no abūbudhat
RV śvānaṃ basto bodhayitāramabravīt samvatsara idamadyā vyakhyata
RV divā yanti maruto bhūmyāgnirayaṃ vāto antarikṣeṇa yati
RV adbhiryati varuṇaḥ samudrairyuṣmānichantaḥ śavaso napātaḥ
RV mā no mitro varuṇo aryamāyurindra ṛbhukṣā marutaḥ parikhyan
RV yad vājino devajatasya sapteḥ pravakṣyāmo vidathe vīryāṇi
RV yan nirṇijā rekṇasā prāvṛtasya ratiṃ gṛbhītāṃ mukhato nayanti
RV supranajo memyad viśvarūpa indrāpūṣṇoḥ priyamapyeti pāthaḥ
RV eṣa chāgaḥ puro aśvena vājinā pūṣṇo bhāgo nīyate viśvadevyaḥ
RV abhipriyaṃ yat puroḷāśamarvatā tvaṣṭedenaṃ sauśravasāya jinvati
RV yad dhaviṣyam ṛtuśo devayānaṃ trirmānuṣāḥ paryaśvaṃ nayanti
RV atrā pūṣṇaḥ prathamo bhāga eti yajñaṃ devebhyaḥ prativedayannajaḥ
RV hotādhvaryurāvayā agnimindho grāvagrābha uta śaṃstā suvipraḥ
RV tena yajñena svaraṃkṛtena sviṣṭena vakṣaṇā āpṛṇadhvam
RV yūpavraskā uta ye yūpavāhāścaṣālaṃ ye aśvayūpāya takṣati
RV ye cārvate pacanaṃ sambharantyuto teṣāmabhigūrtirna invatu
RV upa prāgāt suman me 'dhāyi manma devānāmāśā upa vītapṛṣṭhaḥ
RV anvenaṃ viprā ṛṣayo madanti devānāṃ puṣṭe cakṛmā subandhum
RV yad vājino dāma sundānamarvato yā śīrṣaṇyā raśanārajjurasya
RV yad vā ghāsya prabhṛtamāsye tṛṇaṃ sarvā tā te api deveṣvastu
RV yadaśvasya kraviṣo makṣikāśa yad vā svarau svadhitau riptamasti
RV yad dhastayoḥ śamituryan nakheṣu sarvā tā te api deveṣvastu
RV yadūvadhyamudarasyāpavāti ya āmasya kraviṣo gandho asti
RV sukṛtā tacchamitāraḥ kṛṇvantūta medhaṃ śṛtapākaṃ pacantu
RV yat te gātrādagninā pacyamānādabhi śūlaṃ nihatasyāvadhāvati
RV mā tad bhūmyāmā śriṣan mā tṛṇeṣu devebhyastaduśadbhyo rātamastu
RV ye vājinaṃ paripaśyanti pakvaṃ ya īmāhuḥ surabhirnirhareti
RV ye cārvato māṃsabhikṣāmupāsata uto teṣāmabhigūrtirna invatu
RV yan nīkṣaṇaṃ māṃspacanyā ukhāyā yā pātrāṇi yūṣṇaāsecanāni
RV ūṣmaṇyāpidhānā carūṇāmaṅkāḥ sūnāḥpari bhūṣantyaśvam
RV nikramaṇaṃ niṣadanaṃ vivartanaṃ yacca paḍbīśamarvataḥ
RV yacca papau yacca ghāsiṃ jaghāsa sarvā tā te api deveṣvastu
RV mā tvāgnirdhvanayīd dhūmagandhirmokhā bhrājantyabhi vikta jaghriḥ
RV iṣṭaṃ vītamabhigūrtaṃ vaṣaṭkṛtaṃ taṃ devāsaḥ prati gṛbhṇantyaśvam
RV yadaśvāya vāsa upastṛṇantyadhīvāsaṃ yā hiraṇyānyasmai
RV sandānamarvantaṃ paḍbīśaṃ priyā deveṣvā yāmayanti
RV yat te sāde mahasā śūkṛtasya pārṣṇyā vā kaśayā vā tutoda
RV sruceva tā haviṣo adhvareṣu sarvā tā te brahmaṇāsūdayāmi
RV catustriṃśad vājino devabandhorvaṅkrīraśvasya svadhitiḥsameti
RV achidrā gātrā vayunā kṛṇota paruṣparuranughuṣya vi śasta
RV ekastvaṣturaśvasyā viśastā dvā yantārā bhavatastathaṛtuḥ
RV yā te gātrāṇām ṛtuthā kṛṇomi tātā piṇḍanāṃ pra juhomyagnau
RV mā tvā tapat priya ātmāpiyantaṃ mā svadhitistanva ā tiṣṭhipat te
RV mā te gṛdhnuraviśastātihāya chidrā gātraṇyasinā mithū kaḥ
RV na vā u etan mriyase na riṣyasi devānideṣi pathibhiḥ sugebhiḥ
RV harī te yuñjā pṛṣatī abhūtāmupāsthād vājī dhuri rāsabhasya
RV sugavyaṃ no vājī svaśvyaṃ puṃsaḥ putrānuta viśvāpuṣaṃ rayim
RV anāgāstvaṃ no aditiḥ kṛṇotu kṣatraṃ no aśvo vanatāṃ haviṣmān
RV yadakrandaḥ prathamaṃ jāyamāna udyan samudrāduta vā purīṣāt
RV śyenasya pakṣā hariṇasya bāhū upastutyaṃ mahi jātaṃ te arvan
RV yamena dattaṃ trita enamāyunagindra eṇaṃ prathamo adhyatiṣṭhat
RV gandharvo asya raśanāmagṛbhṇāt sūrādaśvaṃ vasavo nirataṣṭa
RV asi yamo asyādityo arvannasi trito guhyena vratena
RV asi somena samayā vipṛkta āhuste trīṇi divi bandhanāni
RV trīṇi ta āhurdivi bandhanāni trīṇyapsu trīṇyantaḥ samudre
RV uteva me varuṇaścantsyarvan yatrā ta āhuḥ paramaṃ janitram
RV imā te vājinnavamārjanānīmā śaphānāṃ saniturnidhānā
RV atrā te bhadrā raśanā apaśyam ṛtasya yā abhirakṣantigopāḥ
RV ātmānaṃ te manasārādajānāmavo divā patayantaṃ pataṃgam
RV śiro apaśyaṃ pathibhiḥ sugebhirareṇubhirjehamānaṃ patatri
RV atrā te rūpamuttamamapaśyaṃ jigīṣamāṇamiṣa ā padegoḥ
RV yadā te marto anu bhogamānaḷ ādid grasiṣṭha oṣadhīrajīgaḥ
RV anu tvā ratho anu maryo arvannanu gāvo 'nu bhagaḥ kanīnām
RV anu vrātāsastava sakhyamīyuranu devā mamire vīryaṃ te
RV hiraṇyaśṛṅgo 'yo asya pādā manojavā avara indra āsīt
RV devā idasya haviradyamāyan yo arvantaṃ prathamo adhyatiṣṭhat
RV īrmāntāsaḥ silikamadhyamāsaḥ saṃ śūraṇāso divyāso atyāḥ
RV haṃsā iva śreṇiśo yatante yadākṣiṣurdivyamajmamaśvāḥ
RV tava śarīraṃ patayiṣṇvarvan tava cittaṃ vāta iva dhrajīmān
RV tava śṛṅgāṇi viṣṭhitā purutrāraṇyeṣu jarbhurāṇā caranti
RV upa prāgācchasanaṃ vājyarvā devadrīcā manasā dīdhyānaḥ
RV ajaḥ puro nīyate nābhirasyānu paścāt kavayo yantirebhāḥ
RV upa prāgāt paramaṃ yat sadhasthamarvānachā pitaraṃ mātaraṃ ca
RV adyā devāñ juṣṭatamo hi gamyā athā śāste dāśuṣe vāryāṇi
RV asya vāmasya palitasya hotustasya bhrātā madhyamo astyaśnaḥ
RV tṛtīyo bhrātā ghṛtapṛṣṭho asyātrāpaśyaṃ viśpatiṃ saptaputram
RV sapta yuñjanti rathamekacakrameko aśvo vahati saptanāmā
RV trinābhi cakramajaramanarvaṃ yatremā viśvā bhuvanādhitasthuḥ
RV imaṃ rathamadhi ye sapta tasthuḥ saptacakraṃ sapta vahantyaśvāḥ
RV sapta svasāro abhi saṃ navante yatra gavāṃ nihitā sapta nāma
RV ko dadarśa prathamaṃ jāyamānamasthanvantaṃ yadanasthā bibharti
RV bhūmyā asurasṛgātmā kva svit ko vidvāṃsamupa gāt praṣṭumetat
RV pākaḥ pṛchāmi manasāvijānan devānāmenā nihitā padāni
RV vatse baṣkaye 'dhi sapta tantūn vi tatnire kavaya otavāu
RV acikitvāñcikituṣaścidatra kavīn pṛchāmi vidmane na vidvān
RV vi yastastambha ṣaḷ imā rajāṃsyajasya rūpe kimapi svidekam
RV iha bravītu ya īmaṅga vedāsya vāmasya nihitaṃ padaṃ veḥ
RV śīrṣṇaḥ kṣīraṃ duhrate gāvo asya vavriṃ vasānā udakaṃ padāpuḥ
RV mātā pitaram ṛta ā babhāja dhītyagre manasā saṃ hi jagme
RV sā bībhatsurgarbharasā nividdhā namasvanta idupavākamīyuḥ
RV yuktā mātāsīd dhuri dakṣiṇāyā atiṣṭhad garbho vṛjanīṣvantaḥ
RV amīmed vatso anu gāmapaśyad viśvarūpyaṃ triṣu yojaneṣu
RV tisro mātṝstrīn pitṝn bibhradeka ūrdhvastasthau nemava glāpayanti
RV mantrayante divo amuṣya pṛṣṭhe viśvavidaṃ vācamaviśvaminvām
RV dvādaśāraṃ nahi tajjarāya varvarti cakraṃ pari dyām ṛtasya
RV ā putrā agne mithunāso atra sapta śatāni viṃśatiśca tasthuḥ
RV pañcapādaṃ pitaraṃ dvādaśākṛtiṃ diva āhuḥ pare ardhe purīṣiṇam
RV atheme anya upare vicakṣaṇaṃ saptacakre ṣaḷara āhurarpitam
RV pañcāre cakre parivartamāne tasminnā tasthurbhuvanāni viśvā
RV tasya nākṣastapyate bhūribhāraḥ sanādeva na śīryate sanābhiḥ
RV sanemi cakramajaraṃ vi vāvṛta uttānāyāṃ daśa yuktā vahanti
RV sūryasya cakṣū rajasaityāvṛtaṃ tasminnārpitā bhuvanāni viśvā
RV sākaṃjānāṃ saptathamahurekajaṃ ṣaḷ id yamā ṛṣayo devajā iti
RV teṣāmiṣṭāni vihitāni dhāmaśa sthātre rejante vikṛtāni rūpaśaḥ
RV striyaḥ satīstānu me puṃsa āhuḥ paśyadakṣaṇvān navi cetadandhaḥ
RV kaviryaḥ putraḥ sa īmā ciketa yastā vijānāt sa pituṣ pitāsat
RV avaḥ pareṇa para enāvareṇa padā vatsaṃ bibhratī gaurudasthāt
RV sā kadrīcī kaṃ svidardhaṃ parāgāt kva svit sūte nahi yūthe antaḥ
RV avaḥ pareṇa pitaraṃ yo asyānuveda para enāvareṇa
RV kavīyamānaḥ ka iha pra vocad devaṃ manaḥ kuto adhi prājātam
RV ye arvāñcastānu parāca āhurye parāñcastānu arvāca āhuḥ
RV indraśca yā cakrathuḥ soma tāni dhurā na yuktā rajaso vahanti
RV dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyā samānaṃ vṛkṣaṃ pari ṣasvajāte
RV tayoranyaḥ pippalaṃ svādvattyanaśnannanyo abhi cākaśīti
RV yatrā suparṇā amṛtasya bhāgamanimeṣaṃ vidathābhisvaranti
RV ino viśvasya bhuvanasya gopāḥ sa mā dhīraḥ pākamatrā viveśa
RV yasmin vṛkṣe madhvadaḥ suparṇā niviśante suvate cādhi viśve
RV tasyedāhuḥ pippalaṃ svādvagre tan non naśad yaḥpitaraṃ na veda
RV yad gāyatre adhi gāyatramāhitaṃ traiṣṭubhād vā traiṣṭubhaṃ niratakṣata
RV yad vā jagajjagatyāhitaṃ padaṃ ya it tad viduste amṛtatvamānaśuḥ
RV gāyatreṇa prati mimīte arkamarkeṇa sāma traiṣṭubhena vākam
RV vākena vākaṃ dvipadā catuṣpadākṣareṇa mimate sapta vāṇīḥ
RV jagatā sindhuṃ divyasthabhāyad rathantare sūryaṃ paryapaśyat
RV gāyatrasya samidhastisra āhustato mahnā pra ririce mahitvā
RV upa hvaye sudughāṃ dhenumetāṃ suhasto godhuguta dohadenām
RV śreṣṭhaṃ savaṃ savitā sāviṣan no 'bhīddho gharmastadu ṣu pra vocam
RV hiṅkṛṇvatī vasupatnī vasūnāṃ vatsamichantī manasābhyāgāt
RV duhāmaśvibhyāṃ payo aghnyeyaṃ sa vardhatāṃ mahate saubhagāya
RV gauramīmedanu vatsaṃ miṣantaṃ mūrdhānaṃ hiṃṃ akṛṇon mātavā u
RV sṛkvāṇaṃ gharmamabhi vāvaśānā mimāti māyuṃ payate payobhiḥ
RV ayaṃ sa śiṅkte yena gaurabhīvṛtā mimāti māyuṃ dhvasanāvadhi śritā
RV sā cittibhirni hi cakāra martyaṃ vidyud bhavantī prati vavrimauhata
RV anacchaye turagātu jīvamejad dhruvaṃ madhya ā pastyānām
RV jīvo mṛtasya carati svadhābhiramartyo martyenā sayoniḥ
RV apaśyaṃ gopāmanipadyamānamā ca parā ca pathibhiścarantam
RV sa sadhrīcīḥ sa viśūcīrvasāna ā varīvarti bhuvaneṣvantaḥ
RV ya īṃ cakāra na so asya veda ya īṃ dadarśa hirugin nutasmāt
RV sa māturyonā parivīto antarbahuprajā nirṛtimā viveśa
RV dyaurme pitā janitā nābhiratra bandhurme mātā pṛthivīmahīyam
RV uttānayoścamvoryonirantaratrā pitā duhiturgarbhamādhāt
RV pṛchāmi tvā paramantaṃ pṛthivyāḥ pṛchāmi yatra bhuvanasyanābhiḥ
RV pṛchāmi tvā vṛṣṇo aśvasya retaḥ pṛchāmi vācaḥ paramaṃ vyoma
RV iyaṃ vediḥ paro antaḥ pṛthivyā ayaṃ yajño bhuvanasya nābhiḥ
RV ayaṃ somo vṛṣṇo aśvasya reto brahmāyaṃ vācaḥparamaṃ vyoma
RV saptārdhagarbhā bhuvanasya reto viṣṇostiṣṭhanti pradiśāvidharmaṇi
RV te dhītibhirmanasā te vipaścitaḥ paribhuvaḥ pari bhavanti viśvataḥ
RV an vi jānāmi yadivedamasmi niṇyaḥ saṃnaddho manasā carāmi
RV yadā māgan prathamajā ṛtasyādid vaco aśnuve bhāgamasyāḥ
RV apāṃ prāṃ eti svadhayā gṛbhīto 'martyo martyenā sayoniḥ
RV tā śaśvantā viṣūcīnā viyantā nyanyaṃ cikyurna nicikyuranyam
RV ṛco akṣare parame vyoman yasmin devā adhi viśve niṣeduḥ
RV yastan na veda kim ṛcā kariṣyati ya it tad vidusta ime samāsate
RV sūyavasād bhagavatī hi bhūyā atho vayaṃ bhagavantaḥ syāma
RV addhi tṛṇamaghnye viśvadānīṃ piba śuddhamudakamācarantī
RV gaurīrmimāya salilāni takṣatyekapadī dvipadī sā catuṣpadī
RV aṣṭāpadī navapadī babhūvuṣī sahasrākṣarā parame vyoman
RV tasyāḥ samudrā adhi vi kṣaranti tena jīvanti pradiśaścatasraḥ
RV tataḥ kṣaratyakṣaraṃ tad viśvamupa jīvati
RV śakamayaṃ dhūmamārādapaśyaṃ viṣūvatā para enāvareṇa
RV ukṣāṇaṃ pṛśnimapacanta vīrāstāni dharmāṇi prathamānyāsan
RV trayaḥ keśina ṛtuthā vi cakṣate saṃvatsare vapata eka eṣām
RV viśvameko abhi caṣṭe śacībhirdhrājirekasya dadṛśena rūpam
RV catvāri vāk parimitā padāni tāni vidurbrāhmaṇā ye manīṣiṇaḥ
RV guhā trīṇi nihitā neṅgayanti turīyaṃ vāco manuṣyā vadanti
RV indraṃ mitraṃ varuṇamagnimāhuratho divyaḥ sa suparṇo garutmān
RV ekaṃ sad viprā bahudhā vadantyagniṃ yamaṃ mātariśvānamāhuḥ
RV kṛṣṇaṃ niyānaṃ harayaḥ suparṇā apo vasānā divamut patanti
RV ta āvavṛtran sadanād ṛtasyādid ghṛtena pṛthivī vyudyate
RV dvādaśa pradhayaścakramekaṃ trīṇi nabhyāni ka u tacciketa
RV tasmin sākaṃ triśatā na śaṅkavo 'rpitāḥ ṣaṣṭirna calācalāsaḥ
RV yaste stanaḥ śaśayo yo mayobhūryena viśvā puṣyasi vāryāṇi
RV yo ratnadhā vasuvid yaḥ sudatraḥ sarasvati tamiha dhātave kaḥ
RV yajñena yajñamayajanta devāstani dharmāṇi prathamānyāsan
RV te ha nākaṃ mahimānaḥ sacanta yatra pūrve sādhyāḥ santi devāḥ
RV samānametadudakamuccaityava cāhabhiḥ
RV bhūmiṃ parjanyā jinvanti divaṃ jinvantyagnayaḥ
RV divyaṃ suparṇaṃ vāyasaṃ bṛhantamapāṃ garbhaṃ darśatamoṣadhīnām
RV abhīpato vṛṣṭibhistarpayantaṃ sarasvantamavase johavīmi
RV kayā śubhā savayasaḥ sanīḷāḥ samānyā marutaḥ saṃ mimikṣuḥ
RV kayā matī kuta etāsa ete 'rcanti śuṣmaṃ vṛṣaṇo vasūyā
RV kasya brahmāṇi jujuṣuryuvānaḥ ko adhvare maruta ā vavarta
RV śyenāniva dhrajato antarikṣe kena mahā manasā rīramāma
RV kutastvamindra māhinaḥ sanneko yāsi satpate kiṃ ta itthā
RV saṃ pṛchase samarāṇaḥ śubhānairvocestan no harivo yatte asme
RV brahmāṇi me matayaḥ śaṃ sutāsaḥ śuṣma iyarti prabhṛto me adriḥ
RV ā śāsate prati haryantyukthemā harī vahatastā no acha
RV ato vayamantamebhiryujānāḥ svakṣatrebhistanvaḥ śumbhamānāḥ
RV mahobhiretānupa yujmahe nvindra svadhāmanu hi no babhūtha
RV kva syā vo marutaḥ svadhāsīd yan māmekaṃ samadhattāhihatye
RV ahaṃ hyūgrastaviṣastuviṣmān viśvasya śatroranamaṃ vadhasnaiḥ
RV bhūri cakartha yujyebhirasme samānebhirvṛṣabha pauṃsyebhiḥ
RV bhūrīṇi hi kṛṇavāmā śaviṣṭhendra kratvā maruto yadvaśāma
RV vadhīṃ vṛtraṃ maruta indriyeṇa svena bhāmena taviṣo babhūvān
RV ahametā manave viśvaścandrāḥ sugā apaścakara vajrabāhuḥ
RV anuttamā te maghavan nakirnu na tvāvānasti devatā vidānaḥ
RV na jāyamāno naśate na jāto yāni kariṣyā kṛṇuhipravṛddha
RV ekasya cin me vibhvastvojo yā nu dadhṛṣvān kṛṇavai manīṣā
RV ahaṃ hyūgro maruto vidāno yāni cyavamindra idīśa eṣām
RV amandan mā maruta stomo atra yan me naraḥ śrutyaṃ brahma cakra
RV indrāya vṛṣṇe sumakhāya mahyaṃ sakhye sakhāyastanvetanūbhiḥ
RV evedete prati mā rocamānā anedyaḥ śrava eṣo dadhānāḥ
RV saṃcakṣyā marutaścandravarṇā achānta me chadayāthā canūnam
RV ko nvatra maruto māmahe vaḥ pra yātana sakhīnrachā sakhāyaḥ
RV manmāni citrā apivātayanta eṣāṃ bhūta navedā ma ṛtānām
RV ā yad duvasyād duvase na kārurasmāñcakre mānyasya medhā
RV o ṣu vartta maruto vipramachemā brahmāṇi jaritā voarcat
RV eṣa va stomo maruta iyaṃ gīrmāndāryasya mānyasya karoḥ
RV eṣā yāsīṣṭa tanve vayāṃ vidyāmeṣaṃ vṛjanaṃ jīradānum

RV tad vaḥ sujātā maruto mahitvanaṃ dīrghaṃ vo dātramaditeriva vratam

RV sahasraṃ ta indrotayo naḥ sahasramiṣo harivo gūrtatamāḥ
RV sahasraṃ rāyo mādayadhyai sahasriṇa upa no yantu vājāḥ

RV joṣad yadīmasuryā sacadhyai viṣitastukā rodasī nṛmaṇāḥ

RV bhadrā vo rātiḥ pṛṇato na dakṣiṇā pṛthujrayī asuryeva jañjatī

RV eṣa va stomo 
RV mahaścit tvamindra yata etān mahaścidasi tyajaso varūtā
RV sa no vedho marutāṃ cikitvān sumnā vanuṣva tava hi preṣṭhā
RV ayujran ta indra viśvakṛṣṭīrvidānāso niṣṣidho martyatrā
RV marutāṃ pṛtsutirhāsamānā svarmīḷhasya pradhanasya sātau

RV tvaṃ tū na indra taṃ rayiṃ dā ojiṣṭhayā dakṣiṇayeva rātim
RV stutaśca yāste cakananta vāyo stanaṃ na madhvaḥpīpayanta vājaiḥ
RV tve rāya indra tośatamāḥ praṇetāraḥ kasya cid ṛtāyoḥ
RV te ṣu ṇo maruto mṛḷayantu ye smā purā gātūyantīva devāḥ
